CHAPTER ONE OVERVIEW OF ICBC	第一章 工商银行概况	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section One History of Reform and Achievement	第一节 改革历程与成就	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. History of Reform	一、改革历程	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Period as a state-owned specialized bank (1984-1993)	（一）国家专业银行时期（1984年～1993年）	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Industrial and Commercial Bank of China (“ICBC”) was formally established on January 1, 1984, mainly responsible for the industrial and commercial credits and savings business previously undertaken by the People’s Bank of China (“PBOC”) in the early period.	1984年1月1日，中国工商银行正式成立。 初期主要负责原来由中国人民银行办理的工商信贷和储蓄业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In the subsequent one decade, ICBC was actively involved in the economic system reform, vigorously supported the national economic development and fully served as a major channel of financing.	在之后的十年里，工商银行积极参与经济体制改革，大力支持国民经济发展，充分发挥了融资主渠道的作用。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, ICBC continued to improve its service network, rapidly expanded its business scope, developed a nationwide business network system with a focus on serving urban industrial and commercial enterprises and urban citizens, and established a superior position in Chinese financial industry in basic business areas.	同时，工商银行的服务网络不断健全，业务范围迅速扩展，形成了覆盖全国、重点服务城市工商企业和城市居民的经营网络体系，并在基础业务领域确立了国内金融业的优势地位。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Period as a state-owned commercial bank (1994-2004)	（二）国有商业银行时期（1994年～2004年）	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To adapt to the needs of socialist market economic system and allow the financial industry to better support the sustained, rapid and healthy development of national economy, China introduced a reform to the financial system under the traditional planned economic pattern, requiring state-owned specialized banks to transform to state-owned commercial ones as soon as possible and operate based on the modern commercial bank operating mechanism of independent operation, self risk-taking, assumption of sole responsibility for profit or loss and self-restraint.	为适应建立社会主义市场经济体制的需要，更好地发挥金融业支持国民经济持续快速健康发展的作用，国家对传统计划经济模式下的金融体制进行改革，要求国有专业银行尽快转型为国有商业银行，按自主经营、自担风险、自负盈亏、自我约束的现代商业银行经营机制运行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In line with the market economic requirements and the principles for operation of commercial banks, ICBC actively carried out a series of reforms. It established the unified legal person system, accelerated the innovation in various business management mechanisms such as authorization, credit extension, performance assessment and cost control mainly proceeding from resolving asset quality and operational efficiency issues, strengthened risk management and internal control, promoted the adjustment of business structure and the change in development models and enhanced the quality and effectiveness of development, laying a foundation and creating conditions for the joint-stock reform and modern financial enterprise construction.	工商银行按照市场经济要求和商业银行经营原则，积极实施了一系列改革，建立了统一法人体制，并着重从解决资产质量和经营效益问题入手，加快了授权、授信、绩效考核、成本控制等各项经营管理机制的创新，强化了风险管理和内部控制，推进了经营结构的调整和发展方式的转变，提升了发展的质量和效益，为股份制改革和现代金融企业建设奠定了基础、创造了条件。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Period as a joint-stock commercial bank (from 2005)	（三）股份制商业银行时期（2005年至今）	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Entering into the 21st Century, Chinese banking industry has witnessed a big change in its business environment.	进入21世纪以来，中国银行业的经营环境出现了较大变化。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To improve the competitiveness and development level, state-owned commercial banks embarked on the joint-stock reform, realizing the fundamental shift of the business system and mechanism through the restructuring of equity structure and laying a more solid foundation for the sustained and healthy development through the improved internal governance structure and the optimized business management.	为增强竞争能力和发展水平，国有商业银行陆续启动了股份制改造，通过产权结构的重组，实现经营体制机制的根本性转变，通过内部治理结构的完善和经营管理的优化，为持续健康发展奠定更为坚实的基础。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
On April 18, 2005, ICBC formally started the joint-stock reform and generally went through the following stages:	2005 年4 月18 日，工商银行正式启动股份制改革，大体可以分为以下几个阶段：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Financial restructuring	1．财务重组	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Restructuring the capital structure.	（1）重组资本结构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
On April 22, 2005, Central Huijin Investment Ltd. (“Huijin”) made a capital contribution of USD15 billion (or RMB124 billion) to ICBC from its foreign exchange reserve.	2005 年4 月22 日，中央汇金公司运用外汇储备向工商银行注入150亿美元（折合人民币1240 亿元）资本金。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC restructured the capital by retaining an amount the same as that of Huijin and changing the other to risk provisioning. The Ministry of Finance (“MOF”) and Huijin held a 50% stake in ICBC each.	工商银行对现有资本金进行重组，保留与汇金公司等额资本金，其余转为风险拨备，财政部和汇金公司分别持有工行50%的股份。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After the capital restructuring, the core capital of ICBC reached RMB248 billion and its core capital adequacy ratio exceeded 6%.	资本结构重组后，工商银行的核心资本金达到2480亿元，核心资本充足率达到6%以上。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
On August 19, 2005, ICBC successfully issued the first subordinated bonds of RMB35 billion, in which the excess subscription ratio was 2.44x.	同年8 月19 日，工商银行成功发行首期350亿元的次级债券，超额认购率达到2.44倍。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The issue of subordinated bonds helped ICBC further renew the supplementary capital and be well prepared for strategic capital introduction and public offering.	通过次级债券的发行，工商银行进一步补充了附属资本，为战略引资和公开上市做好了准备。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Disposing non-performing assets.	（2）处置不良资产。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC disposed non-performing assets in the way as follows: the assets classified under the loss category were purchased by MOF. MOF and ICBC set up a jointly managed account with its funding source from the share dividends of central finance and the income taxes paid by ICBC; with regard to the doubtful assets, PBOC adopted the market-oriented methods such as bidding to choose asset management companies for disposal.	工商银行处置不良资产的具体方式如下：损失类资产由财政部购买，财政部与工商银行共同建立“特别共管基金账户”，其资金来源为中央财政的股份分红及工商银行上交的所得税；可疑类资产由人民银行采取招标等市场化方式，选择资产管理公司予以处置。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Through the financial restructuring, ICBC obviously lifted its capital adequacy ratio and provisioning coverage ratio and largely reduced its non-performing loan ratio (See Figure 1-1). The long-term issues about capital and non-performing assets bottlenecking the development of ICBC were properly solved, creating conditions for the further deepened joint-stock reform.	通过财务重组，工商银行的资本充足率和拨备覆盖率得到显著提升，不良贷款率大幅下降（见图1-1），长期困扰工商银行发展的资本金和不良资产的问题得到妥善解决，为股份制改造的进一步深化创造了条件。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Figure 1-1 Indicator Comparisons before and after the Financial Restructuring of ICBC	图1-1 工商银行财务重组前后指标对比	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Improvement of the governance structure and establishment of a joint-stock limited company	2．完善治理结构，组建股份有限公司	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Pursuant to the requirements of the Company Law and other laws and regulations, ICBC sets up the Shareholders’ General Meeting, the Board of Directors, the Board of Supervisors and the Senior Management on the principles of “separate establishment of the Shareholders’ General Meeting, the Board of Directors and the Board of Supervisors, separation of the three powers, effective restrictions and coordinated development”. It has built a normative organizational structure and corporate governance mechanism for a joint-stock commercial bank, guaranteed the independent operation and effective check and balance of each party based on the scientific and efficient decision-making, implementation and supervisory mechanism, and established a joint-stock limited company upon the approval of relevant national management authorities.	根据《公司法》等法律法规的要求，工商银行按照“三会分设、三权分立、有效制约、协调发展”的原则设立了股东大会、董事会、监事会、高级管理层，着手建立了规范的股份制商业银行组织机构和公司治理机制，以科学、高效的决策、执行和监督机制，确保各方独立运作、有效制衡，并在国家相关管理机构的批准之下设立股份有限公司。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With the MOF and Huijin as the promoters, the Industrial and Commercial Bank of China Limited was established on October 25, 2005. All of the businesses, assets and liabilities of Industrial and Commercial Bank of China were assumed by Industrial and Commercial Bank of China Limited upon the conversion.	2005年10月25日，中国财政部和中央汇金投资有限责任公司共同发起设立了中国工商银行股份有限公司，新成立的中国工商银行股份有限公司完整承继了原工商银行的资产、负债和所有业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Introduction of strategic investors	3．引进战略投资者	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After a comprehensive consideration, ICBC chose the Goldman Sachs investment group consisting of The Goldman Sachs Group, Inc., Allianz Group and American Express Company as the strategic investors.	经过综合权衡，工商银行确定由高盛集团、安联集团及美国运通公司组成的高盛投资团为战略投资者。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on the bilateral agreement, the Goldman Sachs investment group contributed USD3.78 billion to buy the newly issued shares by ICBC, and all the strategic investors undertook to launch extensive cooperation with ICBC in relevant operations and management areas.	根据双方签订的协议，高盛投资团出资37.8亿美元购买工商银行新发行的股份，各战略投资者承诺在相关业务和管理领域与工商银行广泛合作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Later, ICBC also entered into an agreement on strategic investment and cooperation with the National Council for Social Security Fund (“SSE”). SSF subscribed for newly issued shares of ICBC for an aggregate consideration of approximately RMB18.0 billion.	此后，工商银行还与全国社会保障基金理事会达成了战略投资与合作协议，后者出资180亿元人民币购买工商银行新发行股份。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As a result, ICBC has preliminarily established a diversified equity structure (Figure 1-2), laying a good foundation for conducting the deep-level strategic cooperation and improving the corporate governance mechanism subsequently.	由此，工商银行初步确立了多元化的股权结构（图1-2），为下一步开展深层次的战略合作、完善公司治理机制打下了良好基础。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Figure 1-2 Equity Structure of ICBC after the Introduction of Strategic Investors	图1-2 引入战略投资者后工商银行的股权结构	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Centennial IPO	4．世纪IPO	sample1-en-sample1-zh
On October 27, 2006, ICBC offered the A and H shares simultaneously in Hong Kong and Shanghai.	2006年10月27日，工商银行在香港和上海成功实现A＋H同步IPO。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This IPO raised a total of USD22 billion funds, creating the then highest financing record.	此次IPO共募集资金220亿美元，创下了当时的最高融资规模记录。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC thus completed the transformation from a solely state-invested commercial bank to a state-owned public holding company. This IPO marked that ICBC began to accept the domestic and overseas capital market tests and shareholders’ selections, and it walked toward a well-performed financial enterprise with normative corporate governance structure and “transparent operation”. II.	完成由国有独资商业银行向国有控股公众公司的蜕变，标志着工商银行开始接受国内外资本市场检验和股东选择，向具有规范的公司治理架构并实施“透明经营”的绩优金融企业迈进。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Historical Achievement	二、历史成就	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Through almost 30 years’ reform and development, especially through the joint-stock reform and public offering, ICBC has transformed to a modern financial enterprise with complete governance, established a diversified and globalized modern financial services system, grown to be a listed bank boasting good quality and efficiency and robust sustainable development capability and walked onto the track of building an internationally first-class financial enterprise.	经过近30年的改革发展，特别是经过股份制改革和公开上市，工商银行转变为一家治理完善的现代金融企业，构建起多元化、全球化的现代金融服务体系，成长为质量效益良好、可持续发展能力强劲的上市银行，踏上了建设国际一流现代金融企业的征程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Comprehensive establishment of the modern financial enterprise system	（一）全面确立现代金融企业制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Through the exploration and practice of several generations of ICBC personnel, ICBC has completed the historic transformation from a state-owned specialized bank to a state-owned commercial bank and then to an international publicly-holding company.	经过几代工行人的探索实践，工商银行完成了从国有专业银行到国有商业银行，再到国际公众持股公司的历史性跨越。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Via the joint-stock reform, ICBC has established a modern corporate governance framework consisting of the Shareholders’ General Meeting, the Board of Directors, the Board of Supervisors and the Senior Management, and formed a corporate operation mechanism of scientific decision-making, potent execution and effective supervision.	通过股份制改革，工商银行搭建起了由股东大会、董事会、监事会、高管层组成的现代公司治理结构，形成了决策科学、执行有力、监督有效的公司运行机制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, it, in line with the requirements and regulatory standards of modern financial enterprise system, has built a relatively complete capital management system, assets & liabilities management system, fund operation system, as well as prudent, normative and transparent finance & accounting system; constructed a relatively independent internal audit and control system, as well as an enterprise risk management system with coverage of credit, market, liquidity and operational risks; continued to improve the organizational system of modern commercial bank by establishing the market-oriented and new-typed human resource management system and compensation distribution system.	同时，按照现代金融企业制度的要求和监管标准，建立了较为完善的资本管理制度、资产负债管理体系、资金营运体系以及审慎、规范、透明的财务会计制度；构建起相对独立的内部审计与控制体系以及能够覆盖信用风险、市场风险、流动性风险和操作风险的全面风险管理体系；不断完善现代商业银行的组织机构体系，构建了市场化的新型人力资源管理体制和薪酬分配制度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The establishment and improvement of modern financial enterprise system have guaranteed the bank-wide scientific management, sound operation and scientific development.	现代金融企业制度的建立和完善，保证了全行科学管理、稳健经营和科学发展。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Rapid development of all kinds of businesses	（二）各项业务快速发展	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The enlarging customer circle, increasingly diversified business structure, constantly enhanced innovative capability and continuously improved internal management enable ICBC have realized the sustained, rapid and healthy development of all kinds of businesses. It continues to be a market leader not only in terms of such basic business areas as deposits and loans, but also establishes the leading edges in a majority of emerging business areas.	不断扩大的客户基础、日益多元的业务结构、持续增强的创新能力以及不断完善的内部管理，让工商银行实现了各项业务的持续快速健康发展，不仅在存贷款等基础业务领域继续保持市场领导地位，而且在绝大多数新兴业务领域确立了领先优势。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Total assets increased by 57-folds from RMB272.8 billion upon founding in 1984 to RMB15.5 trillion in 2011; various deposits added by 73-folds from RMB169.6 billion to RMB12.3 trillion; various loans grew by 31-folds from RMB247 billion to RMB7.6 trillion; credit cards, first issued in 1989, exceeded 70 million in number by the end of 2011, thus the bank has become the top credit card issuer in China; through one decade’s development, asset custody service had over RMB3 trillion assets under custody, thus the bank has become China’s first asset custodian; e-banking was initially introduced in 1998, and its trading volume represented 70.1% of total business volume by 2011, making the bank become the largest electronic bank.	总资产从1984年成立时的2728亿元，发展到2011年的15.5万亿元，增长了57倍；各项存款从1696亿元增长到12.3万亿元，增长了73倍；各项贷款从2470亿元增长到7.6万亿元，增长了31倍；信用卡从1989年开始发行，到2011年末已经突破了7000万张，成为中国第一信用卡发卡行；资产托管业务经过十年的发展，托管规模已经突破3万亿元，是中国第一资产托管银行；电子银行业务自1998年开办以来，2011年电子银行交易量占总业务量的比例达到70.1%，是中国最大的电子银行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Such emerging businesses as wealth management, enterprise annuity, investment banking and cash management introduced in recent years develop fast, and the Bank has developed to be a market leader in emerging businesses gradually.	近年来推出的理财、企业年金、投资银行、现金管理等新兴业务发展迅速，逐渐成为新兴业务的市场领导者。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Its business scope has expanded from traditional basic businesses including deposits, loans and remittance to many business areas including money market, capital market and insurance market. Therefore, ICBC has grown to be a banking institution with the strongest financial service supply capability in China.	业务范围从成立初期的存贷汇等传统基础业务，发展到覆盖货币市场、资本市场、保险市场等多业务领域，成长为中国金融服务供给能力最强的银行机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Walked on the track of internationalization and integration	（三）迈出国际化、综合化步伐	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In early 1990s, ICBC has started the exploration of internationalization and integration, and gained manifest achievement through the innovation development of more than one decade.	20世纪90年代初，工商银行开始了国际化、综合化的探索实践，经过十多年的创新发展，取得了显著的成就。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It set up the first overseas institution in 1992 and had 239 overseas institutions by 2011, basically establishing the globalized service network covering major international financial hubs in the world and major trade partners of China.	从1992年设立第一家海外机构，到2011年已经拥有境外机构网点239家，基本形成覆盖世界主要国际金融中心和我国主要经贸往来地区的全球化服务网络。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, by establishing non-banking financial subsidiaries at home and abroad, ICBC successively founded ICBCCS, ICBC Leasing, ICBC International and ICBC-AXA Assurance, successfully entering the fund, leasing, investment banking and insurance business areas and gradually forming a cross-market integrated financial service system with commercial banking service as the pillar.	与此同时，通过在境内外成立非银行金融子公司的方式，先后组建设立了工银瑞信、工银租赁、工银国际、工银安盛，成功进入基金、租赁、投资银行和保险业务领域，逐步形成以商业银行业务为主体、跨市场的综合化金融服务体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iv. Improved asset quality and enhanced profitability	（四）资产质量改善、盈利能力提升	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With the continuously deepened reform and strengthened management, ICBC has fundamentally improved its asset quality, which not only ridded the non-performing loans during the transition of economic reform, but also completed the credit risk prevention mechanism at the level of system.	随着改革的持续深化和管理的不断加强，工商银行的资产质量得到根本改善，不仅彻底解决了经济体制转轨过程中形成的不良贷款包袱，而且从制度上完善了信用风险防范机制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
By the end of 2011, the balance and ratio of non-performing loans of ICBC had been reduced for 12 straight years, with the latter down to 0.94%.	截至2011年末，工商银行不良贷款余额和不良贷款率连续12年实现“双下降”，不良贷款率降至0.94%。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The rapid development of various businesses and ever improved business management level has greatly lifted the profitability of ICBC.	各项业务的快速发展，经营管理水平的不断提升，极大提高了工商银行的盈利能力。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Under IFRS, since 2006, ICBC has reported an annual average compounded growth rate of 32.9% in after-tax profit and made an after-tax profit of RMB208.45 billion in 2011, thus being the most profitable bank globally for three consecutive years.	按国际会计准则计算，自2006年以来，工商银行税后利润年均复合增长率达到32.9%，2011年实现税后利润2084.5亿元，连续三年成为全球最盈利银行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Robust profit growth ability has resulted in the rapid increase in corporate value and shareholders’ return.	强劲的盈利增长能力使公司价值和股东回报呈现快速增长。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has been among the international leading banks in terms of ROE and ROA.	权益回报率和总资产回报率已经达到国际先进银行的水平。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It has greatly enhanced the profit-making sustainability. The percentage of non-interest income has increased from less than 1% upon founding to 23.7% in 2011, where, that of net fee and commission income in net operating income has reached 21.4%.	盈利的可持续性大大增强，非利息收入占比从成立初期的不到1%增长到2011年的23.7%，其中净手续费和佣金收入占营业净收入的比重达到了21.4%。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
v. Constantly improved financial service level	（五）金融服务水平不断完善	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Upholding the concept of “being customer-centric and creating value through service”, ICBC has achieved innovative development in all aspects such as business, product, channel and process.	秉承“以客户为中心、服务创造价值”的理念，工商银行从业务、产品、渠道、流程等各方面不断创新发展。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
By the end of 2011, it set up 16,900 operating institutions at home and abroad, owned a developed e-banking service network consisting of 13,772 self-service banking centers, 59,140 ATMs, as well as internet banking, telephone banking and mobile banking, and provided quality financial services for 282 million personal customers and 4.11 million corporate customers worldwide.	截至2011年末，在国内外共设有1.69万个经营机构，拥有由13772家自助银行中心、59140台自动柜员机以及网上银行、电话银行、手机银行等组成的发达的电子银行服务网络，为全球2.82亿个人客户和411万户公司客户提供优质的金融服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In recent years, ICBC has systematically made improvement in distribution channels, business processes, IT systems, management systems and service patterns, in order to enhance the customer experience and service quality. Section Two	近年来，工商银行还从分销渠道、业务流程、IT系统、管理体制和服务模式等方面系统加以改进，改善客户体验，提升服务品质。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate Governance Framework	第二节 公司治理架构	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Summary of ICBC’s Corporate Governance	一、工商银行公司治理概述	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Since the joint-stock reform, ICBC has made constant efforts to improve the corporate governance framework comprising the Shareholders’ General Meeting, the Board of Directors, the Board of Supervisors and the Senior Management, and optimized responsibilities of the authority organ, decision-making organ, supervisory organ and executive organ. As a result, the operation mechanism featuring clearly defined responsibilities and accountability, coordination and effective checks and balances has been in place.	股改以来，工商银行不断完善由股东大会、董事会、监事会、高级管理层组成的公司治理架构，优化权力机构、决策机构、监督机构和执行机构之间职责，形成了权责分明、各司其职、相互协调、有效制衡的运作机制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Figure 1-3 Corporate Governance Framework Chart of ICBC	图1-3 工商银行公司治理架构图	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Basic Corporate Governance Framework	二、公司治理基本架构	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As the authority organ of ICBC, the Shareholders’ General Meeting involves all shareholders.	股东大会是工商银行的权力机构，由全体股东组成。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Shareholders’ General Meeting is responsible for, among others, deciding on business policies and material investment plans of ICBC; considering and approving the proposals on the annual financial budget, final accounts, profit distribution plans and loss recovery plans, electing and replacing directors, shareholder supervisors and external supervisors; considering and approving the work report of the Board of Directors and the work report of the Board of Supervisors; adopting resolutions on merger, division, dissolution, liquidation, change of corporate form, increase or decrease of registered capital, issuance and listing of corporate bonds or other negotiable securities and repurchase of stocks; and amending the Articles of Association of the Bank.	股东大会负责决定公司经营方针和重大投资计划，审议批准公司的年度财务预算、决算方案、利润分配方案和弥补亏损方案，选举和更换董事以及由股东代表出任的监事和外部监事，审议批准董事会工作报告和监事会工作报告，对公司合并、分立、解散、清算、变更公司形式、增加或者减少注册资本、公司债券或其他有价证券的发行及上市的方案、回购公司股票做出决议，修订公司章程等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As the decision-making organ of ICBC, the Board of Directors of ICBC is accountable to, and shall report to, the Shareholders’ General Meeting.	董事会是工商银行的决策机构，向股东大会负责并报告工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Board of Directors is responsible for, among others, convening the Shareholders’ General Meeting; implementing resolutions of the Shareholders’ General Meeting; deciding on business plans, investment plans and development strategies of ICBC; formulating annual financial budgets and final accounts of ICBC; formulating profit distribution plans and loss recovery plans; formulating proposals on the increase or decrease of registered capital of ICBC; formulating fundamental management rules on risk management and internal control, and supervising the implementation of these rules, appointing or removing the President, and based on the President’s nomination, appointing or removing Senior Executive Vice Presidents and other Senior Management members (except the Board Secretary), and deciding on their remuneration, rewards and sanctions; deciding on authorizing the President to set up relevant internal institutions of ICBC, managing information disclosure of ICBC; and supervising and overseeing the Senior Management.	董事会负责召集股东大会；执行股东大会决议；决定公司的经营计划、投资方案和发展战略；制订公司年度财务预算方案、决算方案；制订公司的利润分配方案和弥补亏损方案；制订公司增加或者减少注册资本的方案；制定公司风险管理、内部控制等基本管理制度，并监督制度的执行情况；聘请或解聘行长，并根据行长提名聘任或解聘副行长及其他高级管理人员（董事会秘书除外），并决定其报酬和奖惩事项；决定或授权行长决定行内相关机构的设置；管理本行信息披露；对高级管理层实施监督等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Board of Directors has established six special committees, namely, the Strategy Committee, the Audit Committee, the Risk Management Committee, the Nomination Committee, the Compensation Committee and the Related Party Transactions Control Committee.	董事会下设六个专门委员会：战略委员会、审计委员会、风险管理委员会、提名委员会、薪酬委员会、关联交易控制委员会。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As the supervisory organ of ICBC, the Board of Supervisors is accountable to, and shall report to, the Shareholders’ General Meeting.	监事会是工商银行的监督机构，向股东大会负责并报告工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Board of Supervisors is responsible for, among others, supervising the performance and due diligence of Directors and Senior Management members; supervising the performance of duties of the Board of Directors and the Senior Management; conducting audits on retiring or resigning Directors and Senior Management members when necessary; examining and supervising ICBC’s financial activities; examining financial information such as financial report, business report and profit distribution plan to be submitted to the Shareholders’ General Meeting by the Board of Directors; examining and supervising business decisions, risk management and internal control of ICBC, and providing guidance to the internal audit departments of ICBC, formulating performance assessment measures for supervisors, assessing the performance and conduct of supervisors, and reporting to the Shareholders’ General Meeting for approval; presenting proposals to the Shareholders’ General Meeting; proposing to convene extraordinary general meetings, and convening and presiding over such meetings in case the Board of Directors fails to perform its duty of convening shareholders’ general meeting; proposing to convene interim meetings of the Board of Directors, etc.	监事会负责对董事和高级管理人员的履职行为和尽职情况进行监督；监督董事会、高级管理层履行职责的情况；根据需要对董事和高级管理人员进行离任审计；检查、监督公司的财务活动；审核董事会拟提交股东大会的财务报告、营业报告和利润分配方案等财务资料；对公司的经营决策、风险管理和内部控制等进行检查监督并指导公司内部审计部门工作；拟定监事的履职评价办法，对监事进行履职评价，并报股东大会决定；向股东大会提出议案；提议召开临时股东大会，在董事会不履行召集股东会议的职责时，召集并主持临时股东大会；提议召开董事会临时会议等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Board of Supervisors has the Supervision Committee.	监事会下设监督委员会。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As the executive organ of ICBC, the Senior Management is accountable to the Board of Directors.	高级管理层是工商银行的执行机构，对董事会负责。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Senior Management is responsible for, among others, carrying out operational management of ICBC; organizing the implementation of business plan and investment plan approved by the Board of Directors; formulating detailed regulations and rules for operational management; formulating proposals on remuneration distribution and performance assessment for heads of internal departments and branches of ICBC; reporting operating results to the Board of Directors and the Board of Supervisors; preparing the annual financial budget, final accounts, profit distribution plans and loss recovery plans, and proposals on the increase or decrease of registered capital, issuance or listing of bonds, and making recommendations to the Board of Directors.	高级管理层负责公司的营运管理，组织实施经董事会批准的经营计划和投资方案，制定公司经营管理的具体规章制度，制订公司内设部门和分支机构负责人薪酬分配方案和绩效考核方案，向董事会、监事会报告经营业绩，拟订公司的年度财务预算、决算方案，利润分配方案和弥补亏损方案，增加或者减少注册资本、发行债券或者其他债券上市方案，并向董事会提出建议等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Sound corporate governance is the key to stable operation of the banking sector and even the entire financial system, and is also one of the most important determinants of a bank’s development.	良好的公司治理是银行业乃至整个金融体系稳健运行的关键所在，也是决定一家银行能走多快、走多远的根本因素。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC pursues the improvement of corporate governance as a basic project of enhancing core competitiveness, continues to improve the corporate governance mechanism of “clear boundaries of responsibilities, orderly checks and balances and coordination, democratic and scientific decisions, efficient and normative operation and timely and transparent disclosure”, and makes efforts toward the vision of “becoming a global leading bank with the best profitability, performance and prestige”. SectIon Three	工商银行坚持把完善公司治理作为增强核心竞争力的基础工程，不断完善“职责边界清晰、制衡协作有序、决策民主科学、运行高效规范、信息及时透明”的公司治理机制；为实现“最盈利、最优秀、最受尊重的国际一流现代金融企业”的愿景而努力。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Status Quo of Internationalization	第三节 国际化发展现状	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Starting from independent application for establishment and emerging markets, ICBC has gradually set up a mechanism of global product line and domestic and overseas interactive development, created a global integrated business system platform, continued to enhance the global service capability, established a sustainable development pattern step by step and entered into a new stage in terms of internationalized development.	从自主申设起步，从新兴市场出发，工商银行逐步建立了全球产品线和内外联动发展机制，创立了全球一体化的业务系统平台，全球服务能力不断提升，可持续发展模式逐步确立，国际化发展迈入新阶段。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Global Service Network	一、全球服务网络	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The construction of ICBC’s overseas service network has gone through three stages.	工商银行境外服务网络建设先后经历了三个阶段。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Prior to 2000, it expanded the overseas network mainly by means of independent application for establishment.	2000年以前，主要依赖自主申设方式拓展海外网络。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Marked by the establishment of Singapore Representative Office in 1992, ICBC formally started the internationalization course following the “going global” of enterprises, and successively set up operating institutions or representative offices in important cities including Almaty, Seoul, Hong Kong, Tokyo, London, New York, Frankfurt, Luxemburg and Sydney.	以1992年设立新加坡代表处为标志，工商银行正式启动了跟随企业“走出去”的国际化进程，相继在阿拉木图、汉城（首尔）、香港、东京、伦敦、纽约、法兰克福、卢森堡、悉尼等重要城市设立了营业机构或代表处。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
From 2000 to 2006, it witnessed fast expansion of overseas institutions, especially Hong Kong-based institutions, through gradual launch of M&As on the basis of independent application for establishment.	2000年至2006年，在申设基础上逐步开展并购，工商银行实现了境外机构尤其是在港机构快速发展。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC acquired Union Bank of Hong Kong in 2000 as a pioneer among Chinese banks for acquisition and restructuring of foreign listed banks, and ICBC (Asia) purchased Fortis Bank in 2003, which became the first successful case for a Chinese bank to buy a European bank.	其中2000年收购友联银行开创了中资银行兼并重组境外上市银行的先河，2003年工银亚洲收购华比富通银行成为中资背景银行收购欧资银行的首个成功案例。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Since the public offering in 2006, leveraging on the strengthened overall operating strength and enhanced international ranking and competitiveness, and in combination with own competitive development strategy, ICBC has accelerated the construction of global service network through application for establishment and M&A. By the end of December 2011, a global network with universal licensing, efficient operation and excellent service, consisting of 239 overseas institutions in 33 countries and territories, had been established.	2006年上市以来，依托总体经营实力的增强、国际排名与竞争力的提高，结合自身的竞争发展战略，工商银行通过申设和并购并举，加快全球服务网络建设。 截至2011年12月末，已建成覆盖33个国家和地区、由239家境外机构组成的牌照完备、运营高效、服务优良的全球网络。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, as an important supplementation to the overseas business network, the network of correspondent banks has covered 1,553 banks in 136 countries and territories, and the global business network spanning Asia, Africa, Europe, America and Australia has been preliminarily established.	同时，作为海外经营网络的重要补充，代理行网络已实现覆盖136个国家和地区的1553家银行，初步建成了跨越亚、非、欧、美、澳五大洲的全球经营网络。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
While focusing upon the layout in important target markets globally, ICBC also takes the geographical strength, scope of license and business resources into comprehensive consideration, attaches importance to the integration and extension of existing institutions and builds some competent overseas institutions to overseas business centers of the whole bank via expanding the business functions.	工商银行在着力推进全球重点目标市场布局的同时，还综合考虑各境外机构的地缘优势、牌照范围、业务资源，注重现有机构的整合和延伸，通过扩充业务功能，把一些具备条件的境外机构打造成全行的海外业务中心。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In recent years, it has successively established Frankfurt Euro Clearing Center, Tokyo JPY Clearing Center, New York USD Clearing Center, London GBP Clearing Center, Sydney AUD Clearing Center and Hong Kong HKD Clearing Center; set up the overseas investment banking platform and asset management platform mainly depending upon ICBC International; made efforts to establish overseas wealth management centers, private banking centers, bankcard service centers, global cash management centers, precious metal business centers and cross-border RMB business centers leveraging on the institutions in Hong Kong and Macau; brought the preferential location conditions of those institutions in Hong Kong, New York and London in international financial centers into full play in an effort to promote the construction of overseas treasury operation centers and foreign fund-raising centers.	近年来，先后建成了法兰克福欧元清算中心、东京日元清算中心、纽约美元清算中心、伦敦英镑清算中心、悉尼澳元清算中心、香港港币清算中心；并以工银国际为主体搭建了境外投资银行平台和资产管理平台；依托港澳机构着力打造境外财富管理中心、私人银行中心、银行卡业务中心、全球现金管理中心、贵金属业务中心和跨境人民币业务中心； 充分发挥香港、纽约、伦敦机构地处国际金融中心的有利条件，着力推进海外资金交易中心和境外筹资中心建设。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The rapid scale-up and improved efficiency of overseas institutions have helped them to increase the value contribution to global service chain of ICBC Group.	在境外机构快速扩大自身规模、效益的同时，提升了其对工商银行集团全球服务链的价值。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Global Integrated Technological Platform	二、全球一体化科技平台	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC deems information technology to be an important component of core competitiveness. Backed by technological systems, it provides more diversified and competitive products to the customers.	工商银行将信息科技作为核心竞争力的重要组成部分，在科技系统的支持下，为客户提供更丰富、更有竞争力的产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Now, ICBC offers more than 3,000 products to the customers and is the bank boasting the biggest number of financial products and the most diversified categories in China.	目前工商银行向客户提供3000余项产品，是中国金融产品数量最多、门类最齐全的银行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
During internationalization, ICBC always advances system construction and institutional construction synchronously. As a result, the technological strength has forcefully enhanced the capability of overseas institutions for product supply, business expansion and risk control.	在国际化发展过程中，工商银行始终坚持系统建设与机构建设同步，科技优势有力提升了境外机构的产品供给、业务拓展和风险控制能力。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In 2006, ICBC started the construction of FOVA system under independent R&D, the features of which cover a lot of areas such as deposits, loans, remittance, bankcards, internet banking, international settlement, trade finance and financial market.	2006年，工商银行启动了自主研发的FOVA系统建设，功能覆盖到存款、贷款、汇款、银行卡、网上银行、国际结算、贸易融资、金融市场等多个领域。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Currently, FOVA system has been successfully rolled out in 34 overseas institutions and already covered all the overseas institutions.	目前FOVA 系统已在34家境外机构成功投产，已覆盖全部境外机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As of 2005, ICBC has actively promoted the centralized processing of documentary businesses in overseas institutions. Till now, the international settlement documentary businesses of all of the institutions at home and abroad have been centralized at the Documentary Center of the Head Office.	从2005年开始，工商银行积极推动境外机构单证业务集中处理，目前全部境内外机构的国际结算单证业务均已上挂总行单证中心。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Global Service Capability	三、全球服务能力	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Supported by the advanced FOVA platform, ICBC actively pushes forward the innovation of overseas products that serve the market needs, realized the global linking of key products lines including retail, bankcards, internet banking, clearing, specialized financing, global cash management, investment banking, asset management, trade finance and RMB, and preliminarily formed a globalized and universal service chain following the cross-border customers.	凭借先进的FOVA平台的支撑，工商银行积极推进符合市场需求的境外产品创新，在零售、银行卡、网上银行、资金清算、专业融资、全球现金管理、投资银行、资产管理、贸易金融、人民币等重点产品线上实现了全球联通，初步形成了跟随跨境客户的全球化、全能化服务链。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For example, with respect to internet banking and bankcard service, internet banking can be transacted in 22 overseas institutions, with 162,000 overseas personal online banking customers and 14,000 overseas corporate online banking customers.	例如，网上银行和银行卡业务方面，已在22家境外机构实现网银业务办理，海外网银个人客户达到16.2万户、企业客户达到1.4万户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After the establishment of ICBC Credit Card Center (International) in Hong Kong, overseas retail banking has seen a leaping-forward development leveraging on the bankcard sockets internet banking mode.	在香港设立了工银信用卡中心（国际），依托银行卡套接网银模式，境外零售业务实现跨越式发展。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In terms of investment banking service, ICBC International was established in Hong Kong to serve as the wholly-owned investment banking platform, and successfully participated into the Brazil-based Petrobras' IPO with the largest amount on the global capital market, the American International Assurance’s IPO with the third largest amount and the GE’s IPO, etc.	投资银行业务方面，在港成立了全资所有的投资银行平台——工银国际，并成功参与了融资额排名全球资本市场第一的巴西石油股本融资、融资额排名全球第三的友邦保险IPO，以及美国通用汽车IPO等项目。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With relatively strong power for investment banking, ICBC (Asia), ICBC (Macau), UK Subsidiary, ICBC (Middle East), Indonesia Subsidiary and Sydney Branch conducted a batch of locally influential projects.	工银亚洲、 工银澳门、伦敦子行、工银中东、印尼子行和悉尼分行等分行都具备了较强的投行业务实力，承接了一批在当地有影响力的项目。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Regarding global cash management service, ICBC was the first among Chinese banks to introduce global cash management service, established partnership with 2,232 customers, signed contracts for more than 6,100 accounts and expanded this service to over 40 countries and territories.	全球现金管理业务方面，在中资同业中率先推出全球现金管理业务，与2232家客户建立了合作关系，签约账户数累计超过6100个，业务拓展到40余个国家和地区。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition, ICBC has achieved remarkable results through domestic and overseas interaction and product innovation in the development of such product lines as asset management, asset custody, cross-border RMB service and trade finance.	此外，在资产管理、资产托管、跨境人民币业务、贸易金融等产品线发展方面，通过内外联动和产品创新，也取得了显著成效。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IV. Sustainable Development Pattern	四、可持续发展模式	sample1-en-sample1-zh
During internationalization, ICBC always upholds the unification of speed, scale, quality and efficiency by walking on the road of sustainable development.	在国际化过程中，工商银行始终坚持速度、规模、质量、效益的统一，走可持续发展道路。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Total assets of overseas institutions increased from USD3.6 billion in 2000 to USD132 billion in 2011 (including the investment in Standard Bank of South Africa), profit after provisioning added from USD34 million to USD1.3 billion (including the gain from Standard Bank of South Africa), the compounded growth of both assets and profit of overseas institutions reached about 39%; with steadily improved asset quality, the non-performing loan ratio decreased from 4.49% in 2001 to 0.19% in 2011.	境外机构总资产从2000年的36亿美元增至2011年的1320亿美元（含南非标准银行投资），拨备后利润从3400万美元增至13亿美元（含南非标准银行投资收益），境外机构资产和利润年复合增长率均达到39%左右；资产质量稳定改善，不良资产率从2001年的4.49%降至2011年的0.19%。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In 2011, the per capital assets and profit of overseas institutions were RMB140 million and RMB0.87 million, respectively, representing relatively high operating efficiency.	2011年，境外机构人均资产1.4亿元，人均净利润87万元，体现出较高的经营效率。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The International Regulatory Joint Meeting held in China for the first time in November 2009 chose to evaluate ICBC, where the regulatory authorities iN ten countries and territories spoke highly of ICBC for the sound business results.	2009年11月，在中国首次召开的国际监管联席会议选择工商银行作为评价对象，来自10个国家和地区的监管机构对工行的稳健经营成绩给予了较高评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
V. Construction of the Internationalized Talent Team	五、国际化人才队伍建设	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC creatively introduced the concept of “global staff management” among Chinese banks and organized the first selection and praising of honorable global staff, which improved the professional sense of belonging and quality of global staff and provided the human resource base for the development of overseas institutions.	工商银行在中资同业中开创性地提出了“全球雇员管理”理念，并组织了首届荣誉全球雇员评选表彰和各类培训活动，提升全球雇员的职业归属感和业务素质，为境外机构的发展提供人才基础。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, with keen attention to the construction of internationalized talent team, ICBC unswervingly accelerates the reserve of internationalized management personnel and professionals and strengthens the training toward the staff of overseas institutions, providing a powerful guaranty for the implementation of internationalization strategy. 	同时，工商银行一直高度重视国际化人才队伍建设，坚持加快储备国际化管理人才和国际化专业人才、加强境外机构员工培训，为国际化战略的实施提供了有力保障。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VI. Internationalized Operating Management System	六、国际化经营管理体制	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With the continuous expansion of overseas operations, ICBC has set up a specialized management department of overseas institutions under the International Banking Department, and formed the overseas operating management system of “coordination, unification and professional division of labor”.	随着海外业务的不断壮大，工商银行成立了专门的境外机构管理部门（隶属于国际业务部），形成了“协调统一、专业分工”的境外经营管理体制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The International Banking Department is mainly responsible for the internationalization strategy and planning, analysis and monitoring of dynamics upon the construction of overseas institutions, coordination and integration of in-house resources to promote the internationalized development of businesses and geographical regions and cooperation with departments-in-charge to perform professional management well; the internal departments for business management, comprehensive management as well as support & guaranty launch professional management over businesses, finance, human resources, risks, technologies, internal audits and compliance of overseas institutions according to their respective functions, and they undertake corresponding line management functions based on the responsibilities assigned to them, providing good management infrastructure for the smooth promotion of multinational operations.	国际业务部主要负责国际化战略与规划、分析监测境外机构建设动态、协调整合行内资源促进业务和区域国际化发展、配合主管部门做好专业管理；行内主要业务管理、综合管理和支持保障部门按照职能分工对境外机构的业务、财务、人事、风险、科技、内审、合规等方面进行专业管理，各部门按职责分工承担相应条线管理职能，为顺利推进跨国经营提供了良好管理基础设施。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In 2009, ICBC provided for the Consolidated Management Measures, which further defined that the management departments of consolidation elements shall manage overseas subsidiaries from the perspective of respective elements (enterprise risk, market risk, credit risk, inside trading, liquidity risk, legal risk, operational risk, reputational risk, financial management and internal audit management) accordingly, while the line management departments shall share information for supplementation. CHAPTER TWO	2009年，工商银行制定了《并表管理办法》，进一步明确各并表要素管理部门从相应并表要素维度（全面风险、市场风险、信用风险、内部交易、流动性风险、法律风险、操作风险、声誉风险、财务管理、内部审计管理）对境外附属机构进行条条管理，条块管理部门之间信息共享，互为补充。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
BASIC MANAGEMENT SYSTEMS FOR OVERSEAS INSTITUTIONS	第二章 境外机构基本管理制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section One Financial Management System	第一节 财务管理制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Financial Management Overview	一、财务管理概况	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Financial accounting	（一）财务会计	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC Group, together with its domestic branches, uses a calender year as the financial year, which is from January 1 to December 31 each year.	工商银行集团及境内机构的财务年度为自然年度，即每年1月1日至12月31日。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For financial accounting, it applies RMB as bookkeeping base currency with “Yuan” as a unit.	会计核算以人民币为记账本位币，以“元”为单位。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An overseas branch, as a bank’s localized operation in another country, should firstly meet regulatory requirements of that coutry it is located in. It may determine its financial year and bookkeeping base currency at its discretion based on surrounding economic and regulatory environment, but it is required to submit financial statements converted into RMB over accounting period set by the Head Office of ICBC, make financial accounting according to financial accouting criteria of local country, submit relevant operating statistics and financial reports to local regulatory authorities according to their requirements, and issue financial reports according to local rules.	境外机构作为银行属地化经营，首先应遵守属地国监管要求，可根据其经营所处的主要经济和监管环境自行决定其财务年度及记账本位币，但需在按照总行规定的会计期间报送折算为人民币的财务报表，要按照当地的会计核算标准进行核算，按照所在国监管要求向当地监管当局报送相关经营数据和财务报告，按照当地准则要求出具财务报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, all overseas and domestic branches of ICBC as well as its subsidiaries should also meet the parent company’s requirements, and apply the Head Office’s uniform accounting policies to report financial information for internal management and issue of the group’s consolidated reports, when they submit the financial reports to the Head Office.	同时，工商银行所有境内外分支机构及子公司在向总行报送会计报告时，还应满足母公司要求，使用总行统一的会计政策报送财务信息，用于内部管理及出具集团合并报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Management accounting	（二）管理会计	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Management of Value Accounting (MOVA) has been available inside ICBC with EVA as its core, value-creation as orientation, and value-management as philosophy, throughout the whole process of pre-event, in-process, and post-event, with five dimenstions as management targets including institution, department, product, customer and staff, covering five core operational elements including fund, expenditure, risk, taxation and capital, and incorporating management accounting philosophy, methods, technique and application into an intergrated system.	工商银行形成了以EVA为核心，以价值创造为导向、以价值管理为理念，贯穿于事前、事中、事后全过程，以机构、部门、产品、客户和员工五个维度为管理对象，涵盖资金、费用、风险、税务、资本五大核心经营要素，集管理会计理念、方法、技术及应用于一体的现代管理会计体系(MOVA, Management of Value Accounting)。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With an improvement of an integrated financial management in ICBC, MOVA system will be gradually promoted to overseas branches, forming the group’s intergrated management accounting system.	随着我行财务管理一体化的进步，MOVA体系将会逐步推广至境外机构，形成集团一体化的管理会计体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Financial management	（三）财务管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC’s financial management obeys relevant laws and regulations as well as the Articles of Association.	工商银行的财务管理遵循有关法律法规和《公司章程》的规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Branches at all levels should build and perfect internal financial management system; set functional departments of financial management; equip with professional financial management staffs; and comprehensively employ methods such as project planning, forecast, planning, budget, control, analysis, supervision, assessment and evaluation to raise funds, operate assests, allocate resources, control costs, distribute earnings, reflect operation status, prevent and mitigate financia risks.	各级机构均应建立健全内部财务管理制度，设置财务管理职能部门，配备专业财务管理人员，综合运用规划、预测、计划、预算、控制、分析、监督、考核和评价等方法，筹集资金，营运资产，配置资源，控制成本，分配收益，反映经营情况，防范和化解财务风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Financial Management System	二、财务管理体制	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Financial management system	（一）财务管理体制	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC implements financial management system with “unified management, classified authorization, responsibility for profits and losses, and assessment by levels”.	工商银行实行“统一管理、分类授权、统负盈亏、分级考核”的财务管理体制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Unified management	1.统一管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office uniformly formulates the financial management regulations and measures, allocates financial resources, discloses financial information to the public, and releases the comprehensive operating plans.	总行统一制定财务管理制度办法，统一配置财务资源，统一对外披露财务信息，统一下达综合经营计划。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Classified authorization	2.分类授权	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Superior institutions classify subordinate ones according to certain standards, and implement the authorization management depending on different financial matters.	上级机构对下级机构按照一定的标准划分类别，并区分不同的财务事项实行授权管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
All institutions at different levels carry out financial activities within authorized ranges.	各级机构在授权范围内开展财务活动。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Responsibility for profits and losses	3.统负盈亏	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office is responsible for financial performace of the whole bank. It uniformly arranges for and implements comprehensive operating plans approved by the Board of Directors, and makes unified settlement for profits and losses of the whole bank.	总行对全行财务效益负责，统一安排和执行董事会批准的综合经营计划，统一清算全行损益。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Assessment by levels	4.分级考核	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Superior institutions conduct assessment on subordinate ones’ operating status, and link the assessment results to financial resources allocation, authorization adjustment and performance incentives.	上级机构对下级机构的经营状况进行考核，并将考核结果与财务资源分配、授权调整、绩效奖励等挂钩。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Financial management objectives	（二）财务管理目标	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to the operation and development strategies of the company, ICBC’s financial management aims at building and enhancing incentive and restraint mechanism; optimizing financial resources allocation; preventing and resisting financial risks; boosting sustainable and health growth of all businesses and a stable increase in performance; and achieving value maximization for shareholders.	工商银行的财务管理目标为根据公司经营发展战略，建立健全激励约束机制，优化财务资源配置，防范和抵御财务风险，促进各项业务持续健康发展和经营效益稳步增长，实现股东价值最大化。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Principles of financial management	（三）财务管理原则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC follows the principles of “legality and compliance, prudence and steadiness, unified planning and pursuing benefits” in its financial management.	工商银行财务管理遵循“依法合规、审慎稳健、统筹兼顾、讲求效益”的管理原则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Legality and compliance	1.依法合规	sample1-en-sample1-zh
All financial management work should strictly abide by the state’s relevant financial disciplines, and conduct financial management activities compliantly according to law under the premise of continuous improvement in the financial management system.	各项财务管理工作严格遵守国家有关财经纪律，在不断完善财务管理制度的前提下，依法合规开展财务管理活动。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Prudence and steadiness	2.审慎稳健	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A complete financial risk management mechanism is established to effectively identify, monitor, measure, prevent and mitigate financial risks and ensure a sound financial foundation.	建立完备的财务风险管理机制，有效识别、监测、计量、防范和化解财务风险，确保财务基础稳健。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Unified planning	3.统筹兼顾	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overall plans on balance among costs, risks and benefits should be made, the relationship among capital restriction, business growth, risk control and return to shareholders should be controlled on a reasonable manner, and all stakeholders’ interest should be considered to enhance an overall, harmonious and sustainable growth	统筹平衡成本、风险和收益，合理把握资本约束、业务增长、风险控制和股东回报的关系，兼顾利益相关方的利益，促进全面、协调、可持续发展。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Pursuing benefits	4.讲求效益	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Institutions at all levels should focus on financial management objectives, strenghthen financial management, improve operating efficiency, and continuously boost value creativity.	各级机构要围绕财务管理目标，加强财务管理，提高经营效率，不断提升价值创造能力。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iv. Financial risk management	（四）财务风险管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Financial risk management is a key component of overall risk management for ICBC Group.	财务风险管理是工商银行集团全面风险管理重要组成部分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Financial risk, throughout the whole process of operation, is a centralized reflection of credit risk, market risk and operational risk on finance.	财务风险贯穿经营活动的各个环节，是信用风险、市场风险以及操作风险等在财务上的集中体现。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has established a financial risk control system involving recognition, measurement, monitor, and control, defining the responsibility, procedure, emergency plans and detailed steps for financial risks management. It also implements a whole-process management for pre-, middle- and post-financial risks, analyzes risks status regularly, evaluates anticipated losses, and prevents and mitigates financial risks.	工商银行建立了包括识别、计量、监测和控制等内容的财务风险控制体系，明确财务风险管理的职责、程序、应急方案和具体措施，对财务风险实施事前、事中、事后全过程管理，定期分析风险状况，评估预期损失，防范和化解财务风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
v. Financial supervision	（五）财务监督	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC’s institutions at all levels should build and perfect internal financial supervision system.	工商银行的各级机构要建立健全内部财务监督制度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Institutions including internal control supervision departments and financial management departments should supervise and examine financial activities in line with the requirements of relevant financial regulations and internal supervision regulations.	内控监督部门以及财务管理部门等机构应按照相关财务制度和内部监督制度要求对财务活动进行监督和检查。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Through financial supervision, they should appraise any institution or individual who has strictly followed financial regulations, effectively controlled financial risks, and criticize publicly institution or individual who has performed pooly in financial management, occurred with bigger financial risks, and disobeyed financial regulations, or even propose to attribute their administrative and legal responsibilities.	通过财务监督，对严格遵守财务制度、有效控制财务风险的单位或个人要提出表扬；对财务管理不力、财务风险较大、违反财务制度的机构或个人要通报批评，直至追究行政及法律责任。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on financial statements and financial analysis reports as well as financial information system platform, institutions at all levels should strengthen off-site financial inspection and monitoring on the ones under their administration, and report the irregular fluctuations of key financial monitoring indicators to the Head Office in time.	各级机构应通过财务报表和财务分析报告，以及财务信息系统平台，加强对辖内机构非现场财务检查和监控工作，对重点财务监测指标的异常波动情况，及时报告总行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Institutions at all levels are required to receive supervision, inspection or audit from the state’s external regulatory authorities as well as social intermediaries, and to cooperate actively with them. They need to make timely adjustments and corrections on problems found in both internal and external financial inspections. 	各级机构要依法接受并积极配合国家外部监管机构以及社会中介机构的监督检查或审计，对于内外部财务检查中发现的问题要及时整改。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vi.Overseas financial management system	（六）境外财务管理制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas financial management should be operated under ICBC Group system, which includes the group’s unfied system set by the Head Office, systems set by the Head Office to adapting to domestic or overseas branches, as well as systems set by institutions at all levels internally.	境外财务管理工作应在工商银行集团的制度体系下运行。 工商银行集团制度体系包括总行制定的集团统一的制度、总行制订的适应境内机构或境外机构的制度，以及各机构内部制定的制度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institutions’ financial management is consistent with the group in terms of management principles and directions.They should implement the systems with reference to the group and domestic institutions’ systems under the circumstance of non-conflicting with local regulatory requirements.	境外机构的财务管理工作在管理原则、管理方向上和集团财务管理制度保持一致，在不与当地监管要求冲突的情况下，应参照集团及境内机构的制度执行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Major financial management systems at the group-level include the Basic Regulations on Financial Accounting (G.Y.F. [2005] No.198), the Administrative Measures on Fixed Assests (Trial) (G.Y.F. [2009] No.98), the Administrative Measures on Operating Expense (Revised) (G.Y.F. [2012] No.1), and the Administrative Regulations on the State-owned Assets Assessment (G.Y.B.F. [2011] No.726).	集团层面有代表性的财务管理制度主要有：《财务会计基本制度》（工银发[2005]198号）、《固定资产管理办法（试行）》（工银发[2009]98号）、《营业费用管理办法（修订）》（工银发[2012]1号）、《国有资产评估管理规定》（工银办发[2011]726号）。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, the Head Office has released a serie of financial managent regulations and systems specific to actual status of overseas institutions in order to meet their actual management situation and serve for actual operation.	同时，总行发布了一系列针对境外机构实际情况的财务管理制度，以符合境外机构的实际管理情况，为实际运营服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Primarily, they are the Management Regulations for Expenses in Establishing Overseas Institutions (G.Y.B.F. [2011] No.202), the Administrative Measures on Overseas Institutions’ Book Capital (G.Y.B.F. [2007] No.721), and the Administrative Measures on Operating Performance Assessment of Heads of Overseas Institutions (Revised) (G.Y.F. [2011] No.72).	主要有《筹建境外机构费用管理规程》（工银办发[2011]202号）、《境外机构账面资本管理办法》（工银办发[2010]721号）、《境外机构负责人经营绩效考评办法(修订)》（工银发[2011]72号）。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition, institutions at all levels have launched their internal financial management regulations or implantation rules in order to satisfy their own financial management requirements, such as review and approval system for large-value financial affairs, regulations on finanacial expense payment, regulations on financial accounting, and regulations on financial accounting archives management.	此外，各机构为满足自身财务管理需要，出台了各机构的内部财务管理规定或实施细则，如大额财务事项的审议制度、财务费用支付规程、财务核算规定、财务会计档案管理规定等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Accounting and Financial Reports	三、会计核算及财务报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Accounting management	（一）会计核算管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC’s accounting follows the Accounting Standard for Business Enterprises - Basic Standard” issud by Ministry of Finance in February 2006, and 38 specific accounting rules, application instructions, and explanations as well as other relevant regulations.	工商银行的财务核算遵循财政部2006年2月颁布的《企业会计准则——基本准则》和38项具体会计准则、应用指南、解释以及其他相关规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Currently, the structure and contents of China’s accounting standards are getting consistent with the international ones.	目前中国会计准则的结构及内容均与国际会计准则趋同。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Accounting item management	（二）会计科目管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Finance & Accounting Department at the Head Office manages the accounting items’ setting, adjustment, numbering and accounting standards used by ICBC centrally.		sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office and domastic branches should use a unified accounting item system produced by the Head Office.	工商银行会计科目的设置、调整、编号及核算标准均由总行财务会计部集中管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The overseas institutions may set up an accounting item system on their own based on business development of themselves, and requirements of local regulatory authorities. However, when submit and send financial reports as well as relevant basic information statements to the Head Office, on the premise of maintaining consistent with ICBC’s accounting policies, they need to transmit their financial & accounting information into the Group’s accounting items or statements items.	总行、境内各分支机构必须使用总行统一制定的会计科目体系，境外机构可根据自身业务发展和当地监管要求自行设置会计科目体系，但向总行报送财务报告及相关基础信息表时，应在保持与工商银行会计政策一致的前提下，将其财务会计信息转换为集团会计科目或报表项目反映。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institutions are responsible for examining regualry whether the Head Office’s accounting item system is able to meet requirements of business growth and of producing and submitting financial reports to the Head Office. They are also in charge of doing financial report convertion and adjustment based on the Head Office’s accounting item system and accounting policies, and submitting requirements to the Head Office timely for adding, changing, discontinuing or cancelling account items based on relevant procedures.	境外机构负责定期检查总行会计科目体系能否满足其各项业务发展和向总行报表填报需要，负责根据总行会计科目体系和会计政策进行报表转换和调整，负责按照相关程序及时向总行提交新增、变更、停用或撤销会计科目的需求申请。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Financial reports	（三）财务报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Financial reports by overseas institutions	1.境外机构财务报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In general, overseas institutions have three kinds of financial reports.	境外机构财务报告一般分为三类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The first one is financial reports issued according to the requirements of regulatory authorities in the countries where they are located. The second one is financial reports together with business reports issued according to the requirements of the parent company’s regulatory authority as well as overseas institutions’ own requirements and internal management requirements of the Group. The third one is management statements of overseas institutions issued by their financial departments due to requirements of internal management during daily management, to reflect the internal operation as well as advantages and disadvantages of operating results.	一是受属地国监管当局的要求出具的财务报告；二是受母公司监管当局以及本机构及集团内部的管理要求出具的财务报告及各类业务报；三是在日常管理过程中，管理层由于内部管理的需要，也需要财务部门出具本机构的各项管理明细，体现内部运作情况及经营成果的优劣。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Group’s consolidated financial reports	2.集团合并财务报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office requires all domestic and overseas branches, and subsidiaries to make financial statements according to the accounting policies used by the Head Office when they prepare and submit accounting statements to it.	总行要求所有境内外分支机构、子公司在编制上报给总行的会计报表时，必须按照总行使用的会计政策编制报表。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For any inconsistency between accounting polices used by the overseas institutions and the Head Office, they should make necessary adjustments on financial statements of subsidiaries according to the Head Office’s accounting policies, or prepare individual accounting statements according to the parent company’s accounting policies.	境外机构所采用的会计政策与总行不一致的，应当按照总行的会计政策对子公司财务报表进行必要的调整，或者按照母公司的会计政策另行编报会计报表。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In case those subsidiaries have subordinated institutions, they need to first collect statements from subordinated institutions, and to consolidate statements to produce ones at subsidiary-level, and afterwards report to the Head Office. 	子公司存在下属机构的，应先汇总下级机构的报表，形成子公司层面的合并报表后上报总行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IV. Financial Authorization Management	四、财务授权管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Management approaches for financial authorization	（一）财务授权的管理方式	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Each year, the Head Office passes financial authorizations down to all overseas institutions through issuing authorization documents or shareholders’ advice letters.	总行每年通过下发授权文件或股东意见函的方式给各境外机构下达财务授权。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
All overseas institutions should implement financial matters controlled strictly within authorized scope.	各境外机构财务事项均应严格控制在授权范围内执行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For events beyond authorized scope, they should report to the Head Office for review and approval. They should not deal with those matters beyond authorized scope unless they have received approved documents from the Head Office. Reports after those beyond authorized scope have occurred or concealed and unreported ones are not permitted.	超授权事项应报总行审批，获得总行批文后方可进行超授权事项的处理事宜，不得事后上报或隐瞒不报。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Financial authorization to overseas institutions	（二）境外机构财务授权	sample1-en-sample1-zh
At present, authorization to ICBC overseas institutions features by the following: first, it covers all overseas and holding institutions’ financial authorizations, and implements financial authorization to the Group’s subsidiaries which have controlling abilities.	目前我行境外机构的授权特点：一是实现境外及控股机构财务授权全覆盖，对具有控制力的集团子公司均进行财务授权。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Second, based on overseas institutions’ development, structure of financial authorization indicators are optimized and adjusted regularly.	二是根据境外机构的发展状况定期优化调整财务授权指标结构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Third, a mechanism linked to performance has been introduced into financial management authorization system.	三是在财务管理授权体系中引入业绩挂钩机制，部分财务授权项目和机构的经营业绩挂钩。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Part of financial authorization items have been linked with institutions’ operating performance. Currently, overseas institutions’ authorization indicators primarily involve purchase of premises & vehicles, expenditure on purchasing other fixed assets and intangible assets (single purchase), rental on premises, single investment on decoration and rebuilding of fixed assets, loss from fixed asset disposal (single purchase), accumulated end-of-year donation expenditure, other expenditure beyond business (single purchase), first-time hiring and changing of auditor, and allocation of profits.	目前境外机构授权指标主要包括购置房屋车辆、购置其他固定资产及无形资产（单笔）支出、营业办公用房租赁、单项固定资产装修改造总投资、处置固定资产损失（单笔）、年度捐赠累计支出、其他营业外支出（单笔）、首次聘请及更换审计师、利润分配等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
V. Financial Budget Management	五、财务预算管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Contents of budget management	（一）预算管理的内容	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC’s financial budget management mainly includes three parts, that is, all branches’ budgets, operating expense budget and budgets by product and department.	工商银行财务预算管理主要有各分支机构预算、营业费用预算、分产品分部门预算三部分内容。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Branches shall set their budget targets scientifically according to the driving effects of each asset & liability business and fee-based business on operational outcome.	各分支机构均应根据各项资产负债业务和中间业务发展对经营成果的驱动关系，科学编制分机构预算目标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Budgets by product and department are decomposed to each product from branch budget. First, product budgets are produced after being consolidated at each level bottom-up; then, budgets by department are made according to corresponding relationship between departments and products. A budget management model integrated of departments & regions at different levels is finally generated.	分产品、分部门预算由机构预算分解到各产品，“自下而上”层层汇总编制成产品预算，再按照部门产品对照关系，建立分部门预算，最终形成“条块结合”的预算管理模式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
How to allocate and manage operating expenses should stick out to the efficiency-first principle, promoting a resource allocation mechanism with focus on economic added-value and orientation on value-contribution.	营业费用的分配和管理，坚持贯彻效率优先原则，推行以经济增加值为核心、以价值贡献为导向的资源配置机制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
On the basis of guaranteeing all branches’ basic operation, expense incentives should be related to value-creation in order to fully boost a positive role of resources in business growth and profit increase, and lead the whole bank to establish the philosophy of capital constraint and the business target of sustainable growth.	在满足分支机构基本运营保障的基础上，实行激励费用和价值创造相挂钩，充分发挥费用资源对业务发展和盈利增长的促进作用，引导全行树立资本约束理念和可持续增长的经营目标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Implementation process for overall budget	（二）全面预算的实施流程	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The implementation of overall budget management involves setting budget targets, decomposing and passing down budget targets and monitoring implementation of budget as well as getting feedback on implementation.	全面预算管理的实施包括预算目标的制定、预算目标的分解与下达、预算执行情况的监测与反馈等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Set budget targets	1.预算目标的制定	sample1-en-sample1-zh
First, setting budget targets should be based on long-term development strategies; second, budget targets should be set reasonably on the basis of reasonable judgments on economic and financial development conditions, and a balance between developing business and controlling risks; third, setting budget targets should reflect adequately the requirements for optimizing business structure and strengthening foundation of profit.	一是以长期发展战略规划为依据。 二是以合理判断经济金融发展形势、业务发展与风险控制的平衡为基础合理编制。 三是充分体现优化经营结构、夯实盈利基础的要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Decompose & pass down targets	2.预算目标的分解与下达	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office sets and reports indicators, principles, methods and procedures according to the Group’s plan; each branch makes forecasting on its financial budget and business plan by combining market environment with requirements for its own growth, and reports them to the Head Office in time; the Head Office determines budgets and passes them down to all branches, referring to forecasting results reported by each branch; each branch decomposes all targets of plans to the institutions in its jurisdiction to secure realizing business targets of the whole bank.	总行根据集团计划编报指标、原则、方法和流程；分支机构结合市场环境和自身发展要求，对本行各项财务预算及经营计划进行预测，及时上报总行；总行参考各机构上报的测算结果，确定预算，下达分行；各机构向辖属机构逐级分解各项计划目标，确保全行经营目标的实现。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Monitor implementation of budgets and get feedback	3.预算执行情况的监测与反馈	sample1-en-sample1-zh
At the end of budget implementation or a critical point in the middle of budget implementation (for example, end of quarter, end of half-year, end of year), branches are responsible for reporting status of budget implementation, discovering reasons for differences, putting forward solutions, and setting correction steps to ensure a successful implementation of budget in the next period; if there exists objective deviations which are difficult to be revised in budget implementation outcomes and budget targets, the latter might be adjusted if necessary.	在预算执行结束或预算期中间的关键时点（如季末、半年末、年末等），由分支机构上报预算执行情况报告，查找差异原因，提出解决对策，制定纠偏措施，确保下一阶段预算执行顺利完成；若预算执行结果与预算目标存在难以纠正的客观偏离，必要时可调整预算目标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Overseas institutions’ budget management	（三）境外机构预算管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Currently, there are three indicators used in overseas institutions’ financial budgets, including post-provisioning profit, post-provisioning profit deducting capital costs and operating expense budget.	目前境外机构财务预算指标包括提取拨备后利润、扣除资本成本后拨备后利润及营业费用预算三项。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Post-provisioning profit	1.提取拨备后利润	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This indicator is mainly used by overseas institutions for day-to day financial monitoring and deciding assessment target value for ROE (Return on Equity) at the end of year.	该指标主要用于境外机构日常财务监测和年末确定ROE（权益回报率）考核目标值。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Post-provisioning profit deducting capital costs	2.扣除资本成本后拨备后利润	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Setting this indicator aims to leading actively overseas institutions in building philosophy of capital costs, and keeping them raising levels of return on capital, primarily used in year-end performance assessment and deciding assessment target value for ROA (Return on Assets).	设定该指标的目的旨在积极引导境外机构树立资本成本理念，持续提高资本回报水平，主要用于年末经营绩效考核及确定ROA（资产回报率）考核目标值。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Of them, calculation method for cost to capital ratio should be taken according to the Notice on Strengthening Capital Valuation and Assessment in Overseas institutions (G.Y.B.F. [2011] No. 227).	其中资本金占用成本的计算方法按照《关于加大对境外机构资本金计价和考核力度的通知》（工银办发[2011]227号）的规定执行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Operating expenses	3.营业费用	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This indicator is composed of basic, earmarked and incentive expenses.	该指标由基础费用、专项费用及激励费用组成。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Of them, basic expense takes previous year’s actual expenditure as a benchmark, excluding current year’s irregular expenses and deductions with expenses exceeding budgets, and relating to growth rate of net operating income in the budget.	其中，基础费用以上年度实际费用支出为基准，剔除当年非常规性费用支出及费用超预算扣除项目，并与预算营业净收入增长率挂钩。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Earmarked expenses include the ones for purchasing, renting and decorating houses by overseas institutions.	专项费用包括境外机构购置、租赁房屋及装修事项等相关支出。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Incentive expenses, a line of flexible ones, are associated with all branches’ operating performance.	激励费用为弹性费用额度，与各机构的经营效益挂钩。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VI. Operating Performance Assessment	六、经营绩效考评	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Over recent years, ICBC has been keeping strengthening to establish an assessment system for overseas institutions, and set assessment measures for overseas institutions, namely, the Measures for Assessing Operating Performance of Leaders at Overseas Institutions, which is gradually being adjusted towards a perfect one based on overseas institutions’ development strategies and operation orientations of whole bank.	近年来，工商银行不断加强境外机构考评体系建设，制定了境外机构考评办法，即《境外机构负责人经营绩效考评办法》，并根据境外机构发展战略和全行经营导向逐年调整完善。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Target and principle of performance assessment	（一）绩效考评的目标和原则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The target of performance assessment on overseas institutions is leading them to take both current-period performance and long-term benefits into consideration through improving incentive mechanism and clarifying operation orientation, boosting adjustment of business and revenue structures, advancing strategic transformation, boosting overall management of overseas institutions and their operating performance, improving a balanced development for both domestic and overseas institutions, and pushing ICBC to implement transnational operation strategies successfully.	境外机构考评的目标是通过完善激励机制和明确经营导向，引导境外机构兼顾当期效益与长远利益，加快推进业务结构和收益结构调整，推进战略转型，提升境外行整体管理水平和经营绩效，促进境内外机构协调发展，推动我行跨国经营战略顺利实施。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Assessment of overseas institutions follows mainly four principles as seeking “operation orientation, different assessment, comprehensive and balanced, simple and efficient”. The principle of operation orientation is for a purpose of pushing ICBC to take transnational operation strategies, leading overseas institutions to increase the return on capital, to realize strategic transformation. The one of different assessment is to implement differential assessment of overseas institutions according to their specific features, take “branch-specific policy” to determine assessment plan, and provide classified guidance. The one of comprehensive and balanced is to take the balance of short-term performance and long-term development, balance of growth rate and revenue quality, balance of operating performance and risk prevention, balance of finance and non-finance into consideration when an assessment system is designed. The one of simple and eFficient is to design an assessment system with simple and clear contents, to select key performance indicators that are typical, comprehensive and highly recognizable, and to make assessment procedures clear about each responsibility and highly efficient and prompt.	境外机构考评主要遵循经营导向、差别考评、综合平衡、简便高效四个原则。 经营导向原则即考评以推动我行跨国经营战略实施为目的，引导境外机构提高资本回报，实现战略转型；差别考评原则即根据境外机构的特点实施有差别的考核评价，“一行一策”制定考评方案，进行分类指导；综合平衡原则即考评体系设计兼顾短期业绩与长期发展的平衡、发展速度与收益质量的平衡、经营效益与风险防范的平衡、财务与非财务的平衡；简便高效原则即考评体系设计力求内容简洁明确，选择具有代表性、综合性、认同度高的关键业绩指标，考核流程分工明确，高效快捷。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Main content of performance assessment	（二）绩效考评的主要内容	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Assessment approaches	1.考评方式	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Assessment approaches combine both quantitative and qualitative evaluations.	采用定量考评和定性评价相结合的考评方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Quantative assessment uses KPIs for evaluation, and a computation with weighted multiple indicators, primarily setting three indicators as operating performance, business development and risk control.	定量考核采用KPI考核，运用多指标加权方法计分，主要设置经营效益、业务发展和风险控制三方面指标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Qualitative assessment mainly targets at the results of overseas institutions in terms of strategic transformation, long-term and efficient operating system construction as well as internal and external interactions.	定性评价主要考核境外机构在战略转型、经营长效机制建设以及内外联动方面的工作业绩。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Classification of assessment on overseas institutions	2.考评机构分类	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Bases on overseas institutions’ establishing time and business growth stages, they are classified into category A (an institution at a developed stage in business) and B (an institution at a developing stage in business) for respective assessment.	依据境外机构成立的时间顺序和业务发展阶段，将境外机构分为A类（业务相对成熟机构）和B类（处于成长阶段的机构）机构分别考核。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Different weights have been set for those two categories. For category A institutions, the assessment focuses on performance indicators such as ROE; for category B institutitions, the assessment focuses on qualitative evaluation based on an appropriate lowering of requirement on return on capital because they normally have smaller business size, and greater volatile performance.	对两类机构设置差异化的考核权重，A类机构重点考核ROE等效益类指标，B类机构由于经营规模普遍较小，业绩波动较大，在适当降低资本回报要求的基础上更强调定性考核。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Assessment target value and scoring methods	3.考评目标值及计分方法	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Quantitative assessment indicators.	（1）定量考评指标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These adopt target value scoring method with setting three levels of annual assessment target value including bottom-line target T1, basic target T2 and ideal target T3 for each measurement, corresponding to a score of 30, 60 and 100, respectively.	定量考评指标采用目标值计分法，对每个指标分别设置保本目标T1、基本目标T2、理想目标T3三档年度考核目标值，对应分值分别为30分、60分、100分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
T1 target value is set based primarily on the lowest level in previous assessing period among all institutions assessed with an emphasis on the minimum task requirement for each institution.	T1目标值设定以全部被考评机构上一考核期最低水平为基本依据，强调对各机构的最低任务要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Institutions would get 30 points if they reached the T1 value; otherwise, they would get nothing.	指标达到T1值时可得30分，否则不能得分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
T2 target value sets a starting point at an actual operation status of each institution, and implements “branch-specific policy” according to its performance history and growth trend combining market environment, interest rate level and monitoring requirements.	T2目标值制定以各机构的实际经营情况为出发点，根据机构绩效指标的历史情况和发展趋势，结合市场环境、利率水平和监管要求等方面因素“一行一策”制定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An institution would get 60 if it met T2 value.	指标达到T2值时可得60分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
T3 target value is set primarily based on the whole level of the Group and the best one of overseas institutions, directing overseas institutions to keep up with the whole group, and to boost continually their operation.	T3目标值设定主要以集团整体水平和境外机构的最优水平为基本依据，引导境外机构向集团水平看齐，不断提升经营水平。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Branches would get 100 if they reached the T3 value.	指标达到T3值时可得100分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Qualitative assessment indicators.	（2）定性考评指标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A leveled scoring method is used, that is, different levels of scoring are set according to degrees of meeting assessment indicators. A branch assessed would get points corresponding to that level if it had met assessment requirement of the level.	对定性评价指标采用分级计分法，即根据考评指标达标程度设定不同的计分级次，被考核行达到某级次的考核要求则得到该级次对应的分数。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Major application of assessment results	（三）考评结果的主要应用	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Assessment outcomes for overseas institutions are mainly used as important references to evaluate work performance of leaders at overseas institutions, resources allocation such as financial budget, overseas institutions’ bonus distribution, operation authorization, staff appointment and replacement and leave audit.	境外机构考评结果主要作为评价境外机构负责人工作业绩、财务预算等资源配置、境外机构奖金分配、经营授权、人事任免、离任稽核等方面的重要参考依据。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The institutions assessed can also take the assessment results as the analysis basis for their self-discipline assessment and the reference for improving the business management.	被考评单位也可将考评结果作为其自律性评价分析的依据和改进经营管理的参考。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VII. Taxation Management	七、应税事务管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Management approach	（一）管理方式	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC currently hires external consultant to provide globally uniform service on taxation consulting for the Head Office and all overseas institutions.	工商银行目前聘请了外部咨询顾问为总行及各境外机构提供全球统一的税务咨询服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The service provider’s global service agencies supply overseas branch consulting service on taxation of the country that the branch is located in. The Head Office and the provider‘s company in China, as general coordinators, monitor status of service supplied and collect service results.	该服务商的全球服务机构分别为境外机构提供所在国家的税务咨询，总行及服务商中国公司作为项目总协调人，监督服务情况、汇总服务成果。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Management contents	（二）管理内容	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A global taxation consulting service includes three parts: tax return, transfer pricing and international taxation planning.	全球税务咨询服务包括纳税申报、转移定价以及国际税收筹划三大板块。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Tax return	1.纳税申报	sample1-en-sample1-zh
China team of the consulting company monitors work progress of global institutions at all times through internal communication and project management tool, and periodically reports overseas institutions’ tax return progress together with problems combined to the Head Office.	咨询公司中国团队通过内部沟通和项目管理工具随时监控全球各机构的工作进展，并定期向总行提供境外机构的纳税申报进度报告及问题汇总。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Transfer pricing	2.转移定价	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It includes: (1) risk testing worldwide: assess and summarize risk of transfer pricing from aspects of country, enterprise, and business for all overseas institutions; (2) formulating transfer pricing policy: based on satisfying requirements of laws and regulations, assisting in formulating transfer pricing policies for all institutions by summarizing relevant laws and regulations of country (region) that each overseas institution is located in; and (3) information disclosure and documentation support: assisting overseas institutions in preparing for same-period materials, meeting requirements of disclosing related party transaction information of all areas, and reacting actively to inspection of authorities.	转移定价包括：（1）全球范围风险测试：从国家、企业、业务层面评估和总结各境外机构转移定价风险。 （2）转移定价政策制定：总结各境外机构所在国家（地区）的相关法规，在满足法规要求的基础上，协助制定我行各机构的转移定价政策。 （3）信息披露与文档支持：协助境外机构准备同期资料、协助满足各区域关联交易信息披露需求，主动应对监管机构的检查。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. International taxation planning	3.国际税收筹划	sample1-en-sample1-zh
International taxation planning may lower effectively global investment and financing costs, ensuring a free flow of foreign capital, enabling overseas institutions to obtain effective tax rates over competitors, and boosting maximizing benefits of shareholders at transnational company.	国际税收筹划可有效降低在全球范围内的投资和融资成本支出，保证海外资金自由流动，使境外机构获得优于竞争对手的有效税率，促进跨国公司股东利益最大化。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Presently, international taxation planning service used by ICBC mainly concentrates in three sides: perennial taxation consultancy, specific tax consultancy and tax policy updating.	目前工商银行采用的国际税收筹划服务主要集中于常年税务顾问、专项税务咨询、税务政策更新三方面。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VIII. Comprehensive System for Overseas Financial Management	八、境外财务管理综合系统	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC, through building electronic platform for a comprehensive system of overseas financial management, has achieved a unification and standard management of the Group’s financial expenses and financial resources worldwide, realized an integrated management system of financial payment and accounting approaches as well as financial management model both domestically and overseas.
