By constructing a total information database on overseas institutions’ financial affairs, ICBC builds globally a foundation for the Group’s refined financial management, providing data support and analysis methods for the Group’s optimized management over financial decisions, financial risk control, financial cost control and financial process control.	工商银行通过境外财务管理综合系统电子化平台的建设，在全球实现了集团财务费用及财务资源的统一、规范管理，实现境内了外财务支付和核算手段、财务管理模式的一体化管理；通过境外机构财务事件的全量信息数据库的建设，构建集团全球范围内财务精细化管理的基础，为全集团的财务决策、财务风险控制、财务成本控制、财务流程控制等环节的优化管理提供了数据支持和分析手段。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A comprehensive system for overseas financial management covers authorization approval, accounting & payment, information feedback, ledger management and fixed assets card management for all the financial monitoring items.	境外财务管理综合系统涵盖包括所有财务监控科目在内的授权审批、核算支付、信息反馈、台账管理、固定资产卡片管理等内容。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Two Capital Management System	第二节 资本管理制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Capital Management System	一、资本管理制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to regulate and strengthen capital management, with reference to documentation promulgated by the Basel Committee on Banking Supervision, according to the Management Measures for Capital Adequacy Ratios of Commercial Banks of China Banking Regulatory Commission (CBRC) and the Articles of Association of Industrial and Commercial Bank of China Limited, ICBC promulgated and implemented officially the Capital Management System in February 2008 applicable to all of its overseas and domestic branches.	为规范和加强资本管理，并借鉴巴塞尔银行监管委员会颁布的有关文件，依据中国银监会《商业银行资本充足率管理办法》和《中国工商银行股份有限公司章程》，工商银行《资本管理制度》于2008年2月正式颁布实施，该办法适用于全行境内外所有分支机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Primarily, ICBC manages capital aiming at first, maintaining a reasonable capital adequacy ratio level, keeping satisfying regulatory requirements, and guaranteeing the Bank’s safe operation; second, building the Bank’s value management system focusing on economic capital, optimizing the whole bank’s resources allocation and operation management system, and generating best return on capital for shareholders; and third, using varied capital tools, optimizing total capital amount and structure, and bringing down capital financing costs. 	工商银行资本管理的基本目标：一是保持合理的资本充足率水平，持续满足监管要求，确保银行安全运营；二是建立以经济资本为核心的银行价值管理体系，优化全行资源配置和经营管理机制，为股东创造最佳回报；三是运用各类资本工具，优化资本总量与结构，降低资本融资成本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Management Measures for Capital Adequacy Ratio	二、资本充足率管理办法	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to regulate and strengthen capital adequacy ratio management, with reference to documentation promulgated by the Basel Committee on Banking Supervision, according to the Management Measures for Capital Adequacy Ratios of Commercial Bank of CBRC and the Capital Management System of Industrial and Commercial Bank of China, ICBC promulgated and implemented officially the Management Measures for Capital Adequacy Ratio in February 2008 applicable to all of its overseas and domestic branches. The capital mentioned in the Measures includes core and supplementary capital, defined by regulatory regulations.	为规范和加强全行资本充足率管理，依据银监会《商业银行资本充足率管理办法》和《中国工商银行资本管理制度》，工商银行《资本充足率管理办法》于2008年2月正式颁布实施，该办法适用于全行境内外所有分支机构。 该办法所指资本包括符合监管规定的核心资本和附属资本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Core capital includes share capital, items recognized into capital reserve, general reserve, surplus reserve, items recognized into retained profits, and minority equity.	核心资本包括股本、资本公积可计入部分、一般准备、盈余公积、未分配利润可计入部分和少数股权等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Supplementary capital includes items recognized into revaluation reserve, general provision for loan impairment, preferred shares, convertible bonds, convertible bonds, long-term subordinated debits, and hybrid capital bonds.	附属资本包括重估储备可计入部分、贷款损失一般准备、优先股、可转换债券、长期次级债务及混合资本债券等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Capital definition and calculation way by an overseas branch shall follow regulatory requirements of the country or region where it is located.	境外分支机构的资本定义和计算方法应遵照所在国家或地区的监管规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
	该办法所指风险加权资产是资产负债表内和表外各类资产按照风险权重进行加权后的风险敞口、市场风险资本要求乘以12.5倍转化系数后的风险敞口之和。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
	境外分支机构的风险加权资产定义和计算方法应遵照所在国家或地区的监管规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Objective of capital adequacy ratio management	（一）资本充足率管理目标	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The management objective for ICBC is to set up a reasonable control target for its capital adequacy ratio, and restrict risk assets from an overexpansion, through establishing an efficient management system for the capital adequacy ratio on the premise of ensuring the whole bank’s capital adequacy ratio not lower than regulatory requirements.	工商银行资本充足率管理目标是通过建立有效的资本充足率管理机制，在确保全行资本充足率不低于监管要求的前提下，制定合理的资本充足率控制目标，约束风险资产过度扩张。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on the CBRC’s relevant requirements in the Management Measures for Capital Adequacy Ratios of Commercial Banks, the whole bank’s consolidated and unconsolidated capital adequacy ratio shouldn’t be lower than 8%; the whole bank’s consolidated and unconsolidated core capital adequacy ratio shouldn’t be lower than 4%; if regulatory authorities set dynamic regulatory indicators or raise minimum capital requirements, their requirements should be met.	根据中国银监会《商业银行资本充足率管理办法》的相关要求，全行并表口径和未并表口径资本充足率不得低于8%；全行并表口径和未并表口径核心资本充足率不得低于4%；若监管部门设置动态监管指标或提高最低资本要求，则须达到监管部门相关要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Moreover, in future, regulatory authorities in China might further boost minimum capital requirements for commercial banks according to relevant regulations in the Basel III.	此外，未来中国监管部门可能会根据巴塞尔协议III的相关规定，进一步提高商业银行最低资本要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An overseas branch should meet regulatory requirements for the minimum capital of the country or region where it is located.	境外分支机构应满足所在国家或地区的最低资本监管要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Capital adequacy ratio calculation	（二）资本充足率计算	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The calculation of consolidated and unconsolidated capital adequacy ratios should meet requirements of the CBRC’s Management Measures for Capital Adequacy Ratios of Commercial Banks as well as its follow-up normative documents. Computation ways for capital adequacy ratio by an overseas branch should meet regulatory requirements of the country or region where it is located.	并表口径和未并表口径的资本充足率计算应符合银监会《商业银行资本充足率管理办法》及后续规范性文件要求，境外分支机构的资本充足率计算方法应按照所在国家或地区的监管规定执行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Plan and control of capital adequacy ratio	（三）资本充足率计划与控制	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on the development strategies, the Head Office takes factors such as returns to shareholders, regulatory requirements, business expansion and external market environment into full consideration, and determines yearly targets of consolidated and unconsolidated capital adequacy ratios of ICBC.	总行根据发展战略，统筹考虑股东回报、监管要求、业务发展和外部市场环境等因素，确定工商银行并表口径和未并表口径的资本充足率年度目标值。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office sets current-year plans for risk assets control and capital supplementation (repurchase) based on the annual capital adequacy plan. In case of any significant events affecting capital adequacy ratio, the plan for capital adequacy ratio may be adjusted. 	总行根据年度资本充足计划，制定当年风险资产控制方案和资本补充（回购）方案，如发生影响资本充足率的重大事项，可调整资本充足率计划。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iv. Monitoring of and early warning about capital adequacy ratio	（四）资本充足率监测预警	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office monitors whole bank’s (including subsidiaries and holding institutions) capital adequacy status regularly.	总行定期监测全行（包括子行和控股机构）的资本充足状况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Typically, a monitoring frequency shouldn’t be less than once per quarter; under special mention and early warning, the frequency should be intensified according to specific situations; primarily, capital and risk assets changes are required to be monitored.	正常状态下，监测频度不少于每季一次，关注和预警状态下，根据具体情况提高监测频度；监测内容主要是资本变动和风险资产变动情况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to the bank-wide capital adequacy ratio target, an early warning interval for capital adequacy ratio is set up in order to distinguish three statuses: normal, special mention and early warning, and corresponding steps need to be taken.	根据全行资本充足率目标，设置资本充足率预警区间，区分正常、关注和预警三种状态并分别采取相应的措施。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
v. Information disclosure	（五）信息披露	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Regarding statistics related to capital adequacy ratio, authorized departments are responsible to disclose them to the public according to the system on information disclosure of ICBC, after approved by the Board of Directors.	资本充足率相关数据，经董事会批准后，由授权部门依据我行相关信息披露制度负责对外披露。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vi. Miscellaneous	（六）其他情况说明	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If CBRC adjusts its regulatory regulations on capital adequacy ratio of commercial banks, ICBC will calculate and disclose its capital adequacy ratio pursuant to new regulations.	如中国银监会对商业银行资本充足率相关监管规定进行调整，则工商银行按照新规定计算并披露资本充足率。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Management Measures for Economic Capital	三、经济资本管理办法	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to enhance economic capital management and improve capital management system, ICBC has promulgated and implemented officially the Management Measures for Economic Capital since February 2008 in accordance with the regulations such as the Capitla Management System of Industrial and Commercial Bank of China. The Measures are applicable to all of its domestic and overseas branches.	为规范经济资本管理，完善资本管理体系，依据《中国工商银行资本管理制度》等规定，工商银行《经济资本管理办法》于2008年2月正式颁布实施，该办法适用于全行境内外所有分支机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Objective of economic capital management	（一）经济资本管理目标	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For economic capital management, the objective of ICBC is to allocate capital return requirements to each branch and product by constructing an effective measurement and allocation system for economic capital, and to put restriction on its overall risk level through setting an economic capital limit in order to enhance an optimum allocation and effective usage of the whole bank’s resources. 	工商银行经济资本管理目标是通过建立有效的经济资本计量和配置体系，将资本回报的要求贯彻落实到各个分支机构和产品上，并通过经济资本限额对其风险总水平进行约束，以促进全行资源的优化配置和有效使用。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Economic capital measurement	（二）经济资本计量	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Economic capital measurement includes the calculation of economic capital supply, demand and buffering capacity.	经济资本计量包括经济资本供给量、经济资本需求量、经济资本缓冲量的计量。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The economic capital of the whole bank should maintain a dynamic balance between supply and demand.	全行经济资本供给量与经济资本需求量应保持动态平衡。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A difference, where economic capital supply is greater than demand, is regarded as the buffering capacity, used for strategic capital reserve and covering other risk economic capital needs.	经济资本供给量高于经济资本需求量的差额为经济资本缓冲量，用于战略性资本储备和覆盖其他风险经济资本需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An economic capital gap occurs when economic capital supply is less than demand.	经济资本供给量少于经济资本需求量的差额为经济资本缺口。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Economic capital allocation	（三）经济资本配置	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An economic capital allocation needs to maintain a dynamic balance between economic capital supply and demand. 	经济资本配置应保持经济资本供给量与经济资本需求量之间的动态平衡。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iv. Economic capital evaluation	（四）经济资本评价	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An economic capital evaluation is a comprehensive one made on risks and earnings of object evaluated with economic capital indicators, including evaluation contents, indicators, and frequency as well as application of evaluation results.	经济资本评价是运用经济资本指标，对评价对象的风险和收益进行综合评判。 评价要素包括评价内容、评价指标、评价频率和评价结果应用。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
v. Economic capital application	（五）经济资本应用	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC is gradually applying economic capital to such areas as bank-wide performance assessment, resources allocation, risk management, credit decisions, customer management, product pricing and institution management.	我行正逐步将经济资本全面应用于全行绩效考核、资源配置、风险管理、信贷决策、客户管理、产品定价和机构管理等领域。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vi. Monitoring and reporting of economic capital	（六）经济资本监测与报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Each domestic tier-one branch (or that directly under the Head Office) is required to send its half-year and annual reports on economic capital management regularly to the Head Office. Overseas institutions are required to send relevant statistical statements on economic capital to the Head Office regularly.	境内各一级（直属）分行定期向总行报送经济资本半年度、年度管理报告，境外分支机构定期向总行报送经济资本统计报表。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office combines the whole bank’s economic capital data, analyzes operating status and features of economic capital, and reports regularly to the Senior Management on economic capital management.	总行汇总全行经济资本相关数据，分析经济资本运用情况和特点，定期向高级管理层提交经济资本管理报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Three Credit Management System	第三节 信贷管理制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Overall Structure of Credit Management	一、信贷管理整体架构	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Organizational structure	（一）组织架构	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In recent years, ICBC is gradually constructing a flat organizational structure centering on the Head Office.	近年来，工商银行逐步建立以总行为中心的扁平化组织架构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office determines uniformly risk criteria and appetite, sets and issues credit policy system, directs the bank’s credit resources to be allocated scientifically among regions, sectors, products and customers, and manages the whole bank’s credit risks of all customers (corporate, institutional and personal, domestic and overseas); all branches conduct credit business within a scope permitted according to all kinds of normative documents issued by the Head Office, and feedback on the implementation of credit policy system.	总行统一确定风险标准和偏好，制定和发布信贷政策制度，指导全行信贷资源在区域、行业、产品、客户间的科学配置，对全行各类客户（公司、机构与个人，境内与境外）的信用风险进行管理；各分支机构根据总行发布的各类规范性文件，在权限内开展信贷业务，对政策制度执行情况进行反馈。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In terms of the Head Office, a Credit Risk Management Committee is built under the Senior Management, responsible for reviewing and approving of regulations involving bank-wide credit risk’s basic credit policy, management system, business process and related system standards; reviewing of yearly credit risk business’ basic authorization, the whole bank’s credit risk management reports, internal assessment and measurement models of credit risk, and important credit risk management issues. Functional departments of credit business are required to separate front-, middle- and back offices from each other with front-office departments in charge of marketing due diligence investigation of credit business, middle-office departments in charge of customer ratings-based credit extensions, business examination and approval, and back-office risk management departments in charge of formulating and issuing credit policies and systems as lending entry, business process operation, and post-lending management, undertaking post-lending supervision and inspection, and managing uniformly post-lending risks.	总行层面，高级管理层下设信用风险管理委员会，负责审议涉及全行信用风险的基本信贷政策、管理制度、业务流程和相关系统标准等规定，审议年度信用风险业务基本授权，审议全行信用风险管理报告，审议信用风险内部评估和计量模型，审核重大信用风险管理事项；信贷业务职能部门实行前、中、后台分离，前台部门负责信贷业务的营销尽职调查，中台部门负责客户评级授信、业务审查和审批，后台风险管理部门负责信贷准入、流程操作、贷后管理等信贷政策制度的制订和发布，承担贷后监督检查等职能，对贷后风险进行统一管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Figure 2-1 Organizational Structure of ICBC’s Credit Business	图2-1 工商银行信贷业务组织架构图	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Policy system	（二）政策体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC’s credit policy system is to set risk management target based on the whole bank’s development strategies and risk appetite, and to adjust and optimize timely the credit structure through business authorization and credit limit, ensuring an implementation of bank-wide development strategies, which involves four dimensions, that is, credit policies by customer, product, industry and region.	工商银行的信贷政策体系是根据全行的发展战略和风险偏好设定风险管理目标，通过业务授权、信贷限额等工具对信贷结构进行及时调整与优化，确保全行发展战略的贯彻实施，包括客户信贷政策、产品信贷政策、行业信贷政策和区域信贷政策四个维度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Customer credit policy	1.客户信贷政策	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customer credit policy is based on classification of customers, matching different financial services and management requirements to different customers.	客户信贷政策是基于客户分类，对不同的客户匹配不同的金融服务和管理要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to social and economic identities, customers may be divided into corporate and personal customers.	根据客户在社会经济生活中的身份，可将客户划分为公司客户和个人客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on nature of organization, corporate customers can be subdivided into legal representative of corporation, legal representative of public-sector organizations, organizations, and social groups.	根据组织性质对公司客户再进行细分，有企业法人、事业法人、机关团体、社会社团等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on organizational form of customers’ business growth and economic activities, customers can be divided into group, big, medium and small ones.	根据客户业务发展和经济活动的组织形式，可将客户划分为集团客户、大型客户、中型客户和微小型客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition, there are many other perspectives to classify customers.	除此以外，还有很多其他角度对客户进行分类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Since different customers have different credit demands and risk appetites, customer credit policy needs to subdivide customers by following the principle of matching credit resources input to output, conduct differential management and apply different credit entry criteria as well as patterns of ratings-based credit extensions and post-loan management standards based on the characteristics, ensuring a superior credit market to be expanded, and an entry of high-risk customers to be controlled, and enhancing a customer structure to be more reasonable.	不同的客户具有不同的信贷需求和风险偏好，客户信贷政策根据信贷资源投入与产出相匹配的原则，细分客户，根据其特性实行差异化管理，实行不同的信贷准入标准、评级授信模式和贷后管理标准等，从而拓展优质信贷市场，控制高风险客户的进入，促使客户结构更加合理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Product credit policy	2.产品信贷政策	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has constructed a diversified corporate and personal credit product system through recent years’ development and innovation.	经过近年来的发展和创新，工商银行构建了多元化的法人、个人信贷产品体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate credit products include working capital loans, trade finance, project loans, property loans, and bills as well as off-balance sheet business such as gurantee and commitment. Personal credit products cover financing requirements for all areas such as personal housing, business, consumption, health care and education. Different products are matched with different risk control requirements for business processing conditions, business processing flow and duration management, according to their risk characteristics.	法人信贷产品包括流动资金贷款、贸易融资、项目贷款、房地产贷款、票据业务产品以及担保、承诺等表外业务产品；个人信贷产品覆盖了个人住房、经营、消费、医疗教育等各个领域的融资需求，不同的产品根据其风险特征分别匹配不同的业务办理条件、业务处理流程和存续期管理等风险控制要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Industry credit policy	3.行业信贷政策	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on industry development conditions, industry credit policy is used to judge an industry’s overall risks, discover its market opportunity and identify superior customers of a industry as well as provide them with differential credit strategies.	行业信贷政策根据行业发展状况，判断行业整体风险，挖掘行业市场机会，甄别行业优质客户并提供差异化信贷策略。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An industry consists of enterprise groups with common characteristics. For a same industry, its enterprise members shares the same or similar features in production and operation, and products or services can replace one another.	行业由具有共同特性的企业群体组成，同一行业内的企业成员在生产经营上存在着相同性或相似性，其产品或服务具有很强的替代性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Once industry credit risk occurs, which means that quite a large number of enterprises in an industry suffer from risk, they will affect seriously commercial banks.	一旦发生行业信贷风险，即意味着同一行业内相当一部分企业出现了风险，对商业银行影响很大。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Industry credit risk management, between macro-risk management for forecasting and judging a growth trend of whole economy, and micro-risk management primarily for single customer, belongs to a scope of medium-risk management.	行业信贷风险管理是介于对整个经济走势进行预测判断的宏观风险管理和以单个客户为主的微观风险管理之间的中观风险管理范畴。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Industry credit policy is the one for industry credit resources allocation based on credit risk characteristics shown during development cycles of an industry and a bank’s strategic development targets, including compulsory policies on industry orientation and limit management, and instructive industry advices and information reminders and alerts on industry trends. Industry credit policy is used to control the excessive concentration of loans in part of areas or highly related industries, achieving the adjustment and optimization of industry credit structure, and preventing systematic risks.	行业信贷政策是基于行业发展周期呈现出的信贷风险特征和银行发展战略目标而制定的行业信贷资源配置政策，包括具有强制执行力的行业投向和限额管理政策、具有指导性的行业指导意见和对行业动向的信息提示和预警，用于控制贷款在部分领域或高关联度行业的过度集中，实现行业信贷结构调整优化，防范系统性风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
By the end of June 2011, ICBC has formulated credit policies for more than forty industries, dividing industries into such four categories as active entry, moderate entry, prudent entry and limited entry ones, dividing an industry’s internal customers into such five categories as important, moderate, remained, restricted and exit ones, and matching different credit entry criteria and management requirements to them.	截至2011年6月末，工商银行制定了40余个行业的信贷政策，将行业划分为积极进入类、适度进入类、谨慎进入类和限制进入类，行业内部客户分为重点类、适度类、维持类、限制类和退出类，匹配不同的信贷准入标准和管理要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, by following China’s industrial and environment protection policies, ICBC advocates implementing the “Green Credit”, says no to all customers or projects unable to meet requirements of environment protection policies, eliminates actively backward capacities, and strengthens loan supports to energy-saving, pollution treatment, circular economy and integrated use of resources.	同时，工商银行遵循国家产业政策、环保政策，倡导实施“绿色信贷”，对达不到环保政策要求的客户或项目一律予以否决，积极淘汰落后产能，加大对节能环保、污染治理、循环经济和资源综合利用等领域的信贷支持力度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Regional credit policy	4.区域信贷政策	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Regional credit policy, including ones for regional credit increase, quality management, structural adjustment, performance/efficiency and competition, is a key part of the entire credit policy system.	区域信贷政策包括区域信贷增长政策、质量管理政策、结构调整政策、效益/效率政策和竞争政策等方面内容，是整体信贷政策体系的重要组成部分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A multiple-level regional credit system includes varied levels involving country, economic region, industry region and administrative region.	一个多层次的信贷区域体系包含国家、经济区域、产业区域、行政区域等不同层次。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Regional credit policy differs from other credit ones in addressing more about a comprehensive feature, and its primary purpose is to improve development and enhance competition, calling for taking all factors into consideration.	区域信贷政策与其他信贷政策的主要不同是更加强调综合化，根本目的是促发展、促竞争，需要统筹兼顾。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With an accelerated progress of ICBC in internationalization, country risk management tends to be important (country risk refers to a possibility of loss from cross-border loans. Such loss is caused by a country-specific event but not by a private enterprise or individual).	随着工商银行国际化进程加快，国别风险管理日趋重要（国别风险是指跨边界贷款中的损失的可能性，这种损失是由某个特定国家发生的事件所引起，而不是由私人企业或个人所引起）。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC performs a classified management on country risk, dividing it into five categories in terms of risk level: low, relatively low, medium, relatively high, and high.	工商银行对国别风险进行分类管理，按照风险高低分为“低、较低、中等、较高、高”五类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Each year, the Head Office appraises and decides country limit for each country. All institutions should process businesses within those country limits. For any excess, they need to apply to the Head Office for increasing limits.	每年度总行会对各个国家核定国别限额，各机构应在国别限额内办理业务，超限额应向总行申请调增额度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Major Credit Management Regulations	二、信贷管理主要规定	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Basic standards for credit business	（一）信贷业务基本准则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
At ICBC, credit business needs to obey the following basic standards:	在工商银行，办理信贷业务应遵守基本准则包括：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Credit business shall meet laws and regulations of the country where it is located, as well as all management regulations of the Head Office.	1.办理信贷业务应遵守所在国家法律法规，以及总行各项管理规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Credit risk appetites shall be consistent with the Head Office.	2.信贷风险偏好应与总行保持一致。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. A complete credit business policy system shall be constructed, and maintained stable.	3.应建立完善的信贷业务政策制度体系，并保持稳定性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. An efficient allocation shall be conducted for credit assets, avoiding an overconcentration of risk exposure on a certain customer, region, industry, country and product.	4.应对信贷资产实施有效配置，避免对某一客户、区域、行业、国家、产品风险敞口过分集中。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For country and industry limits, relevant businesses shall be processed within limits.	对总行要求执行的国别、行业等限额，应在限额内办理相关业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. Great attention shall be paid to risk pricing management. Other cost factors such as economic capital occupation shall be taken into consideration other than customer earning level which needs to be matched with his/her risk level.	5.应重视风险定价管理，客户收益水平除应与其风险水平相匹配外，还应考虑经济资本占用等其他成本因素。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
6. Great concern shall be paid to environment protection and a boost of Green Credit construction. Environment protection, energy-saving and pollution treatment shall be taken as an important basis for credit decisions.	6.应重视环境保护，推动绿色信贷建设，将促进环境保护、资源节约、污染治理等作为信贷决策的重要依据。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
7. Immoral and illegal business is forbidden. Businesses with customers who are imposed sanction by organizations or institutions producing legal effects such as the United Nations and European Union are not allowed. Speculative trading and credit business involving money laundering and terrorist financing are forbidden. And	7.不能与从事不道德的、非法的，以及联合国、欧盟等具有法律效力的组织或机构制裁的客户办理业务，不能参与投机性交易，不能参与与洗钱和恐怖融资相关的信贷业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
8. When processing credit business, a principle of fairness shall be obeyed. Criteria and process flow for stakeholders’ credit business shall not be superior to that for normal borrower.	8.办理信贷业务应遵循公平性原则，对关系人办理信贷业务的标准、流程等应不优于一般借款人。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A credit officer cannot handle his/her related person’s credit business and shall avoid.	信贷人员不能办理与自己相关的关系人信贷业务，应采取回避制度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Basic process for credit business	（二）信贷业务基本流程	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC implements standard credit business process, which typically goes through such operational steps as due diligence investigation- review - approval- contract signing- loan disbursement approval- loan disbursement (business transaction) - post-loan management – repayment by the borrower (disposal of non-performing loans).	工商银行实行标准化信贷业务流程，信贷业务流程一般要经过尽职调查-审查－审批－合同签订－放款核准－贷款发放（业务办理）－贷后管理－贷款收回（不良贷款处置）等操作环节。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After receiving customer’s application, a customer manager at front-office banking department should make a due diligence investigation on the customer, checking whether the documents are legal, true and valid, produce an initial plan on rating and credit extension, and submit this plan to a risk manager for review.	接到客户申请后，前台业务部门客户经理应对客户进行尽职调查，对其所提供资料的合法性、真实性、有效性进行核实，形成评级及业务授信的初步方案，提交风险经理提出审查意见。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For the application which needs to be submitted to the Credit Risk Committee for review, afterwards it will be sent to an authorized signatory for final approval; for the application needing no collective review, it will be reported directly to an authorized signatory for final approval.	对于需要需提交信用风险委员会审议的，经审议后提交业务有权签批人进行最终签批；对无需提交集体审议的，直接报业务有权签批人进行业务最终签批。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After business review and approval, the customer manager communicates with customer and monitor customer to meet preconditions and other requirements for approval before issuing a loan.	业务审批后，客户经理与客户沟通并督促客户落实前提条件以及其他放款前须落实的审批要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If it is accepted by customer, office staffs need to be notified to prepare financing agreement (according to requirements, legal review staffs submit legal opinions), and afterwards the two parties sign the financing agreement.	客户接受的，通知文本人员准备融资协议文本（根据需要，由法律审查人员出具法律意见），双方签订融资协议文本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Before disbursing loan, customer manager should send relevant supporting documents involving customer’s meeting preconditions to risk manager for checking and confirmation.	贷款发放前，客户经理应将客户落实前提条件涉及的有关证明材料，提交风险经理进行核查确认。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Subsequently, loan can be disbursed.	核查确认后，方能进行放款环节操作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After transaction, customer manager needs to make an onsite inspection on customer, get to know regular operational status such as customer’s cash flows in order to guarantee safety of loan, produce a post-loan inspection report and submit it to risk manager.	业务办理后，客户经理应对客户进行现场检查，了解客户现金流等日常经营情况，保证贷款安全，形成贷后检查报告提交给风险经理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Risk manager, based on the inspectin report and offsite monitoring, makes a comprehensive analysis on customer and business risks.	风险经理在检查报告及非现场监测基础上，对客户及业务风险进行综合分析。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If any problem is detected, risk manager needs to set risk prevention steps, and sends reminder and alert against risk to banking department, pushing it to taking relevant steps.	若发现问题，拟订风险防范措施，向业务部门进行风险提示和预警，督促采取措施。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Besides, regular asset quality classification should be made for credit assets.	业务办理后，还应定期对信贷资产进行资产质量分类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Before maturity, customer manager should remind customer of repaying the loan plus interest in time, preparing for relevant material on customer’s repayment.	业务到期前，客户经理应提示客户按时还本付息，提前准备客户还款有关资料。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
On the maturity day, loan recovery operation is conducted, and afterwards risk manager should review the collateral or pledge release if any, prepare for collateral or pledge release list and release the collateral or pledge after submitting the list to an authorized person for signature.	贷款到期当日，实施贷款收回操作。 贷款收回后，涉及抵押物释放的，风险经理应对抵质押物释放情况进行审核，准备抵质押物释放清单，提交有权人签字后，进行抵质押物释放操作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Customer credit rating	（三）客户信用评级	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Rating on non-retail banking	1.非零售业务评级	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customer rating is a comprehensive assessment on its solvency and debt-paying willingness, the results of which reflect a probability of default (PD) within a year. One customer only has one customer rating.	法人客户评级是对法人客户偿债能力和偿债意愿的综合评价，评级结果反映其一年期违约概率，同一客户只有一个客户评级。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Rating is required before business with a corporate customer.	对法人客户办理业务前，均要求进行评级。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For other members in a group who have been already rated, their rating results should be directly used.	集团内其他成员已经进行评级的，应直接使用其评级结果。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to ICBC’s relevant regulations, currently, credit ratings of a corporate customer are divided into fourteen levels based on different probabilities of default, each level corresponding to a determinate range of PD and average PD.	根据工商银行相关制度规定，目前法人客户信用等级根据其对应的违约概率不同，分别划分为十四个级别，每个等级均对应一个确定的违约概率区间和平均违约概率。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Rating a corporate customer is based on the scoring card method, adjusted and limited in special situations.	法人客户信用评级采用打分卡的方法进行评价，并根据特殊情况进行级别调整与限定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Scoring card based rating consists of two parts, quantative and qualitative assessments.	打分卡评级由定量评价和定性评价两部分构成。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Quantative assessment indicators, following such principles as strong ability in forecasting default, low correlationship between indicators, and clear economic meaning, are selected using statistical methods such as AR value analysis, KS test, and Spearman’s rank correlation coefficient.	定量评价指标基于违约预测能力强、指标间相关性较低、经济含义明确等原则，采用AR值分析、KS检验、Spearman秩相关性分析等统计方法选取。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Weights for quantitative assessment indicators, on the principle of the larger contribution to default forecasting, the bigger weights are, are set with the logistic regression analysis.	定量评价指标权重基于违约预测贡献越大权重越大的原则，采用logistic回归分析法进行设定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Qualitative assessment indicators, based on principles of strong ability in forecasting default, being prospective and objective, and able-to-operate, are selected using statistical methods such as IV value analysis, monotonicity analysis and concentration analysis with weights being set according to each indicator’s forecasting ability in default.	定性评价指标基于违约预测能力强、前瞻性、客观性和可操作性等原则，采用IV值分析、单调性分析、集中度分析等统计方法进行选取，并根据各指标违约预测能力设定权重。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Rating on retail banking	2.零售业务评级	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An internal rating on retail credit assets refers to, through an internal ratings-based approach such as credit scoring models and asset pool division, realizes the measurements of credit scoring, PD, loss given default (LGD), and exposure at default as well as indicators related to internal rating, the results of which are applied to the whole process of operation management.	零售信贷资产内部评级是指通过信用评分模型、资产池划分等内部评级方法，实现零售信贷资产信用评分、违约概率、违约损失率、违约风险暴露以及内部评级相关指标的计量，并将计量结果应用于经营管理的全过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Retail credit risk rating approach includes two models, i.e. credit scoring and asset pool division, as well as risk parameter measurement.	零售信用风险评级方法包括信用评分和资产池划分与风险参数计量两类模型。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on above two models, results of retail banking credit risk rating can be obtained as between 100 to 850. The Head Office sets rigid controlling lines for scores by product and region.	零售业务根据上述模型，得出信用风险评分结果（100分-850分之间），总行分产品、地区设置评分刚性控制线。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iv. Global credit line	（四）统一授信	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Definition	1.统一授信定义	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Global credit line refers to a management system that a credit plan is examined uniformly worldwide for customer, and customer’s credit exposure is controlled collectively.	统一授信是指工商银行在全球范围内为客户统一核定授信方案，并集中控制客户信用敞口的管理制度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit plan typically contains the maximum credit line; sub-credit line; credit type, period, pricing, guarantee, conditions of use and management requirements, as well as other credit support and risk control measures which include other commercial terms that are set for customers.	授信方案一般包括对客户制定的最高授信额度、分项授信额度和授信品种、期限、定价、担保、使用条件、管理要求及其他商务条款等在内的信用支持与风险管控措施。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Under the maximum credit line, different sub-credit lines are set based on types of credit business for management.	最高授信额度项下按照授信业务的类型设不同分项授信额度进行管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The maximum credit line is used to control uniformly a customer’s total credit exposures.	最高授信额度用于统一控制客户的总信用敞口。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Besides that financial derivative products are converted into credit exposures according to credit risk coefficients, and that credit exposures are determined for loan commitments according to amount committed in the agreement, credit exposures are calculated for other credit types according to the balances.	除金融衍生产品交易按信用风险系数折算信用敞口、承诺授信按协议承诺金额确定信用敞口外，其余授信品种均按余额计算信用敞口。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Total credit exposures for a customer can’t exceed the maximum credit line set by ICBC at any time point.	客户的总信用敞口在任何时点均不得超过我行对其核定的最高授信额度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Basic principles	2.统一授信基本原则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit appetites shall be unified.	授信偏好统一。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Both domestic and overseas institutions, based on the whole bank’s unified risk appetites, need to follow identical standards and requirements, and make objective, fair and accurate assessment on customers’ or loans’ risk level and solvency. Under preconditions of meeting relevant regulations, and ICBC’s capital management, business development and risk control requirements, they need to examine reasonably customer credit plan, and realize an effective balance between risk and return, quality and efficiency.	境内外机构应基于全行统一的风险偏好，遵照相同的标准和要求，客观、公正、准确评判客户或债项的风险水平和偿债能力，在符合监管有关规定、我行资本管理、业务发展与风险控制等经营要求的前提下，合理核定客户授信方案，实现风险与收益、质量与效率的有效平衡。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit entity shall be unified.	授信主体统一。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For the same customer (including related customer), only one institution at ICBC is allowed to examine credit plan according to the prescribed procedures and authority.	对同一客户（含关联客户）只能由全行的一个机构按规定程序和授权权限核定授信方案。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit form shall be unified.	授信形式统一。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Off and on-balance sheet credit risk businesses of domestic and foreign currency involving working capital loan, trade finance, project loan, guarantee, bills, overdraft, inter-bank placement, commitment, bond investment in banking book and financial derivatives trading are entirely included into the global credit line management.	对客户办理的营运资金贷款、贸易融资、项目贷款、担保、票据、透支、拆借、承诺、银行账户债券投资、金融衍生产品交易等本外币、表内外信用风险业务均纳入统一授信管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit currencies shall be unified.	授信币种统一。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
When examining customer credit plans, based on ICBC’s business development and risk management needs, domestic and overseas institutions shall select RMB, USD, or one of other official currencies of places with which ICBC handles businesses primarily or where the major operating institutions are located as the currency for credit line.	核定客户授信方案时，应根据工商银行业务发展和风险管理需要，选择人民币、美元、工商银行与其主要的业务往来币种或其主要经营机构所在地的法定流通货币中的一种作为授信额度的核定币种。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
v. Authorization management	（五）授权管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Primarily, ICBC performs credit business authorization management through a corporate authorization system.	工商银行主要通过法人授权体系实现信贷业务授权管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate authorization refers to the one that the Head Office or upper-level branch delegates authority to its affiliated institutions for conducting various Business management activities, within the scope prescribed by national laws, regulations and Articles of Association of the Bank.	法人授权是指总行或上级行在国家法律、法规和银行章程规定的范围内，对所属机构从事各项业务管理活动的授权。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For overseas branches, the Head Office passes business authorization down to branch managers each year. For overseas subsidiaries, the Parent Bank passes down authorization each year in the form of resolutions by the Shareholders’ General Meeting. Each institution shall engage in various businesses within the authorized scope.	对于境外分行，总行每年对分行总经理下达业务授权，对于境外子行，母行每年以股东大会决议的方式下达授权。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For any business exceeding the authorization if necessary, it needs to be reported to the Head Office for review and approval (or examination) or apply for a special authorization.	各机构应在授权范围内办理各类业务，如确需办理超授权业务，应报总行审批(或审核)或申请特别授权。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Within an institution, it shall establish a clear internal system of sub-authorization according to management requirement for sub-authorization. The authorized signatory shall review and approve business within his/her authority permitted.	在机构内部应按照转授权管理要求，内部建立清晰的转授权体系，有权签批人应在规定权限内进行业务审批。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vi. Guarantee management	（六）担保管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
All institutions of ICBC can only accept legitimate and compliant guarantees, and also consider such factors as the Head Office’s system, local laws and regulations, regulatory requirements, market practices, ownership of collateral or pledge and its value stability, liquidity and realization to determine reasonably collateral or pledge types that they can accept and corresponding collateral or pledge ratio.	工商银行各机构仅能接受合法合规的担保，并应考虑总行制度、当地法律规定、监管要求、市场惯例、抵质押物权属及价值稳定性、抵质押物流动性和变现难易程度等因素合理确定可接受抵质押物种类和相应的抵质押率。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The main collaterals or pledges acceptable to ICBC include mortgage on real estate, personal deposit (certificate of deposit) pledge, bonds (except structural bonds), charging right, receivable and stock (shareholding right) pledge. The main warrandice that ICBC can accept are guarantee provided by sovereign institution within a country limit assessed by the Head Office, guarantee provided by international financial organizations with a long-term “AAA” or above credit rating by Moody’s or Standard & Poor’s, guarantee provided by correspondent bank already having credit line assessed, and guarantee provided by corporate customer with a credit rating being “A-2” or above.	工商银行主要可接受的抵质押物主要有：房地产抵押，存款（单）质押，债券（结构性债券除外）、收费权、应收账款、股票（权）质押等；主要接受的保证担保有：总行核定国家限额内主权机构提供的担保；穆迪或标准普尔长期信用评级A以上国际金融组织提供的担保；已核有授信额度的代理行提供的担保；信用等级在A2级（含）以上的公司客户提供的担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
When accepting collateral or pledge guarantee, normally, ICBC, as the exclusive mortgagee (pledge), shall have a priority right that is not inferior to other mortgagee (pledge).	接受抵质押担保时，一般本行须为唯一抵（质）押权人或享有不劣于其他抵（质）押权人的受偿权。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Generally, ICBC can’t accept mortgage or pledge guarantee with mortgagor’s subject qualification having flaws, unclear ownership of collateral or pledge, diffculty in realization, big fluctuations in value and that involving lawsuit.	一般不得接受抵押人主体资格存在瑕疵、抵押物权属不明确、不易变现、价值波动大以及涉及诉讼的抵质押担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It is required to conduct collateral (creditor’s rights) confirmation procedures such as registration of collateral or pledge, according to laws of the place where collateral or pledge is located.	应按照抵质押物所在地法律要求办理抵质押登记等押品（债权）确认手续。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An evaluation and regular monitoring shall be performed on collateral value.	应对押品价值进行评估和定期监测。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vii. Post-loan management	（七）贷后管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Post-loan management of ICBC refers to peforming onsite inspection and offsite monitoring on credit assets, identity any possible risk affecting debt service and make effective response to prevent and mitigate customer risks within the duration of a credit business.	工商银行的贷后管理是必须在信贷业务存续期内，对信贷资产进行现场检查和非现场监测，识别出的可能影响还款能力的风险，并做出有效的回应，从而达到防范化解客户风险的目的。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customer manager shall keep track on customer’s operational and credit use status by visiting customer, talking to customer on phone and information collection, find out possible risks, and put forward initial opinion on risk control.	客户经理应通过客户走访、电话会谈、信息搜集等方式，对客户的经营状况和授信使用情况进行动态跟踪，发现风险隐患，初步提出风险控制意见。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A post-loan inspection on customer mainly focuses on the following: whether credit fund has been applied as per contract requirements; whether customer’s debt service has changed through an analysis on customer’s operational and financial status; performing key inspection based on business type and feature; and checking value of collateral.	对客户贷后检查，主要侧重以下方面：信贷资金是否按照合同约定使用；通过分析客户经营、财务状况分析客户偿债能力是否发生变化；针对业务品种特点，区别对待重点检查；对押品价值情况进行检查。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Opinions after post-loan inspection shall be reported to risk manager.	贷后检查形成的意见应报送给风险经理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Risk manager analyzes risk profile of ICBC’s credit asset portfolio, mainly through offsite monitoring.	风险经理主要通过非现场监测方式分析本行信贷资产组合风险状况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Risk manager shall pay major attention to significant changes in market environment, industries with concentration of ICBC’s loans, significant but adverse changes in country risk, status of credit assets by country, industry, customer and income structure at ICBC, changes in asset quality migration, comprehensive status of assets of industries with relatively concentrated loans of ICBC and exposed to bigger fluctuation in operation, customers borrowing a lot, customers with low credit rating, unsecured loans and comprehensive status of special-mention assets.	风险经理应重点对市场环境重大变化，本行融资较为集中的行业、国别风险重大不利变化；本行信贷资产国别、行业、客户、收益结构情况；资产质量迁徙变化情况；融资较为集中、且经营波动较大行业资产整体情况；融资大户、信用等级较低客户、信用贷款、关注类资产整体情况。 资产组合风险状况应定期报告高管层。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
viii. Credit risk reporting	（八）信用风险报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Each institution of ICBC shall report to the Head Office regularly on risks, covering its credit business development and quality, details on major customers with higher risks, issues identified in regulatory inspections with respect to credit management and relevant requirements.	工商银行各机构应定期向总行履行风险报告义务，定期向总行报告事项包括：本行信贷业务发展及质量情况，风险较高重点客户具体情况，监管检查中发现的信贷管理方面问题以及相关要求等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If loan deteriorates, or customer suffers a big loss or crisis that may result in the impairment of ICBC’s assets, all institutions shall make report to the Head Office in time.	如遇贷款出现劣变，或客户发生重大损失、危机，可能导致我行资产损失，应及时向总行报告有关情况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Person-in-charge of risks at each institution needs to report its risk management status to the Chief Risk Officer of the Head Office at least yearly.	各机构主管风险的负责人应至少每年向总行首席风险官汇报本行风险管理现状。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ix. Asset quality classification	（九）资产质量分类	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit asset quality classification is to examaine credit asset quality regularly, analyze and classify the examination results on the principle of prudence and out of the risk management needs, based on the inherent risk characteristics of credit assets.	信贷资产质量分类是工商银行出于审慎的原则和风险管理的需要，根据信贷资产的内在风险特征，定期对信贷资产质量进行审查，并将审查的结果进行分析和归类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Grades and standards regarding credit asset quality classification serve as a benchmark to measure credit business’ inherent risks.	信贷资产质量分类的档次和标准是衡量信贷业务内在风险的一种价值尺度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
At ICBC, credit assets are classified into 5 categories: normal, special-mention, substandard, doubtful and loss. Credit assets for corporate customers are sub-classified into twelve categories based on above.	工商银行信贷资产分为正常、关注、次级、可疑和损失五类，法人客户在上述基础上细分为十二类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Normal: debtors can perform contact’s obligations. There is no adequate reason to doubt their ability to repay all of the loan principals and interests and other debts in time.	正常类：债务人能够履行合同，没有足够理由怀疑贷款本息和其他债务（含或有债务）不能按时足额偿还。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Special mention: though debtors currently have the ability to repay the loan principals and interests and other debts, there exist some factors possibly producing negative effects on repayment of debts.	关注类：尽管债务人目前有能力偿还贷款本息和其他债务，但存在一些可能对偿还债务产生不利影响的因素。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Substandard: there are apparent problems with the solvency of debtors, who are unable to repay all of the loan principals and interests and other debts if totally rely on their normal business incomes. Even a guarantee may incur a loss.	次级类：债务人的偿债能力明显出现问题，完全依靠其正常营业收入无法足额偿还贷款本息和其他债务，即使执行担保，也可能会造成一定损失。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Doubtful: debtors are unable to repay all of the loan principals and interests and other debts. Even a guarantee will definitely incur a big loss. And	可疑类：债务人无法足额偿还贷款本息和其他债务，即使执行担保，也肯定会造成较大损失。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Loss: even after all possible measures or necessary legal proceedings are taken, the loan principals and interests and other debts cannot be recovered, or only a very small part can be paid back.	损失类：在采取所有可能的措施或一切必要的法律程序后，贷款本息和其他债务仍然无法收回，或只能收回极少部分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
x. Credit archives management At ICBC, there are primarily the following types of credit archives:	（十）信贷档案管理 工商银行信贷档案主要有以下种类：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Warrants: for credit business by collateral (pledge), these documents are able to demonstrate that ICBC has the right to mortgage (pledge) and its value, including documents proving ownership of collateral (pledge), collateral (pledge) list, insurance policy for collateral (pledge), and collateral (pledge) notarization.	权证类：以抵（质）押办理信贷业务，能够证明我行享有抵（质）押权及抵质押物价值的的资料。 包括：抵（质）押所有权证明文件、抵（质）押物清单、抵（质）押物保险单、抵（质）押物公证书等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Important documents: these are materials able to prove the legitimacy and compliance of credit business during transaction, including customer application, due diligence report, risk investigation report, minute of Credit Risk Committee, credit review and approval letter, loan contract, commitment letter of intent, guarantor’s contract of guarantee, advice of drawing for business and materials generated for post-loan management.	要件类：办理信贷业务中产生的能证明信贷业务合法合规性的材料。 包括：客户申请书、尽职调查报告、风险审查报告、信用风险委员会纪要、贷款审批书、贷款合同、各类承诺意向函、保证人保证合同、业务提款通知书、贷后管理形成的档案资料。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Management documents: basic materials about borrower, guarantor and cooperative institution, including customer’s signature and financial statements.	管理类：借款人和保证人、合作机构的基本资料。 客户印鉴证明、财务报表信息等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Documents for preservation: relevant documents to lawsuit or disposal of non-performing loans.	保全类：涉及诉讼或者不良贷款处置的相关资料。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Comprehensive documents: in-house by-laws and regulations on authorization and sub-authorization.	综合类：行内各类制度办法、授权转授权规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
All credit business archives need to be kept collectively in a fire-proof cabinet with “one customer-to-one archive”.	所有信贷业务档案都应该集中保管在防火的柜子中。 应做到“一户一档”。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
On the cover of archive for a customer, there is table of contents for inquiry.	在每户档案封面，有可供查询的目录。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
All archives are stored in the same format.	所有档案存放成相同格式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Specific staffs are responsible for managing keys to the cabinets, and borrowing registration.	应有专人负责管理档案柜钥匙，对档案实行借阅登记工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
xi. Global Credit Management System (GCMS)	（十一）全球信贷管理系统（GCMS）	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With a steady implementation of the globalization strategy, ICBC has developed a Global Credit Management System (GCMS) independently, aimed at building an information system covering domestic and overseas corporate customers, institutional customers, personal customers and counterparties, and extending 24-hour supports to asset business operation, risk control and management and business decision-making and analysis of domestic and overseas institutions. GCMS will fully enhance ICBC’s information management level with respect to credit business and provide a credit business supporting system of technology innovation that is consistent with an internationally first-class commercial bank.	随着工商银行全球化战略的稳步实施，工商银行自主研发的全球信贷管理系统将打造一个覆盖境内外公司客户、机构客户、个人客户、交易对手，全天候支持境内外机构资产业务操作、风险控制管理、经营决策分析的信息系统，全面提升工商银行信贷业务信息化管理水平，锻造与国际一流商业银行相适应的信贷业务创新技术支撑体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Four Enterprise Risk Management System	第四节 全面风险管理制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Organizational Structure and Framework of Enterprise Risk Management	一、全面风险管理组织架构和管理框架	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC’s organizational structure of risk management comprises the Board of Directors and its special committees, the Senior Management and its special committees, the Risk Management Department and the Internal Audit Department, etc.	董事会及其专门委员会、高级管理层及其专业委员会、风险管理部门和内部审计部门等构成工商银行风险管理的组织架构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The risk management organizational structure is illustrated in Figure 2-2:	工商银行风险管理组织架构如图2-2：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Figure 2-2 ICBC’s Organizational Structure of Risk Management	图2-2 工商银行风险管理组织架构	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Regulatory requirements and management practice	（一）监管要求及管理实践	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In July 2009, the Basel Committee on Banking Supervision issued the Enhancements to the Basel II Framework, addressing basic requirements for constructing a comprehensive risk management framework under Pillar II, including mainly general principles of comprehensive risk management, supervision by the board of directors and senior management, risk management policy and limit, risk management process, and comprehensive internal controls.	2009年7月，巴塞尔银行监管委员会印发了《新资本协议完善框架》，在第二支柱的指导意见中，突出强调了构建全面风险管理框架的基本要求，主要包括全面风险管理的总体原则、董事会和高级管理层监督、风险管理政策和限额、风险管理流程、全面的内部控制等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The document also proposes to strengthen the management of other substantial risks not under Pillar I, and makes clear that stress testing shall be taken as an important tool for risk management.	文件还提出加强对第一支柱外的其他实质性风险的管理、明确将压力测试作为风险管理的重要工具等要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Ever since 2009, CBRC has consecutively issued a series of regulatory documents in order to promote the implementation of new capital accord by China’s banking industry.	2009年以来，银监会为推进中国银行业实施新资本协议，陆续出台了一系列监管文件。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In December 2009, CBRC issued the Guidance for Supervision and Inspection of Commercial Banks’s Capital Adequacy Ratios (Y.J.F. [2009] No.109) (the “Guidance”), which aims to pushing banks to construct a reasonable, efficient internal capital adequacy assessment process (ICAAP), improving comprehensive risk management framework, fully assessing various substantial risks and management abilities, strengthening the management of substantial risks such as concentration risk, strategic risk and reputational risk on the basis of credit, market and operational risks under Pillar I, and setting up corresponding risk management policies and processes.	2009年12月，银监会印发了《商业银行资本充足率监督检查指引》（银监发[2009]109号）（以下简称为《指引》）。 《指引》的目的是要银行建立合理有效的内部资本充足评估程序（ICAAP），完善全面风险管理框架，全面评估其面临的各类实质性风险状况和管理能力，在第一支柱信用、市场和操作风险的基础上，加强对集中度风险、战略风险、声誉风险等实质性风险的管理，建立相应的风险管理政策和流程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Guidance puts forward clearly the elements that shall be contained in an assessment of a bank’s comprehensive risk management framework.	《指引》明确提出评估银行全面风险管理框架所应包含的要素。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In 2004, the Committee of Sponsoring Organizations of the Treadway Commission (COSO) in the U.S. issued the Enterprise Risk Management – Integrated Framework, becoming an important reference for risk management framework construction in the banking industry. 	2004年美国COSO发布了《企业风险管理－整合框架》，成为业内风险管理框架建设的重要参考。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Enterprise risk management framework	（二）全面风险管理框架	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Principles of enterprise risk management	1.全面风险管理原则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Match risk to return.	（1）风险与收益匹配。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Take both risk and return into consideration, carry out business activities under a moderate risk level, and ensure return to cover risk and appropriate returns to shareholders.	兼顾风险与收益管理风险，在适度风险水平下开展经营活动，确保收益覆盖风险并实现适当的股东回报。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Consider both an internal balance and efficiency.	（2）内部制衡与效率兼顾。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has defined clearly in risk management rules and regulations on specific rights and obligations of each department, each institution, and risk management staff at each level, applying a management system separating the functions of front, middle and back offices, defining clearly responsibilities and reporting routes of banking and risk management departments to guarantee the independence of risk management department.	工商银行在风险管理规章制度中明确界定各部门、各级机构和各层级风险管理人员的具体权责，实行前中后台职能相对分离的管理机制，清晰界定业务部门和风险管理部门的职责划分和报告路线，确保风险管理部门的独立性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Departments, domestic and overseas branches and all staffs need to communicate and coordinate effectively one another to optimize the management process and keep improving the management efficiency.	各部门、境内外分支机构和全体员工之间要有效沟通与协调，优化管理流程，不断提高管理效率。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Diversify risks.	（3）风险分散。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC realizes the adequate diversification of credit risk exposure by country, region, industry, product, term and currency in order to prevent concentration risk.	工商银行实现信用风险敞口在国家、地区、行业、产品、期限和币种等维度上的适度分散，防范集中风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In strict compliance with regulatory standards, ICBC is prudent in assessing and deciding credit limits for single and related customers, to effectively control customer credit risk concentration; realizes the adequate diversification of market risk exposure by country, region, market, product, term and currency, and adopts suitable means to diversify market risks effectively; uniformly manages the whole bank’s liquidity, establishes liquidity reserve system at different levels, and guarantees the diversification of financing channels.	严格遵循监管标准，审慎核定单一客户和关联客户授信额度，有效控制客户信用风险集中度；实现市场风险敞口在国家、地区、市场、产品、期限和币种等维度上的适度分散，并采用适当的方式实现市场风险的有效分散；统一管理全行的流动性，建立分层次的流动性储备体系，确保融资渠道的多元化。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(4) Combine both quantitative and qualitative analyses.	（4）定量与定性结合。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC makes efforts to upgrade its risk measurement level, develops risk measurement techniques suitable to business nature, scale and degree of complexity, promotes application of world-wide advanced banks’ mature experience in risk management, and realizes a synthetic combination of both quantitative and qualitative analyses; assesses regularly the reasonableness and effectiveness of measurement model methods and tools, and carries out corresponding validation work; takes stress testing as a key part of risk management, including stress testing of single risk type and integrated stress testing involving two or more risk types. The stress testing covers major risks all business lines face and takes effect of macroeconomic changes on risks into full consideration.	工商银行着力提升风险计量水平，开发与业务性质、规模和复杂程度相适应的风险计量技术，推广应用国际先进银行业成熟的风险管理经验，实现定性分析和定量分析的有机结合；定期评估计量模型的方法和工具的合理性和有效性，开展相应的验证工作；将压力测试作为风险管理的重要组成部分，包括单一风险种类压力测试以及涵盖两种以上风险种类的整合性压力测试，压力测试覆盖各业务条线所面临的主要风险，充分考虑宏观经济变化对风险的影响。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(5) Dynamic adaptability adjustment.	（5）动态适应性调整。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC continuously checks and assesses changes in both internal and external operation management environments and competitive situations as well as their substantive influence on enterprise risk management, and timely adjusts risk management policy, system and process in order to ensure risk management to be consistent with business development strategies.	持续不断地检查和评估内外部经营管理环境和竞争格局的变化及其对全面风险管理所产生的实质性影响，及时调整风险管理政策、制度和流程，以确保风险管理与业务发展战略等相一致。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(6) To be progressive.	（6）循序渐进。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on ICBC’s risk management status, the enterprise risk management framework puts forward development objectives and outlook requirements for future risk management, serving as a guiding document for ICBC in risk management.	全面风险管理框架立足于工商银行风险管理现状，提出了未来风险管理的发展目标和前瞻性要求，是工商银行风险管理的指导性文件。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Elements of enterprise risk management	（三）全面风险管理要素	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Internal environment	1.内部环境	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal environment of ICBC’s risk management is made up of risk management culture, risk appetite, risk management strategy, risk management framework, risk management policy and system and risk management information system, a basis for all elements of risk management.	风险管理文化、风险偏好、风险管理战略、风险治理架构、风险管理政策与制度和风险管理信息系统等构成工商银行风险管理的内部环境，是风险管理所有构成要素的基础。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Target management	2.目标管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A premise for risk management is setting target.	目标设定是风险管理的前提。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Strategic, operating, reporting and compliance targets are key parts of conducting enterprise risk management.	战略目标、经营目标、报告目标和合规目标是实施全面风险管理的重要组成部分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has established a target management responsibility system, performing duty division-based and level-by-level accountability system.	工商银行建立目标管理责任制，实行分工负责制和逐级负责制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Risk management process	3.风险管理流程	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A risk management process refers to an entire process of a series of risk management activities including risk identification, risk measurement, risk control, risk monitoring and reporting. It shall be capable of implementing established strategic targets, and be matched to the Bank’s risk management culture.	风险管理流程是指包括风险识别、风险度量、风险控制、风险监测与报告等一系列风险管理活动的全过程，应能贯彻执行既定的战略目标，与银行风险管理文化相匹配。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Risk management information and communication	4.风险管理信息与沟通	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC builds data warehouse and management information system covering all levels of institutions and business areas, providing varied statistics required by risk management timely and accurately in order to effectively identify, measure and monitor risks.	工商银行建设覆盖各级机构、业务领域的数据仓库和管理信息系统，及时、准确地提供风险管理所需要的各种数据，以实现对风险的有效识别、计量、监测等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
There are four types of communication ways regarding risk management information: top-down vertical communication, bottom-up vertical communication, horizontal communication and external communication.	风险管理信息的沟通方式可分为以下四类：自上而下的纵向沟通、自下而上的纵向沟通、横向沟通与外部沟通。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. Supervision and assessment	5.监督与评价	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC, through continuous monitoring, individual assessment or the combination of the above two, supervises and assesses the effectiveness of risk management.	工商银行通过持续监控、个别评价或者两者结合对风险管理的有效性进行监督与评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Continuous monitoring occurs during a normal process of risk management activity, and individual assessment is a supplementation for the former.	持续监控发生在风险管理活动的正常进程中，个别评价是对持续监控的补充。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
6. Group risk management	6.集团风险管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC implements classification based management on its subsidiaries.	工商银行对附属机构实行分类管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to factors such as business nature, operation scale and management level of those subsidiaries, ICBC implements risk control and management upon them through capital distribution, limit management and differentiated authorization.	根据附属机构的业务属性、经营规模和管理水平等因素，通过资本分配、限额管理、差异化授权等工具，实现对附属机构风险的控制和管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Risk Appetite and Management	二、风险偏好与管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Selecting risk appetite indictors follows those principles mainly:	风险偏好指标选取的原则主要包括:	sample1-en-sample1-zh
first, considering both comprehensiveness and advancedness.	一是兼顾全面性和先进性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Risk appetite shall reflect expectations of major stakeholders of ICBC and cover all substantial risks operation management faces.	风险偏好应反映工商银行主要利益相关人的期望，涵盖经营管理中面临的所有实质性风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC shall consider not only horizontal competitions, consistency with its market position, and keeping boosting its core competence, but also measurement techniques currently taken by ICBC as well as their promotion and application in risk management. ICBC takes the advanced measurement approach under the new Basel capital accord in the calculation of relevant indicators, leading the other banks.	既要考虑同业竞争、与工商银行市场地位相称，不断提升工商银行核心竞争力，又要考虑工商银行当前的计量技术及其在风险管理中的推广应用，在相关指标的测算时，采用了新资本协议实施高级计量方法成果，保持同业先进性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Second, highlighting importance and principles.	二是突出重要性和原则性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Risk appetite shall define important targets and directions needing long-term persistence with a focus on highlighting core and key indicators that shall not alter frequently.	风险偏好重在明晰需长期坚持的重要目标、方向，重点突出核心指标、关键指标，不宜频繁调整。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Risk appetite indicators, concise but to the point, are not only convenient to grasp substantial issues, but also flexible to accustom to development requirements.	简明扼要的风险偏好指标，既便于抓住实质问题，又便于灵活适应发展需要。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For those important operation management concepts and principles long-time accumulated by ICBC, they need to be further exacted and clarified in risk appetite.	对于工商银行长期积累的重要经营管理理念、原则，在风险偏好中予以进一步提炼和明确。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Setting risk appetite is a process balancing and coordinating the relationship among capital, return and risk.	风险偏好的设定是一个平衡协调资本、收益和风险三者之间关系的过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Therefore, ICBC’s risk appetite indicators primarily include capital indictors, return indicators and zero-tolerance indicators, which reflect expectations of major stakeholders of ICBC and cover main risks ICBC faces in the operation.	因此，工商银行风险偏好指标主要包括资本类指标、收益类指标、风险类指标及零容忍度类指标，反映工商银行主要利益相关人的期望，并覆盖工商银行经营中面临的主要风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Risk Management Assessment	三、风险管理评价	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Classification	（一）银行风险管理评价的分类	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A bank’s risk management assessment includes internal and external risk management assessments at a bank.	银行风险管理评价包括银行内部风险管理评价和外部风险管理评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal risk management assessment is required for keeping enhancing its risk management level, while external risk management assessment reflects acknowledgement of outside agencies about a bank’s risk management status, which can be used by a bank to perfect its risk management.	进行内部风险管理评价是不断提升自身风险管理水平的需要，而外部评价则反映了外部机构对银行风险管理现状的认识，可以作为银行完善其风险管理的参考。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Purposes	（二）风险管理评价的目的	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Risk management assessment has two purposes mainly.	风险管理评价的目的主要有两种。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. To ensure the effectiveness of risk management	1.保证风险管理有效性	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Enterprise Risk Management- Integrated Framework released by COSO includes eight major elements, among them, monitoring has pointed out clearly that, a bank needs to monitor risk management and assess the existence and operation of risk management elements.	COSO委员会公布的《企业风险管理－整合框架》中包含八个要素，其中“监控”要素明确指出，要对风险管理进行监控，对其构成要素的存在和运行情况进行评估。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Assessment on risk management, mentioned by it, primarily aims to guaranteeing the effectiveness of risk management assessed.	其中所提到的“对风险管理进行评估”，主要目的就是为了保证被评估者风险管理的有效性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. To provide reference for commercial decisions	2.为商业决策提供参考	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to provide reference for investment or other commercial decisions, it is required to make a comprehensive assessment of the institution assessed. An assessment by external rating companies that has been introduced briefly before belongs to such assessment.	为了给投资或其他商业决策提供参考，需要对被评价机构进行综合全面的评估，之前已经简单介绍银行面临的外部评级公司的评价就属于这类评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In most cases, risk management assessment is a part of total one, how much it accounts for differs greatly due to different assessment objectives and objects.	在大多数情况下，风险管理评价是整个评估的组成部分，其所占的比重由于评价的目的和对象的不同而有很大差异。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Such assessment results mainly serve some stakeholders of assessed institutions, for example, their investors and creditors. Those stakeholders need to learn assessed institutions’ risk management status through assessment, and accordingly obtain information as reference for commercial decisions.	该类评价的结果主要服务于被评价对象的一些利益相关者，例如被评价者的投资者、债权人等，这些利益相关者需要通过评价了解被评价对象的风险管理状况，从而获得作出商业决策的参考信息。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Contents	（三）银行风险管理评价的内容	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For a bank, risk management involves all sides of operation management, and is a continuous and dynamic process.	对于银行来讲，风险管理涉及到经营管理的各个方面，是一个持续的、动态的过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To comprehensively assess risk management, it needs to assess not only the management process but also the management outcomes.	要对风险管理进行全面的评价，既要对管理过程进行评价，也要对管理结果进行评估。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Of them, risk management process is “what have been done, and how”, while risk management outcome indicates “what about the effect”, which constitutes two basic classifications of risk management assessment indicators.	其中风险管理过程是“做了什么、怎么做的”，而风险管理结果体现的是“效果如何”，这构成了风险管理评价指标的两个基本分类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
When designing a specific risk management assessment system, appropriate adjustment shall be made to the percentages that risk management process and outcomes take in line with the designer’s purpose.	在制定具体的风险管理评价体系时，要根据制定者的意图，对风险管理过程和结果所占的比例进行合适的调整。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IV. Risk Reports and Requirements for Preparation	四、风险报告及编制要求	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Regulatory requirements on risk reports	（一）风险报告的监管要求	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Objectively, the implementation of the New Basel Capital Accord requires the banking industry to enhance its risk management level, and strengthen its forecasting and analysis ability.	《巴塞尔新资本协议》的实施，客观上要求银行业提升风险管理水平，加强预测分析能力。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Quantative analysis reports on risks with different styles and contents shall be made corresponding to different risk management level in credit, market, and operation risks.	在信用风险、市场风险和操作风险方面都要针对不同的风险管理水平进行不同风格、内容的风险定量分析报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A bank’ risks report is an important way to improve its own risk management level.	银行的风险报告是银行提升自身风险管理水平的重要手段之一。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Risk report contents	（二）风险报告内容	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Risk reports have diversified forms and contents. A risk reporting system which is rich in content and varied in form may be produced based on different management requirements.	风险报告的形式和内容是多种多样的，根据不同的管理需要，可以形成形式各异、内容丰富的风险报告体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Comprehensive risk reporting system	1.全面风险报告体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It is a synthetic report reflecting various substantial risks ICBC faces in operation management during a reporting period, including such report types as enterprise risk management report, risk and ICAAP report, integrative stress testing report, risk appetite implementation report and country risk management report.	综合反映工商银行报告期内经营管理所面临的各类实质性风险状况，包括以下报告类别：全面风险管理报告、风险及资本充足评估（ICAAP）报告、整合性压力测试报告、风险偏好执行情况报告、国别风险管理报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Classified risk reporting system	2.分类风险报告体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It reflects the profile of a certain type of risk ICBC faces in operation management during a reporting period.	反映工商银行报告期内经营管理所面临的某一类风险状况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Credit risk reporting system, which reflects the credit risk status ICBC faces in operation management during a reporting period.	（1）信用风险报告体系。 反映工商银行报告期内经营管理所面临的信用风险状况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC is constructing and gradually perfecting an internal ratings-based credit risk reporting system, including credit risk management report, credit risk measurement report and credit risk stress testing report.	工商银行建立并逐步完善基于内部评级法的信用风险报告体系，包括信用风险管理报告、信用风险计量报告、信用风险压力测试报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Market risk reporting system, which reflects the market risk status ICBC faces in operation management during a reporting period.	（2）市场风险报告体系。 反映工商银行报告期内经营管理所面临的市场风险状况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC is constructing and gradually perfecting an internal models-based market risk reporting system, including market risk management report, market risk measurement report and market risk stress testing report.	工商银行建立并逐步完善基于内部模型法的市场风险报告体系，包括市场风险管理报告、市场风险计量报告、市场风险压力测试报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Operational risk reporting system, which reflects the operational risk status faced by ICBC in operation management during a reporting period.	（3）操作风险报告体系。 反映工商银行报告期内经营管理所面临的操作风险状况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC is constructing and gradually perfecting an advanced measurement approach-based operational risk reporting system, including operational risk management report, operational risk measurement report and operational risk stress testing report (which will be elaborated on in Section Five of this chapter).	工商银行建立并逐步完善基于高级法的操作风险报告体系，包括操作风险管理报告、操作风险计量报告、操作风险压力测试报告（在本章第五节会有具体阐述）。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(4) Liquidity risk reporting system, which reflects the liquidity risk status faced by ICBC in operation management during a reporting period, including liquidity risk management report and liquidity risk stress testing report.	（4）流动性风险报告体系。 反映工商银行报告期内经营管理所面临的流动性风险状况，包括流动性风险管理报告、流动性风险压力测试报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(5) Reports on other types of risks, which reflect the status of other substantial risks contained in the new capital accord, including reputational risk, strategic risk, concentration risk and asset securitization risk.	（5）其他类型风险报告。 反映新资本协议包含的其他实质性风险状况，包括声誉风险、战略风险、集中度风险、资产证券化风险等报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(6) Risk profile report, which adopts data statements to reflect risk profile, including ICBC risk profile statement and statements on ICBC’s credit risk, market risk, operational risk and liquidity risk.	（6）风险状况报告。 采用数据报表形式反映风险状况，包括中国工商银行风险状况表以及中国工商银行信用风险、市场风险、操作风险和流动性风险明细表。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In general, risk profile report is a part of enterprise risk management report, which can also be reported separately.	风险状况报告一般作为全面风险管理报告的组成部分，也可单独报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Definitions and calculation formulas of risk indicators are adopted according to existing regulatory requirements and ICBC’s statistical system.	风险指标定义及计算公式按照现行监管要求和工商银行统计制度执行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Themed risk management reports	3.专题风险管理报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
They focus on risk profile of a certain area such as region, industry, customer and product.	重点反映地区、行业、客户、产品等某一领域的风险状况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In principle, the items subject to themed risk management reports are determined by the Risk Management Committee or professional risk management committee.	专题风险管理报告项目原则上由风险管理委员会或专业风险管理委员会确定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Major unexpected risk event report	4.重大突发风险事件报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It reports in time on major unexpected risk events occurred in ICBC, reflecting facts, analyzing reasons, assessing losses, summarizing lessons and making suggestions on risk management improvement.	及时报告工商银行发生的重大突发风险事件，包括反映事件事实、分析事件成因、评估损失影响、总结吸取教训和提出风险管理改进建议。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Major unexpected risk event scope and reporting requirements are based on relevant regulations of ICBC.	重大突发风险事件范围和报告要求按照行内相关规定执行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
V. Risk and ICAAP Management	五、风险及资本充足评估管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Assessment on substantial risks	（一）实质性风险评估	sample1-en-sample1-zh
There are two approaches to assess substantial risks.	实质性风险评估的方法主要有两大类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
One of them is that a bank, with “scoring card”, assesses the risk levels and risk management quality (including governance, risk management framework and internal control) as well as stress testing and capital intensity of various substantial risks, and gets the capital requirement taking all substantial risks into consideration on the basis of assessment.	其中一类是银行通过打分卡的方法，对各实质性风险的风险水平和风险管理质量（包括治理、风险管理框架和内部控制）以及压力测试、资本强度等方面进行评估，并在评估的基础上得出考虑所有实质性风险的资本要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The other is mainly implementing the Pillar II through economic capital.	另一类银行主要通过经济资本的方法来实施第二支柱。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In areas where the new capital accord has been implemented, including banks in the Europe and Australia, economic capital is a major tool used for assessing risks.	在已实施新资本协议的地区，包括欧洲和澳洲的银行，经济资本是这些银行用于评估风险的主要工具。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To be more accurate, the most initial and primary purpose of those banks to build and perform an economic capital model is not to meet regulatory requirements, but to meet banks’ internal management needs, including calculation of return on capital after risk adjustment as well as related performance assessment.	更准确地说，这些银行建立和实施经济资本模型的最初和最主要目的不是为了落实监管要求，而是为了满足银行的内部管理需要，包括计算风险调节后的资本回报率及相关的业绩考核等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Capital adequacy forecast	（二）资本充足预测	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Purpose	1.资本充足预测的目的	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Forecasting capital adequacy aims to, under the continuous changes in operational scale and risk profile, guarantee a bank to be able to maintain its capital adequacy level above the minimum capital adequacy ratio obtained from risk assessment.	资本充足预测的目的是为了确保银行在不断变化的业务经营规模和风险轮廓下，资本充足水平能维持在银行风险评估得出的最低资本充足比率之上。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
From the perspectives of regulation and risk management, capital may be used for absorbing possible non-expected losses.	从监管和风险管理角度来看，资本用于吸收可能发生的非预期损失。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Therefore, given all other conditions unchanged, the more capital a bank has, the safer the bank is.	因此，其他条件保持不变，银行持有的资本越多，银行越安全。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
But from the perspective of operation management, capital is a kind of expensive and limited resource.	但是，从经营管理角度来看，资本是一种昂贵且有限的资源。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
So, holding more capitals means operating costs are higher, reducing return on capital of stakeholders.	因此，持有较多的资本意味较高的经营成本并会降低利益相关者的资本回报率。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Under the framework of ICAAP, banks need to be prudent in assessing various substantial risks, and continuously keep a capital level consistent with the risk profile (or capital adequacy ratio), based on which banks conduct effective forecasting on capital adequacy ratios to ensure that they may consecutively satisfy target capital adequacy ratio requirements when preparing and carrying out business operation and risk management plans.	ICAAP 框架下，银行审慎评估各类实质性风险，并持续保持与银行风险状况相适应的资本水平（即资本充足率）。 在此基础上，银行开展有效的资本充足率预测以确保银行在制定和实施业务经营规划和风险管理规划时可以持续地满足目标资本充足率要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Typically, banks make forecasting on capital adequacy ratios in the next three years.	银行一般对未来3年的资本充足率进行预测。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Relationship between capital adequacy ratio forecasting process and business planning process	2.资本充足率预测流程和业务规划流程的关系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Capital management plays an important role in business planning and operational orientation. Banks shall assess and analyze each detailed business planning item as the following:	资本管理对业务规划和经营的导向有重要作用，应对每个业务规划细项进行下述评估和分析：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Effect on risk profile, and further effect on capital demand;	——对风险状况的影响，进而对资本需求的影响；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Effect on income growth, and further effect on capital supply; and	——对收益增长的影响，进而对资本供给的影响；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Assess and analyze the amount of distributable capital.	——评估并分析可分配的资本数额。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Composition The main purpose of capital adequacy ratio foresting is to understand effect of a bank’s operation and strategic development planning on its capital, and maintain an appropriate level of capital adequacy.	3.资本充足率预测的构成 资本充足率预测主要目的是理解银行经营和战略发展规划对资本的影响，保持资本充足的适当水平。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Forecasting on capital adequacy ratio is primarily based on the regulatory capital and total risk-weighted asset forecasting.	预测资本充足率预测主要基于对监管资本的预测和对总风险加权资产的预测。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Regulatory capital forecasting includes that on the following items:	对监管资本的预测包括对下列细项的预测：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Table 2-1 Items under Regulatory Capital Forecasting	表2-1 监管资本的预测细则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Category	大类	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Item	细项	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Core capital	核心资本	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Paid-in capital	· 实收资本	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Capital reserve	· 资本公积	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Surplus reserves (incl. statutory surplus reserve and discretionary surplus reserve)	· 盈余公积（包括法定盈余公积、任意盈余公积）	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· General reserve	· 一般准备	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Retained profits	· 未分配利润	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Minority equity	· 少数股权	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Deduction: goodwill, etc.	· 扣减项：商誉等	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Supplementary capital	附属资本	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Revaluation reserve	· 重估储备	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· 50% of unrealized net gain due to changes in fair value of available-for-sale equity and bond financial assets	· 可供出售的股权类、债券类金融资产的公允价值变动形成的未实现净利得的50％	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· 50% of unrealized net gain due to changes in fair value of hedging tool and hedged items in an effective part of cash flow hedging	· 现金流套期有效部分中的套期工具和被套期项目公允价值变动形成的净利得的50％	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Unrealized net gain due to changes in fair value of financial instrument for trading (after-tax)	· 交易性金融工具公允价值变动形成的未实现净利得(考虑税收影响后)	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Allowance for excess impairment losses	· 超额减值准备	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Preferred shares	· 优先股	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Convertible bond	· 可转换债券	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Hybrid debt capital tool	· 混合债务资本工具	sample1-en-sample1-zh
· Long-term subordinated debt	· 长期次级债务	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Total risk-weighted assets are equal to the sum of credit risk-weighted, operational risk-weighted and market risk-weighted assets.	总风险加权资产等于信用风险加权资产、操作风险加权资产以及市场风险加权资产的总和。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Currently, ICBC is applying the prevailing approach for calculating credit risk-weighted assets, and the standardized approach for calculating both operational risk-weighted and market risk-weighted assets.	工商银行目前使用现行法计算信用风险加权资产，使用标准法计算操作风险加权资产，以及使用标准法计算市场风险加权资产。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After the implementation of new capital accord, the foundation IRB approach, the standardized approach of market risk and the standardized approach of operational risk will be applied for calculating various risk-weighted assets, respectively.	在新资本协议实施后，将采用内部评级初级法、市场风险标准法和操作风险标准法来分别计算各类风险的风险加权资产。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To majority commercial banks, credit risk is the largest one of total risk-weighted assets.	信用风险对于大多数商业银行而言，是总风险加权资产中最大的一项。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If a forecasting on credit risk-weighted assets is based on internal ratings-based approach, a quantitative growth and quality improvement of assets shall be taken into consideration.	信用风险加权资产的预测如果基于内部评级法，应考虑量的增长以及资产质量的变化。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
At present, credit risk is the largest one faced by commercial banks in China which focus on lending business.	信用风险是当前以信贷业务为主的中国商业银行所面临的最大风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Operational risk is relatively a stable one for banks.	操作风险对银行来说是相对稳定的风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
There is a higher probability of operational risk to occur primarily due to imperfect rules and regulations, lack of experience in operation by staffs, and possible shortcomings in management at the time when new business gets started or new system goes alive; when new business and system gradually become mature, rules and regulations are improved, and staff get experienced in operation, operational risk becomes less frequent.	主要因为在新业务开展或新系统上线时，由于规章制度不完善、员工操作经验不足、管理上可能存在的漏洞，此时操作风险出现的概率较高；而随着新业务和新系统的逐渐成熟，规章制度的逐步完善，员工的操作经验也会日渐丰富，这就使得操作风险发生的频率降低。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Therefore, the measurement results of operational risk-weighted assets in terms of banks’ current operational status have been stablized.	因此，就银行目前运营状态而言，对操作风险加权资产的计量结果已相对稳定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Market risk exposure position change is mainly subject to market factors such as interest rate, exchange rate, and stock price; it is also affected by factors such as front-office dealer’s personal judgment on trends.	市场风险暴露头寸的变化主要受利率、汇率、股价等市场因子的影响，同时也会受到前台交易人员对趋势的个人判断等因素影响。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Therefore, it is relatively difficult to forecast changes in market risk position.	因此，市场风险头寸的变动相对更难以预测。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
