So, regarding the methodology of capital adequacy ratio forecasting, because credit risk produces greater effect on banks’ future capital requirement, a more complicated forecasting method will be used to credit risk-weighted assets growth compared with market risk and operational risk ones.	因此，在资本充足率预测方法论中，由于信用风险对银行未来的资本需求的影响更大，对信用风险加权资产增长的预测将使用比市场风险和操作风险更复杂的预测方法。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VI. Country Risk Management	六、国别风险管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Country risk overview	（一）国别风险简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In 2010, CBRC issued the Guidelines for Country Risk Management of Banking Financial Institutions (Y.J.F. [2010] No.45), in which country risk is defined as the risk that results to the borrower or debtor in the country or region where its economy, politics and society gets change and undergoes relevant events is incapable of or refuses to pay the debt to banking financial institution, or causes the commercial interest of banking financial institution to suffer the loss in the country or region, or causes banking financial institution to experience other losses.	我国银监会于2010年颁布了《银行业金融机构国别风险管理指引》（银监发[2010]45号），将国别风险定义为由于某一国家或地区经济、政治、社会变化及事件，导致该国家或地区借款人或债务人没有能力或者拒绝偿付银行业金融机构债务，或使银行业金融机构在该国家或地区的商业存在遭受损失，或使银行业金融机构遭受其他损失的风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To meet regulatory requirements, ICBC later issued the Management Measures for Country Risk Ratings of Industrial and Commercial Bank of China (Tentative).	根据监管要求，工商银行随后颁布了《中国工商银行国别风险评级管理办法（试行）》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Country risk classification	（二）国别风险分类	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to CBRC’s Guidelines for Country Risk Management of Banking Financial Institutions (Y.J.F. [2010] No.45), country risk can be classified into seven categories, namely, transfer risk, sovereign risk, contagion risk, currency risk, macroeconomic risk, political risk and indirect country risk.	根据银监会《银行业金融机构国别风险管理指引》（银监发[2010]45号），国别风险可以分为7类，即转移风险、主权风险、传染风险、货币风险、宏观经济风险、政治风险、间接国别风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Country risk rating	（三）国别风险评级	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to strengthen country risk management, and regulate country risk rating, ICBC enacted the Management Measures for Country Risk Ratings of Industrial and Commercial Bank of China (Tentative), according to CBRC’s Guidelines for Country Risk Management of Banking Financial Institutions (Y.J.F. [2010] No.45) and ICBC’s Consolidated Management Measures (G.Y.F. [2009] No.72), and other relevant laws and regulations.	为加强国别风险管理，规范国别风险评级，根据银监会《银行业金融机构国别风险管理指引》（银监发[2010] 45号）和工商银行《并表管理办法》（工银发[2009]72号）以及相关法律法规，工商银行制定了《中国工商银行国别风险评级管理办法（试行）》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Rating subject	1.评级对象	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Subjects of country risk rating are countries or regions doing business or possibly doing business with ICBC as well as countries or regions that will likely to produce indirect significant effect on ICBC’s operation yet they have no business contact with ICBC now.	国别风险评级对象为与工商银行有业务往来或可能与之开展业务往来的国家或地区，以及虽与工商银行没有业务往来，但可能对工商银行业务造成间接重大影响的国家或地区。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Countries or regions refer to different jurisdictions or economies.	国家或地区指不同的司法管辖区或经济体。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Rating principles	2.评级原则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Comprehensiveness.	(1)全面性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Rating shall consider comprehensively various risks that may bring losses to ICBC’s operation in this country or region, such as transfer, sovereign, contagion, currency, macroeconomic, political and indirect country risks.	评级应全面考察可能给工商银行在该国家或地区的业务带来损失的各类风险，包括转移风险、主权风险、传染风险、货币风险、宏观经济风险、政治风险以及间接国别风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Objectivity.	(2)客观性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Country risk rating needs to be independent from Banking departments.	国别风险评级独立于业务办理部门。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Employees shall conduct country risk rating with scientific, objective and fair attitude, truly reflecting risk status of each subject rated.	评级人员以科学、客观、公正的态度进行国别风险评级，真实反映各评级对象的风险状况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Integrity.	(3)整体性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Country risk rating needs an integrated inspection on all factors in this country or region such as political, economic and social ones, systematically reflecting overall risk status of the country or region.	国别风险应综合考察该国或地区政治、经济、社会等各方面因素，系统反映国家或地区总体风险状况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(4) Importance.	(4)重要性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Country risk rating shall cover all countries or regions to which ICBC has significant risk exposures with rating system needing to be consistent with ICBC’s country risk exposure size and complexity.	国别风险评级应覆盖工商银行所有重大风险暴露所处的国家和地区，评级体系应与工商银行国别风险暴露规模和复杂程度相适应。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Significant country risk exposure refers to a risk exposure above 25% of ICBC’s net capital with regard to one country or region.	重大国别风险暴露是指对单一国家或地区超过工商银行净资本25%的风险暴露。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Rating indicators	3.评级指标	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A rating indicators system includes six aspects: economic environment; financial environment; international balance of payment & foreign debt level; political and diplomatic environment; system operating environment; and social security environment, their weights in comprehensive country risk rating scores are 20%, 25%, 20% , 15%, 15% and 5%, respectively.	评级指标体系分为经济环境、金融环境、国际收支及外债水平、政治外交环境、制度运营环境、社会安全环境六个方面，在国家风险综合评价得分中的权重依次为20％、25％、20％、15％、15％和5％。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Table 2-2 Country Risk Rating Indicators System	表2-2 国别风险评级指标体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Indicator	指标类型	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Rating content	评价内容	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Economic environment	经济环境	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Economic growth rate, pattern and sustainability; inflation rate; employment; pillar industries; economic exposure to other countries or regions.	经济增长水平、模式和可持续性，通货膨胀水平，就业情况，支柱产业状况，经济受其他国家或地区问题影响的程度等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Financial environment	金融环境	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Money supply; interest rate; foreign exchange rate; government financial situation; whether it is an international financial center; major market functions; completeness of financial market infrastructures and regulatory capacity; development level of financial system; financial system leverage ratio and stability of funding source; matching degree of financial development with real economy; growth of banking system and private sector loan growth.	货币供应量，利率，汇率，政府财政状况，是否为国际金融中心，主要市场功能、金融市场基础设施完备程度和监管能力，金融系统发达程度，金融系统杠杆率和资金来源稳定性，金融发展与实体经济匹配性，银行体系增长情况，私人部门信贷增长情况等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
International balance of payment and foreign debit level	国际收支及外债水平	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Current account status and stability; inflows of foreign capital; foreign exchange reserve size; foreign debit structure, size and solvency.	经常账户状况和稳定性，国外资本流入情况，外汇储备规模，外债结构、规模和偿债能力等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Political and diplomatic environment	政治外交环境	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Political stability; political force balance; form of government maturity; geopolitics and diplomatic relations.	政治稳定性，政治力量平衡性，政体成熟程度，地缘政治与外交关系状况等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
System operating environment	制度运营环境	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Legal system; investment policy; compliance with international laws, as well as business, accounting and financial regulatory standards; information transparency; governmental willingness and ability in modifying economic and budget problems.	法律体系，投资政策，遵守国际法律、商业、会计和金融监管等标准情况，以及信息透明度，政府纠正经济及预算问题的意愿和能力等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Social security environment	社会安全环境	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Social civilization level and cultural traditions; religious and ethnic conflicts; terrorist activities; other social problems, including but not limited to criminal and public security, natural conditions and other disasters.	社会文明程度和文化传统，宗教民族矛盾，恐怖主义活动，其他社会问题，包括但不限于犯罪和治安状况、自然条件和自然灾害、疾病瘟疫等。 4.评级管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Rating management	（1）评级流程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Rating process: country risk rating mainly includes initiation, examination, identification, overthrowing and updating.	国别风险评级流程主要包括评级发起、评级审查、评级认定、评级推翻和评级更新。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After country risk rating has been completed, if there happens an event needing re-rating in a certain country or region, updating is required to be finished within 30 days.	在国别风险评级完成后，若某国或地区发生需要进行重新评级的事件时，应在30天内完成评级更新。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Rating agency.	（2）评级机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Risk Management Department of the Head Office is responsible for conducting country risk ratings.	总行风险管理部负责组织开展国别风险评级工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Expert Review Panel for Country Risk Rating of the Head Office is responsible for examining and overthrowing the scores based on country risk rating indicators and initial results.	总行国别风险评级专家审查小组负责对国别风险评级的指标得分和初评结果进行审查和推翻。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Risk Management Committee of the Head Office is responsible for finalizing annual country risk rating levels.	总行风险管理委员会负责年度国别风险等级的最终审定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Each country risk rating application department and overseas branch shall assist the he Risk Management Department of the Head Office in monitoring country risk ratings.	各国别风险评级应用部门和各境外分支机构协助总行风险管理部做好国别风险评级监测工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iv. Country risk exposure	（四）国别风险敞口	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Definition and types	1.国别风险敞口定义及类型	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Country risk exposure is the maximum risk exposure of ICBC’s all business activities in the country risk.	国别风险敞口，是指工商银行各项业务经营活动在国别风险中的最大风险暴露。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The business types of ICBC’s country risk exposure include but not limited to such business activities as loans, trade finance, letter of guarantee & commitment, bills, bonds, foreign exchange, placements, financial derivatives, transfers between correspondent banks, overseas leasing, setup of overseas institutions, overseas strategic investment, reorganization and M&A, overseas equity investment, and outsourcing services provided by overseas service providers.	工商银行国别风险敞口的业务类型包括但不限于：贷款、贸易融资、保函及承诺函、票据、债券、外汇、资金拆放、金融衍生业务、代理行往来、境外租赁、设立境外机构、境外战略投资和重组并购、境外股权投资、以及由境外服务提供商提供的外包服务等经营活动。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Statistical rules	2.国别风险敞口的统计规则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Country risk exposure statistics are made at the group and corporate levels.	国别风险敞口统计包括集团和法人两个层面。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Group-based statistical rule.	集团口径统计规则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The institutions under the group approach shall be the same with ICBC’s consolidated management institutions, including the Head Office, domestic and overseas branches, domestic and overseas affiliates, and domestic and overseas subsidiaries. Business operational activities that have country risks of these institutions are all included into the Group’s country risk exposure statistics.	集团口径的机构范围与工商银行并表管理机构保持一致，具体包括：总行本部、境内外分行、境内外子行、境内外附属机构，这些机构存在国别风险的业务经营活动均纳入集团国别风险敞口统计范围。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Single corporate-based statistical rule.	单一法人口径统计规则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The institutions under the single corporate approach (i.e. Industrial and Commercial Bank of China Limited) include the Head Office, domestic and overseas branches. Business operational activities exposed to country risks of these institutions are included into the corporate’s country risk exposure statistics.	单一法人口径（指中国工商银行股份有限公司）的机构范围包括：总行本部、境内外分行，这些机构存在国别风险的业务经营活动纳入法人国别风险敞口统计范围。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office enters the amount of investment in domestic and overseas affiliates, subsidiaries and shareholding institutions into the exposure statistics as “Equity Investment”, respectively.	总行对境内外子行、附属机构和参股机构的投资入股金额分别以“股权投资”进入敞口统计范围。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
v. Country limit	（五）国别限额	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Definition and classification	1.国别限额定义及分类	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Country limit refers to the upper limit set by ICBC to the country risk exposure of a particular country or region.	国别限额，是指某一国家或某些国家的累计国别风险敞口的上限。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Here, country risk exposure refers to the final risk exposure after risks have been transferred. Exposure amount and country to which risks are exposed are determined by ICBC’s country risk exposure statistical system.	此处国别风险敞口指风险转移后的最终风险敞口，敞口金额及敞口所在国家按照工商银行国别风险敞口统计制度确定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Country limit can be divided into whole bank’s total country limit, regional country limit and single country risk limit.	国别限额可分为全行国别总限额、区域国别限额和单一国别限额等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The whole bank’s total country limit is the one for a maximum total country risk exposure that ICBC is willing to take.	全行国别总限额为工商银行愿意承担的最大国别风险总敞口的限额。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A regional country limit is the one for a country risk exposure to a certain region, normally represented by a percentage of regional country risk exposure accounting for the whole bank’s total country limit.	区域国别限额为某一区域内的国别风险敞口限额，通常以区域国别风险敞口占全行国别风险总敞口的比重的形式表示。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Single country risk exposure ceiling is the maximum value among all single country limits.	单一国家风险敞口上限为所有单一国别限额的最大值。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Limit setting Country limit is mainly decided by country risk, business opportunity and country (region) importance.	2.国别限额的设定方法 国别限额主要依据国别风险、业务机会和国家（地区）重要性三个因素确定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Of three, business opportunity represents volume of business that ICBC may deal with in a certain country. Country (region) importance refers to the importance of ICBC’s business in this country relative to ICBC’s overall development strategies and business income.	其中业务机会表示工商银行在某国可能的业务量相对大小，国家（地区）重要性是指工商银行在该国业务对工商银行整体发展战略、经营收益的相对重要性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Business opportunity is associated with this country (region)’s economic scale and its bilateral trade relationship with China. Country (region) importance is related to ICBC’s development strategies. Both do not consider country (region) risk.	业务机会与国家（地区）经济规模以及与中国的双边经贸往来有关，国家（地区）重要性与工商银行发展战略有关，两者均不考虑国家（地区）风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Country (region) importance	3.国家（地区）重要性	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The countries (regions) are divided into three types: core strategic importance, prior development and general based on their importance to the Bank’s international strategy, market distribution, profit growth and international influence.	按照各国家和地区对工商银行国际化战略、市场布局、利润增长、国际影响等方面的重要性，将其分为核心战略类、重点发展类、一般类三类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The countries (regions) of core strategic importance are the countries and regions that have great contribution to the Bank’s profit or non-monetary benefit, that the Bank plans to make access to or those that have an importance influence on the Bank’s international reputation; the countries (regions) of prior development are the countries (regions) less important than the countries (regions) of core strategic importance, including the countries and regions that have frequent business exchanges with the Bank, those that play an important role in the Bank’s business development or those that have a great potential of business growth; and the countries (regions) classified as general are the countries and regions other than the those of core strategic importance and prior development.	核心战略类国家（地区）是影响工商银行国际化战略实施、对工商银行利润或非货币收益贡献巨大、工商银行拟重点进入、或对工商银行国际声誉具有重要影响的国家和地区；重点发展类国家（地区）是重要性低于核心战略类的国家（地区），包括与工商银行有经常性的业务往来、对工商银行业务发展具有重要作用，或具有较大业务增长潜力的国家和地区；一般类国家（地区）是除核心战略类和重点发展类以外的国家和地区。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Five Internal Control and Compliance Management	第五节 内部控制与合规管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Internal Control	一、内部控制	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal control work at ICBC is subject to two major regulatory documents. One is the Guidelines for Internal Control of Commercial Banks issued by CBRC in 2007, which introduced the overall framework standards of the Committee of Sponsoring Organizations of the Treadway Commission (COSO) into China’s banking industry. The other is the Basic Standard for Enterprise Internal Control jointly issued by the Ministry of Finance, National Audit Office, CBRC, CSRC and China Insurance Regulatory Commission in June 2008, supplemented by the Supporting Guidelines for Enterprise Internal Control released in April 2010.	工商银行内部控制工作所遵循的主要监管法规有以下两部：一是2007年银监会发布的《商业银行内部控制指引》，将COSO（Committee of Sponsoring Organizations of the Treadway Commission）整体框架标准引入我国银行业；二是2008年6月，财政部、审计署、银监会、证监会、保监会等五部委联合发布的《企业内部控制基本规范》，以及于2010年4月发布的《企业内部控制配套指引》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Definition, objective and principles of internal control	（一）内部控制的定义、目标与原则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In accordance with relevant regulations, ICBC defines internal control as a process aimed at achieving control objectives and implemented by the Board of Directors, the Board of Supervisors, Senior Management and all employees.	根据监管法规，工商银行将内部控制定义为由我行董事会、监事会、高级管理层和全体员工实施的、旨在实现控制目标的过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The objective of internal control is to provide reasonable assurance regarding the compliance of operation and management, safety of assets, authenticity and completeness of financial reports and relevant information, enhanced effectiveness and efficiency of operation and fulfillment of corporate development strategy.	内部控制的目标是为经营管理合法合规、资产安全、财务报告及相关信息真实完整、提高经营效率和效果、促进企业实现发展战略提供合理保证。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal control development and implementation follows five principles, namely, completeness, materiality, check and balance, adaptability and cost effectiveness.	内部控制建设与实施遵循全面性、重要性、制衡性、适应性和成本效益五项原则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Elements of the internal control system of ICBC	（二）工商银行内部控制体系的构成要素	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal control system of ICBC comprises five elements, namely, internal environment, risk assessment, control activities, internal supervision, and information and communication.	工商银行内部控制体系包括五大要素，即内部环境、风险评估、控制活动、内部监督、信息与沟通。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Internal environment	1.内部环境	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal environment, as the foundation for internal control implementation, generally includes corporate governance structure, organizational structure setup, distribution of powers and responsibilities, internal audit, human resource policy and corporate culture.	内部环境是实施内部控制的基础，一般包括公司治理结构、组织机构设置及权责分配，内部审计、人力资源政策、企业文化等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Heads of internal organizations and departments of ICBC concurrently perform duties of business management and internal control management, i.e. dual duties for one post, directly responsible for internal control of their respective organizations or departments.	工商银行内部各机构、各部门负责人同时履行业务管理和内部控制管理职责，即一岗双责，对本机构、本部门的内部控制负直接责任。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC set up an internal control compliance department at each of the Head Office, domestic tier-one branch (branch directly controlled by the Head Office) and tier-two branch levels, charged with leading and coordinating the establishment and implementation of internal controls, carrying out internal control assessment of domestic tier-one (immediate) branches or lower levels and reporting to the Management at the corresponding level. Internal audit bureaus and sub-bureaus, set up in a vertically management mode, are accountable and report to the Board of Directors on their activities, take the lead in group-wide internal control assessment and assist in external disclosure of the internal control assessment report.	工商银行在总行、境内一级（直属）分行和二级分行设立内控合规部门，负责牵头组织协调内部控制的建立实施，开展境内一级（直属）分行及以下机构内控评价工作，并向本级行管理层报告；设立垂直管理的内部审计局及内审分局，对董事会负责并报告工作，履行集团层面内部控制评价工作的牵头职责，协助完成内部控制评价报告的对外披露。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Risk assessment	2.风险评估	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has developed the risk management strategy and objectives and defined the risk tolerance, maintaining close monitoring of internal and external risk-generating factors. Risk assessment procedures, standards and methods have been established and improved to analyze and sequence identified risks according to the possibility and impact of risks, so as to determine the priority list of risk controls. With the risk-return balance considered, risks are effectively controlled by using a range of response tactics, including risk avoidance, risk mitigation, risk sharing and risk taking.	工商银行制定了风险管理战略和目标，确定风险承受度，密切关注产生风险的各类内外部因素；建立健全风险评估的程序、标准和方法，按照风险发生的可能性及其影响程度等，对识别的风险进行分析和排序，确定关注重点和优先控制的风险；权衡风险与收益，综合运用风险规避、风险降低、风险分担和风险承受等应对策略，实现对风险的有效控制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition, ICBC also prepares different levels and types of risk reports at such frequency, within such scope and according to such procedures as laid down in relevant documents, so as to meet the diverse needs of all institutions and departments regarding the risk profile.	此外，工商银行还编制不同层次和种类风险报告，按照制度规定的报告发送范围、程序和频率，以满足各机构、各部门对风险状况的多样性需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Control activities	3.控制活动	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to its internal control objectives and risk response tactics, ICBC uses an array of control measures to effectively control various activities and matters by combining manual control with automatic control, and combining preventive control with reactive control.	工商银行根据内部控制目标，结合风险应对策略，通过手工控制与系统控制、预防性控制与发现性控制相结合的方法，综合运用控制措施，对各种业务和事项实施有效控制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Control measures generally include control over policies and processes, control over segregation of incompatible posts, authority and approval control, accounting system control, property protection control, budget control, operation and management analysis control, performance assessment control, emergency response control, product innovation control, anti-money laundering control, outsourcing control, safety and security control, prevention of conflict of interests control and partnering intermediaries control.	控制措施一般包括：制度流程控制、不相容职务分离控制、授权审批控制、会计系统控制、财产保护控制、预算控制、经营管理分析控制、绩效考评控制、应急处理控制、产品创新控制、反洗钱控制、外包控制、安全保卫控制、防止利益冲突控制、合作中介机构控制等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Internal supervision	4.内部监督	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Institutions and departments of ICBC are responsible for supervisory inspection of relevant business areas with their respective scope of duties.	工商银行各机构、各部门按照职责分工负责本机构、本部门相关业务领域的监督检查工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal control compliance department is responsible for overall management of supervisory inspections and the oversight of all institutions’ and departments’ activities regarding the implementation of supervisory inspections.	内控合规部门负责统筹管理层各项监督检查工作，对各机构、各部门监督检查工作开展情况进行再监督。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit department is responsible for supervisory assessment of operating activities, risk management, internal controls and corporate governance effectiveness.	内部审计部门负责对经营活动、风险管理、内部控制和公司治理效果进行监督评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal supervisions at ICBC take the form of day-to-day supervision, specialized supervision and internal control assessment.	工商银行内部监督方式包括日常监督、专项监督和内控评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has an internal control accountability system.	工商银行建立了内部控制责任追究制度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Board of Directors and the Senior Management are responsible for effectiveness of internal controls and assume the liability for any material loss arising from ineffective internal control.	董事会、高级管理层对内部控制的有效性负责，并对内部控制失效造成的重大损失承担责任。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Senior Management will pursue the liability of and impose punishment upon any internal control violators in accordance with laws and internal control regulations, and shall assume the liability for inadequate resolution of violations.	高级管理层对违反内部控制的人员，依据法律规定、内部管理制度追究责任和予以处分，并承担处理不力的责任。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
All institutions and departments shall make timely correction of problems in internal control and assume relevant liability for risks and losses incurred.	各机构、各部门需及时纠正内部控制存在的问题，对造成的风险和损失承担相应的责任。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The supervisory inspection department will be held liable for non-detection of major problems due to its failure to execute the inspection plan, concealment or untrue reporting of problems detected during inspection, serious inconsistencies between inspection conclusion and facts and inadequate follow-up on the correction of problems detected during inspection.	监督检查部门对未执行检查方案、程序和方法导致重大问题未能被发现，隐瞒不报或者未如实反映检查发现问题，检查结论与事实严重不符，检查发现问题查处整改工作跟踪不力等行为，承担相应的责任。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. Information and communication	5.信息与沟通	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has in place a database and management information system that permeate all levels of institutions and covers all areas of business, allowing real-time and full-range monitoring of all risks. Relevant information in the course of business management and internal control is documented accurately, truthfully and completed in paper or other proper forms. Procedures to manage basic and specialized records are perfected to ensure records are clear, easily identifiable and searchable.	工商银行建立了贯穿各级机构和覆盖各个业务领域的数据库和管理信息系统，实现对各类风险的实时和全面监测；以书面或者其他适当的形式，及时准确、真实完整的记录经营管理和内部控制过程中的相关信息，健全基本档案制度建设和专业档案管理程序，确保档案记录清晰、易于识别和可检索。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Effective internal and external communication mechanisms have been established to ensure all information can be communicated accurately and quickly to relevant institutions, departments and personnel along the internal control line, and the operations of institutions at all levels, duty performance of all departments and personnel, detected deficiencies and weaknesses in internal control, emergencies and significant events can be smoothly fed back to the Management. In particular, information sharing is enhanced between institutions and between departments within information management powers. External information, especially customer information, is screened, checked, consolidated and analyzed in a timely manner. Information on business management, accounting and internal control are disclosed and communicated on a timely, truthful and complete basis as required.	建立了有效的内外部信息交流机制，确保各项信息能够按照内部控制路线准确、快捷地传递到相关机构、部门和员工，各级机构经营情况、各部门和员工履职情况、发现的内部控制隐患和缺陷、各类突发事件和重大事件等信息能够顺畅反馈到管理层，各机构之间和各部门之间按信息管理权限加强各类信息资源的共享，对外部信息尤其是客户信息及时进行筛选、核对、整合和分析，按要求及时、真实、完整地披露和传达各类经营管理、财务会计和内部控制信息。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC maintains a sound confidentiality system that includes standardized requirements on the production, receipt, distribution, transfer, use, reproduction, retention and destruction of media carrying state secrets and ICBC’s business secrets and clearly sets out management requirements regarding state secrets and ICBC’s business secrets involved in overseas institutions’ business activities with foreign, domestic (or mainland) counterparties.	工商银行健全保密制度，规范了国家秘密和工商银行商业秘密载体的制作、收发、传递、使用、复制、保存和销毁等方面的要求，明确了境外机构对外业务往来、同国（境）内联系工作时涉及国家秘密和工商银行商业秘密信息的管理要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC also requires that electronic documents containing business secrets and other sensitive information that shall be treated as business secrets should be subject to security protection and access management through the electronic document security control system.	还规定商业秘密电子文件或其他需要比照商业秘密管理的敏感信息均应通过电子文件安全控制系统进行安全保护和权限管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The anti-fraud mechanism has been created and improved, with emphasis placed on strengthening the monitoring of misappropriation or embezzlement of assets, pursuance of illegal gains, false records, misleading statements or major omissions in financial statements and information disclosures, abuse of powers by directors, supervisors and senior management and collusive frauds by personnel in relevant institutions.	健全反舞弊机制，重点加强对侵占、挪用资产，牟取不当利益, 财务会计报告和信息披露中的虚假记载、误导性陈述或者重大遗漏，董事、监事及其他高级管理人员滥用职权，有关机构人员串通舞弊等方面的监控。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Processes for complaint handling and complainant protection are in place, a reporting line exclusively for complaints has been established and complainant protection has been enhanced to ensure complaints serve as an important route for collecting fraud information.	建立举报投诉和举报人保护制度，设置举报专线，加强对举报人的保护，确保举报和投诉成为有效掌握反舞弊信息的重要途径。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Compliance Management	二、合规管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Objective and principles of compliance management	（一）合规管理的目标及原则	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The objective of compliance management at ICBC is to effectively identify and manage compliance risk and take effective control measures to assure compliance of operations by establishing and improving a compliance management system commensurate with the Bank’s development strategy and organizational structure.	工商银行开展合规管理的目标是通过建立健全与本行发展战略和组织架构相适应的合规管理体系，实现对合规风险的有效识别和管理，采取有效控制措施，为合规经营提供保障。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Principle of compliance paramount.	1.合规至上原则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC advocates and implements the philosophy of “Compliance and Integrity”, persistently complies with supervisory requirements and its corporate regulations to a high standard and carries out all operating and managerial activities on a prudent basis.	工商银行倡导并推行“合规经营，诚实守信”的合规理念，坚持高标准遵守监管要求和工商银行规定，以审慎经营为出发点，开展各项经营管理活动。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Principle of entire staff and total process.	2.全员全过程原则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Compliance management is the common responsibility of all ICBC staff and runs through the total process of operation and management.	合规管理是工商银行所有员工的共同责任，贯穿经营管理事前、事中、事后全过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Principle and independence and collaboration.	3.独立与协作原则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal control & compliance department maintains relative independence, has the right to access necessary information and personnel and assumes no duties that may trigger a conflict of interest with its compliance management duty.	内控合规部门保持相对独立性，享有接触必要信息和人员的权限，不承担与其合规管理职责产生利益冲突的其他职责。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
All institutions (departments) shall collaborate with the internal control & compliance department in compliance management, without restricting or hindering compliance management for whatever reasons. 	各级机构（部门）与内控合规部门协作开展合规管理工作，不得以任何理由限制和阻挠。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Overview of compliance management construction at ICBC	（二）工商银行合规管理建设概况	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Organizational structure for compliance management	1.合规管理组织架构	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A “Centralized + Decentralized” organizational structure for compliance has been created in line with the strategic objectives, organizational structure, business size and business characteristics of ICBC.	结合工商银行的战略目标、组织架构、业务规模、经营特色，搭建了“集中+分散”的合规组织架构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Top-down approach to compliance management.	（1）合规从高层做起。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Board of Directors, the Board of Supervisors and the Senior Management of ICBC strictly perform their compliance management duties within their respective mandate, thereby ensuring all operating and managerial activities satisfy supervisory requirements and the Bank’s strategic development needs.	工商银行的董事会、监事会、高级管理层严格履行职责范围内相应的合规管理职责，确保各项经营管理活动符合监管要求和本行发展战略需要。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Centralized and independent organization of compliance management.	（2）集中独立的合规管理组织。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has an Internal Control & Compliance Department at the Head Office level that oversees internal control and compliance management. Under the leadership of the Senior Management and the Chief Risk Officer, the Internal Control & Compliance Department regularly meets with the Legal Affairs Department, the Risk Management Department and the banking departments to discuss and deal with risk management issues regarding internal control and compliance of the Bank.	工商银行在总行层面设立内控合规部，统筹管理内部控制与合规管理两大管理职能，同法律事务部、风险管理部和各业务部门在高级管理层和首席风险官的领导下形成定期会晤机制，共同研究和解决全行内控合规风险管理问题。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition, the internal audit department audits and assesses the soundness and effectiveness of the Bank’s compliance management system and the performance of compliance management duties by institutions (departments) and the internal control & compliance department at all levels.	此外，内部审计部门对全行合规管理体系的健全性、有效性，以及各级机构（部门）、内控合规部门的合规管理履职情况进行审计评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Decentralized resources of compliance management.	（3）分散的合规管理资源。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Institutions (departments) of ICBC at all levels are responsible for institutional (departmental) compliance management in accordance with rules, standards and the Senior Management’s requirements.	工商银行的各级机构（部门）按照各项规则、准则及高级管理层的要求，负责做好本级机构（部门）的合规管理工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition, each employee shall assume the compliance management duty corresponding to his or her job, follow all rules and standards, accept compliance training and supervisory inspection and report any compliance risk and irregularities in a timely manner.	同时，每位员工承担与其工作岗位相对应的合规管理职责，自觉遵守各项规则和准则、接受合规培训和检查监督，及时报告合规风险和违规行为等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Compliance management procedures	2.合规管理程序	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Tracking of supervisory rules.	（1）监管规则跟踪。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal control & compliance department at each level shall keep track of supervisory rules, collect and analysis the impact of changes in supervisory rules on compliance of the Bank, issue risk reminders and provide the Management with supports for compliance-related decision making. Institutions (departments) at each level shall develop timely countermeasures according to changes in regulatory requirements.	各级内控合规部门及时跟踪监管规则，归集和分析监管规则变化对我行合规经营的影响，发布风险提示，为管理层提供合规决策支持；各级机构（部门）根据监管要求变化及时制定应对措施。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Compliance training and advice.	（2）合规培训与咨询。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Institutions (departments) at each level shall periodically train employees on compliance and familiarize employees with compliance requirements specific to their jobs. The internal control & compliance department at each level shall assist in training and provide compliance advice to ensure employees are familiar with rules and standards they must abide by.	各级机构（部门）定期组织员工开展合规培训，引导员工了解和掌握各工作岗位的合规要求；各级内控合规部门协助组织培训，做好合规咨询等工作，确保员工知悉和掌握必须遵循的规则和准则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Management of regulations.	（3） 制度管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal control & compliance department at each level shall develop procedures for managing regulations and periodically review and evaluate regulations. The institutions (departments) at each level shall develop regulations, procedures and business operating guidelines according to operational and managerial needs.	各级内控合规部门制定制度管理规范，并定期组织开展制度梳理评价；各级机构（部门）根据经营管理需要制定制度、规程和业务操作指南。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(4) Compliance review.	（4）合规审查。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The institutions (departments) at each level shall submit new regulations, new products or services and other significant business matters to the internal control & compliance department for review. New services or products proposed to the regulators must be accompanied by the opinion of the internal control & compliance department.	各级机构（部门）在制定制度、开发新产品、新业务等重大经营事项时须报送内控合规部门审查，向监管部门申报的新业务、新产品申请须附有内控合规部门意见。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(5) Compliance risk monitoring.	（5）合规风险监测。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The institutions (departments) at each level shall monitor the compliance risk in all products, services and managerial activities, take relevant control measures and regularly report to the institutional (departmental) head and the internal control & compliance department at the corresponding level on compliance risk management. The internal control & compliance department at each level shall monitor the overall compliance risk of institutions at the corresponding level and comprehensively identify and assess the impact of compliance risk.	各级机构（部门）对各项产品、业务和管理活动的合规风险进行监测，并采取相应控制措施，定期向本机构（部门）负责人和同级内控合规部门报告合规风险管理情况；各级内控合规部门监测本级机构整体的合规风险信息，全面识别和评估合规风险影响。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(6) Compliance inspection, investigation and assessment.	（6）合规检查、调查与评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The institutions (departments) at each level shall self-inspect the compliance status in their respective operation and management. The internal control & compliance department at each level shall conduct compliance inspection, investigation and assessment at appropriate times, disclose compliance risk and irregularities and provide suggestions on improvement and punishment.	各级机构（部门）对自身经营管理过程中的合规情况进行自查；各级内控合规部门适时组织合规检查、调查与评价，揭示合规风险和违规行为，并提出改进和处罚建议。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(7) Specific compliance obligations.	（7）特定合规义务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The institutions (departments) at each level shall proactively perform AML and other specific compliance obligations in accordance with supervisory requirements. The internal control & compliance department is responsible for causing institutions (departments) to fulfill specific compliance obligations.	各级机构（部门）根据监管要求自觉履行反洗钱等特定合规义务，各级内控合规部门负责推动各级机构（部门）做好特定合规义务的落实工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(8) Compliance risk reporting.	（8）合规风险报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The compliance management reports of ICBC include the report from the Senior Management to the Board of Directors, the report from the Internal Control & Compliance Department of the Head Office to the Senior Management and regular and specific compliance management reports from overseas institutions.	工商银行的合规管理报告包括高级管理层向董事会的报告、总行内控合规部向高级管理层的报告、各境外机构报送的定期和专项合规管理报告等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Compliance management of overseas institutions.	3.境外机构合规管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Establishing and improving the organizational structure for compliance management.	（1）建立健全合规管理组织架构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institutions, responsible for internal compliance management, shall strictly abide by applicable rules and standards of the People’s Republic of China and host countries or regions, fully implement relevant policies and procedures developed by the Head Office, fulfill compliance management duties, effectively prevent compliance risk and ensure institution-wide compliance.	各境外机构承担本机构的合规管理责任，应严格遵守中华人民共和国以及所在国家、地区所适用的规则和准则，认真执行总行制定的相关规章制度，切实履行合规管理职责，有效防范合规风险，确保本机构合规经营。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas branches and subsidiaries shall also create an organizational structure for compliance management commensurate with supervisory requirements and scope of business, clearly assign compliance management duties, appoint principal officers and staff for compliance management and ensure their compliance management function runs properly.	各境外分行、附属机构还应构建与监管要求和经营范围相适应的合规管理组织架构，明确合规管理职责，配备合规负责人、合规管理人员，确保本机构合规管理职能正常运行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Strengthening communication with the Head Office.	（2）加强与总行业务交流与沟通。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institutions shall accept the guidance on compliance management provided by the Internal Control & Compliance Department of the Head Office. Any inquiry made to the Head Office about compliance management shall be filed with both the Internal Control & Compliance Department and the relevant banking department of the Head Office. The Internal Control & Compliance Department of the Head Office will coordinate the relevant banking department to provide compliance advice. If the inquiry is about implementation of relevant policies and procedures developed by the Head Office, the relevant banking department of the Head Office is responsible for responding to the inquiry.	各境外机构的合规管理应接受总行内控合规部的业务指导，向总行进行合规管理咨询时应同时报请总行内控合规部和业务归口管理部门，由总行内控合规部协调相关归口管理部门完成合规咨询事务；就总行制定的有关规章制度执行问题进行咨询的，由总行业务归口管理部门负责解答。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An irregular meeting mechanism for the compliance officers of overseas institutions has been created to strengthen communication on compliance management between the Head Office and overseas institutions.	建立境外机构合规官的不定期会晤机制，加强总行与境外机构的合规管理工作交流。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Establishing and improving the reporting mechanism for compliance management.	（3）建立健全合规管理报告机制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institutions shall create and improve the reporting line for compliance management, regularly submit periodical and specific compliance management reports to the Internal Control & Compliance Department of the Head Office and ensure timelines, completeness and accuracy of information.	各境外机构应建立健全合规管理报告路线，定期向总行内控合规部报送定期和专项合规管理报告，并确保信息的及时性、完整性和准确性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Any major emergencies arising from compliance risk shall be handled in accordance with relevant rules of the Head Office.	因合规风险导致有关重大突发事件的，应按照总行相关规定进行处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Operational Risk Management	三、操作风险管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The overall objectives of operational risk management at ICBC are to: clarify operational risk management roles and responsibilities of all parties and shore up the confidence of shareholders and the public by establishing and improving the operational risk management framework; increase customer satisfaction and employees’ sense of belonging and enhance the overall service standard by identifying high-risk areas and mitigate operational risk hazards; improve allocation of operational risk management resources and increase operating efficiency of the Bank by strengthening process control and balancing risk and control; reduce operational risk losses of the Bank and improve control capability and standard by taking effective risk control and mitigation measures; and meet all supervisory requirements and minimize legal and compliance risks by examination and supervision.	我行操作风险管理总体目标是：通过建立健全操作风险治理架构，明确各方操作风险管理角色和职责，增强股东和公众信心；通过识别高风险领域，化解各类操作风险隐患，增强客户满意度和员工归属感，提升整体服务水平；通过加强过程控制，综合考虑和权衡控制成本与收益，改善操作风险管理资源配置，提高我行运营效率；通过采取有效的风险控制和缓释措施，降低我行操作风险损失，提高控制能力和水平；通过审查和监督，满足各项外部监管要求，将法律及合规风险降至最低。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Tools and process of operational risk management	（一）操作风险管理工具及流程	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The tools of operational risk management at ICBC include but not limited to: business operation flowchart, operational risk and control self-assessment, key indicators of operational risk, management of significant operational risk incidents, loss data collection and management, scenario analysis, continuous operation and emergency management, measurement of regulatory capital and economic capital for operational risk, internal control assessment, disciplinary procedures and operational risk reporting.	工商银行的操作风险管理工具包括但不限于：业务操作流程图、操作风险与控制自我评估、关键操作风险指标、重大操作风险事件管理、损失数据采集和管理、情景分析、持续经营和应急管理、操作风险监管资本和经济资本的计量、内控评价、违规违纪行为处理、操作风险报告等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Tools of operational risk management apply to the total process of operational risk management.	操作风险管理工具应运用于操作风险管理全流程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The operational risk management process of ICBC shall include identification, assessment, control/mitigation, monitoring, measurement and reporting of operational risk.	工商银行的操作风险管理流程应包括操作风险识别、评估、控制/缓释、监测、计量、报告等环节。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Operational risk reporting	（二）操作风险报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Operational risk reporting at ICBC, subject to the principles of completeness, materiality, timeliness, regularity, accuracy and farsightedness, shall truthfully and completely reflect the operational risk profile of all business lines and institutions, reveal potential critical risks and provide effect improvement measures and suggestions.	工商银行的操作风险报告遵循全面性、重要性、及时性、规范性、准确性和前瞻性的原则，真实、全面反映各业务条线和所辖机构的操作风险状况，揭示潜在关键风险，提出有效的改进措施和建议。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Operational risk reporting is classified into the report on operational risk management, the report on operational risk classification control, the report on operational risk in business lines, the specific operational risk report, the statistical analysis report on operational risk and the report on significant operational risk incidents.	操作风险报告包括以下六类：操作风险管理报告、操作风险分类控制报告、业务线操作风险报告、专题操作风险报告、操作风险统计分析报表和重大操作风险事件报告等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas branches and subsidiaries shall submit the report on operational risk management, the statistical analysis report on operational risk and the report on significant operational risk incidents as formal documents to the Head Office at required frequency.	各境外分行和境外附属机构应按照规定频率、以正式文件向总行报送操作风险管理报告、操作风险统计分析报表和重大操作风险事件报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IV. Anti-money Laundering (AML)	四、反洗钱	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. International AML organizations and supervisory requirements	1.反洗钱国际组织及监管要求	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Financial Action Task Force on Money Laundering (FATF), an inter-governmental body that coordinates, assesses and supervises AML control measures of member countries, was created in 1989 at the Paris Summit of leaders of the Group of Seven.	1989年，七国集团首脑在巴黎年度经济峰会上发起设立金融行动特别工作组（FATF），作为政府间协调、评估、监督成员国反洗钱控制措施的组织。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Subsequently, regional AML bodies were established in succession to promote AML worldwide, including the Asia/Pacific Group on Money Laundering (APG), the Caribbean Financial Action Task Force (CFATF) and the Eurasian Group on Combating Money Laundering and Terrorist Financing (EAG).	随后，亚太反洗钱工作组（APG）、加勒比地区金融行动特别工作组（CFATF）、欧亚反洗钱和反恐融资小组（EAG）等区域性的反洗钱组织陆续成立，共同推动全球反洗钱工作开展。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As a founding member of EAG and a member of APG, China officially joined FATF in 2007.	我国是欧亚反洗钱与反恐怖融资组织（EAG）的创始成员国之一，亚太反洗钱组织（APG）成员国之一，并于2007年正式加入了金融行动特别工作组（FATF）。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
At present, AML guidance documents generally accepted in the international community include the “40+9 Recommendations on money laundering and terrorist financing” issued by FATF, the Statement on Prevention of Criminal Use of the Banking System for the Purpose of Money Laundering issued by Basel Committee on Banking Supervision and recommendations released by regional AML bodies. These documents provide fundamental principles for national regulatory bodies to develop their national AML measures.	目前国际比较通用的反洗钱指导文件主要有FATF组织制定的“打击洗钱和恐怖融资的40+9项建议”、巴塞尔银行监管委员会发布的《关于防止犯罪分子利用银行系统洗钱的声明》等文件，以及各区域性反洗钱组织出台的工作建议，这些文件为各国监管机构制定本国反洗钱措施提供了基本原则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Directive on Prevention of the Use of the Financial System for the Purpose of Money Laundering (I, II and III) issued by EU is mandatory and shall be implemented by each member country.	其中，欧盟（EU）颁布的《欧盟关于防止利用金融系统洗钱的指令》（I、Ⅱ、Ⅲ）具有强制性，要求每个成员国家必须贯彻执行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. AML supervisory requirements of China	2. 中国反洗钱监管要求	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Chinese government attaches great importance to AML. With reference to international standards and based on its national conditions, China established the basic legal, regulatory and organizational frameworks for AML and shaped a complete system of AML regulations.	中国政府高度重视反洗钱工作，参照国际标准，立足中国国情，确立了中国反洗钱法律、监管和组织机构的基本框架，建立起了较为完整的反洗钱制度体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
China made four amendments to the Criminal Law to expand the scope of upstream crimes of money laundering, issued judicial interpretations to define subjective elements of the money laundering crime and strengthened the punishment on money laundering activities.	中国先后四次修订《刑法》有关条款，扩大了洗钱罪的上游犯罪范围，并出台司法解释界定洗钱罪的主观要件，加大了对洗钱行为的处罚力度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In October 2006, the Anti-Money Laundering Law of the People’s Republic of China (“AML Law”) was promulgated to legislatively establish China's AML administration system and set forth AML obligations of financial institutions.	2006年10月，颁布了《中华人民共和国反洗钱法》，从法律上确立了中国反洗钱行政管理体制，明确了金融机构的反洗钱义务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To supplement the AML Law, the People's Bank of China (PBOC) released the Provisions on Anti-money Laundering of Financial Institutions, the Administrative Measures on the Reporting by Financial Institutions of Large-Value and Suspicious Transactions, the Administrative Measures on the Reporting by Financial Institutions of Suspicious Transactions Relating to Terrorist Financing and the Administrative Measures on Customer Identification and Retention of Customer Identity Data and Transaction Records by Financial Institutions (“One Law & Four Decrees”).	与《反洗钱法》配套，中国人民银行出台了《金融机构反洗钱规定》、《金融机构大额交易和可疑交易报告管理办法》、《金融机构报告涉嫌恐怖融资的可疑交易管理办法》和《金融机构客户身份识别和客户身份资料及交易记录保存管理办法》（以上简称“一法四令”）。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
“One Law & Four Decrees” establish China's basic framework for AML work, set forth supervisory duties of PBOC in anti-money laundering activities and provide detailed provisions on customer identification and transaction record retention by financial institutions, reporting of large-value and suspicious transactions, reporting of suspicious transactions relating to terrorist financing.	“一法四令”基本构建了我国反洗钱工作的制度体系，明确了中国人民银行在反洗钱活动中的监督管理职责，并对金融机构客户身份识别和交易记录保存、大额和可疑交易报告、涉嫌恐怖融资的可疑交易报告等方面做出了具体的规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
POBC, a department of the State Council in charge of overseeing anti-money laundering, is mainly responsible for coordinating nationwide AML work, monitoring AML funds, developing AML policies and procedures for financial institutions, conducting supervisory inspection over the AML work of financial institutions and particular non-financial institutions, investigating suspicious transactions and providing collaboration in AML.	中国人民银行是国务院反洗钱行政主管部门，主要负责协调全国的反洗钱工作，负责反洗钱资金监测，制定金融机构反洗钱规章，监督检查金融机构及特定非金融机构的反洗钱工作，调查可疑交易，开展反洗钱协作等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Anti-Money Laundering Bureau is a body of PBOC in charge of coordinating nationwide AML work and developing AML rules and policies for financial institutions.	中国人民银行内设机构反洗钱局，负责承办组织协调国家反洗钱工作、研究和拟订金融机构反洗钱规则和政策等工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition, PBOC has set up a body specializing in collection, analysis, monitoring and provision of AML information – China Anti-Money Laundering Monitoring and Analysis Center, a body in charge of centraLly collecting, collating and retaining large-value and suspicious transaction reports submitted by financial institutions.	此外，人民银行还设立了专门收集、分析、监测和提供反洗钱情报的机构——中国反洗钱监测分析中心，负责统一收集、整理和保存金融机构报送的大额与可疑交易报告等工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. AML risk of overseas institutions	3.境外分支机构反洗钱工作的风险	sample1-en-sample1-zh
AML deficiencies of overseas institutions may lead to losses and negative impact on their own business operations, but also hurt business expansion of the parent company and may result in serious consequences, like financial loss, reputational loss and shareholder value loss.	境外机构如在反洗钱工作上存在缺陷，不仅可能为本机构的业务经营带来损失和负面影响，也不利于母公司业务的拓展，可能造成财务损失、声誉损失、股东价值损失等严重后果。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In recent years, Citibank (Japan), Lloyds Bank, Credit Suisse Group, the Royal Bank of Scotland, the Bank of Credit and Commerce International (BCCI) and the US-based Wachovia and J.P. Morgan were punished (in the form of financial service restrictions or huge fines) by regulators in the host jurisdictions due to involvement in money laundering or inadequate AML efforts.	近年来，就有花旗银行（日本）、劳埃德银行、瑞士信贷集团、苏格兰皇家银行、国际信贷商业银行(BCCI)，以及美国本土的美联银行和摩根大通等银行因参与洗钱活动或反洗钱工作不力受到属地监管机构给予的限制金融服务或巨额经济罚款等处罚。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. AML work at ICBC and AML requirements on overseas institutions	（二）工商银行反洗钱工作情况及境外机构反洗钱工作要求	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. AML efforts of ICBC and achievement	1.工商银行反洗钱工作开展情况及成效	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With regard to the organizational framework, ICBC has an AML Leadership Group at the Head Office level that is in charge of the group-wide AML work and headed by the Bank’s executive overseeing AML work.	在组织体系建设方面，工商银行在总行层面设立了反洗钱领导小组，统一领导集团反洗钱工作，由分管反洗钱工作的行领导任组长。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The AML Leadership Group’s Office, set up in the Internal Control & Compliance Department, is responsible for leading the bank-wide AML work.	总行反洗钱领导小组办公室设在内控合规部，负责牵头全行反洗钱工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The AML Leadership Group comprises five specialized AML groups (corporate banking, personal banking, international banking, E-banking and bank card) that are headed by the Operation Management Department, the Personal Banking Department, the International Banking Department, the E-banking Department and the Bank Card Business Department of the Head Office, respectively.	领导小组下设对公、个人、国际业务、电子银行、银行卡业务5个反洗钱专业小组，分别由总行运行管理部、个人金融业务部、国际业务部、电子银行部、银行卡业务部牵头负责。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has preliminarily shaped up the organizational structure for AML, in which the AML Leadership Group is the governing body, the Internal Control & Compliance Department is the lead department, functional departments are main participants and outlets are the foundation.	工商银行已初步形成了以反洗钱领导小组为领导机构、内控合规部门为牵头部门、各职能部门为主体、营业网点为基础的反洗钱组织体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With regard to regulations, ICBC has put in place a relatively complete set of internal control policies and procedures for AML. The Anti-Money Laundering Policy, the Measures on Reporting of Large-value and Suspicious Transactions and the Provisional Measures on Customer Risk Classification Management were promulgated; the AML operating procedures for personal banking, corporate banking, E-banking and bank card segments were issued.	在制度规范方面，工商银行建立了较为完善的反洗钱内控制度体系，先后出台了《反洗钱规定》、《大额交易和可疑交易报告管理办法》、《客户风险分类管理暂行办法》等反洗钱管理制度；印发了个人、对公、电子银行、银行卡等专业的反洗钱内部操作规程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With regard to IT supports, ICBC developed a proprietary AML monitoring system that maintains real-time monitoring of suspicious transactions that meet supervisory criteria on suspicious transaction identification or are manually detected. All suspicious transactions identified will be reported to PBOC on the basis of “head office to head office”.	在系统支持方面，工商银行自主研发了反洗钱监控系统，对满足监管规定可疑识别标准的和人工发现的可疑交易进行实时监控，并按照“总对总”模式统一向人行报送。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The R&D and launch of the global special control list processing system and the overseas AML monitoring system are facilitated to provide IT supports for enhancing the Group’s ability to prevent the risk of money laundering and terrorist financing.	推动全球特别控制名单处理系统及境外反洗钱监控系统中的研发和投产，为强化集团防范洗钱与恐怖融资风险能力提供系统支持。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With regard to AML publicity and training, ICBC carries out the AML Awareness Week, the AML Awareness Month and other publicity programs in accordance with requirements of regulators.	在反洗钱宣传培训方面，工商银行按照各级监管部门要求，积极开展反洗钱宣传周、宣传月等活动。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A sustainable mechanism for AML training is in place to enhance work skills of the Management and first-line staff.	建立反洗钱培训长效机制，提高自管理层到一线员工的工作技能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Certified Anti-money Laundering Specialist (CAMS) certification program was introduced and promoted to improve the competency of employees working in AML roles.	引入并推进国际公认反洗钱师（CAMS）资质认证，提高反洗钱岗位人员素质。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With regard to cooperation in AML supervision, ICBC adequately implements requirements of regulators and has been publicly commended by regulators many times for its outstanding performance in assisting in AML regulatory investigation and reporting suspicious transactions.	在反洗钱监管合作方面，认真落实监管机构的工作要求，在协助反洗钱行政调查、报送可疑交易线索等方面效果显著，多次受到监管部门的通报表扬。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. AML requirements on overseas institutions	2.境外机构反洗钱工作要求	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institutions of ICBC shall carry out AML work in accordance with supervisory standards of China or the host countries (regions), whichever are more stringent.	工商银行的各境外机构按照中国及驻在国家（地区）监管标准孰严的原则开展各项反洗钱工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Improving the management mechanism and organizational structure for AML.	（1）健全反洗钱管理机制和组织架构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Roles and responsibilities in the AML department shall be defined to ensure independence of the AML department’s work. Internal and external reporting duties of all departments shall be clearly set forth. The Board of Directors and the Management shall have knowledge of institution-wide significant AML matters.	明确界定反洗钱部门工作职责以及岗位职责，确保反洗钱部门工作的独立性；明晰各部门的反洗钱事项内、外部报告职责，董事会和管理层须知悉本机构的反洗钱重要工作事项。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Improving the internal control framework for AML.	（2）完善反洗钱内控制度体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The institutional policies and procedures for AML and counter-terrorist financing shall be fully reviewed and improved or revised in a timely manner to reflect any changes in the supervisory requirements of China and host countries (regions) as well as regulations and systems of the Head Office.	全面梳理本机构的反洗钱和反恐怖融资管理制度，及时按照中国及驻在国家（地区）监管要求、以及总行制度和系统建设的变更进行完善、修订。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Creating the AML reporting and crisis/incident management mechanism for overseas institutions.	（3）建立境外机构反洗钱报告及危机事件管理机制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Within five working days following the end of each half year, each overseas institution shall submit an AML work report to the Head Office for that half-year period.	在每半年结束后的5个工作日内，向总行提交报告日前半年的本机构反洗钱工作情况报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
AML crisis/incident disposition shall be included in the institutional contingency plan. If any major AML risk incident (lawsuit, dispute, regulatory punishment or media coverage) takes place, timely measures shall be taken in response in accordance with requirements of the Head Office.	将反洗钱危机事件处置纳入机构应急预案体系，遇有反洗钱重大风险事件（被诉、纠纷、监管处罚或媒体披露等）时，按总行规定及时采取应对措施。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(4) Accelerating the effort to create an integrated AML application system for domestic and overseas institutions.	（4）加快建设境内外一体化的反洗钱应用系统平台。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institutions shall carry out system requirements survey, launch and operation in accordance with the Head Office’s plan for the integrated AML application system for domestic and overseas institutions, promote and apply the global special control list processing system on a full-scale basis and meet AML and CTF risk prevention and control objectives under the Group’s uniform rules.	配合总行境内外一体化反洗钱应用系统规划，做好本机构的系统需求调研、运行投产等工作；全面推广应用全球特别控制名单处理系统，实现集团统一规则下的反洗钱和反恐怖融资风险防控目标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(5) Strengthening AML training and specialist development.	（5）加强反洗钱培训和专家队伍培养。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institutions shall provide training to staff at different levels and in different roles, strengthen trainee examination, ensure all their employees acknowledge in writing their awareness of laws, regulations and personal responsibility relating to AML and ensure AML compliance personnel possess AML skills.	针对不同层次、不同岗位人员组织开展培训，加大培训考核力度，并确保本机构所有员工必须书面确认知晓反洗钱法律法规和个人责任，确保反洗钱合规人员了解和掌握反洗钱专业技能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(6) Stepping up the supervisory inspection of AML work.	（6）加大对反洗钱工作的监督检查力度。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institutions shall conduct multi-tiered, well-focused AML self-inspection and take effective actions to correct problems detected in any external inspections.	分层次、有重点地开展反洗钱自我检查，对各类外部检查发现的问题切实落实整改。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Six Audit Management of Overseas Institutions	第六节 境外机构审计管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Overview of Internal Audit at ICBC	一、工商银行内部审计基本情况	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit system of ICBC, born with the founding of the joint-stock company, evolves as the Bank’s corporate governance mechanism improves.	工商银行的内部审计体系伴随着我行股份公司的成立而诞生，伴随着我行公司治理机制的完善而发展。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Since the internal audit system was officially established in 2004, audit activities have been effectively carried out in risk management, internal control and corporate governance of the Bank, the quality and capability of auditing has improved significantly and the specialization and professionalism in auditing have been enhanced rapidly. An internal audit system with unique ICBC characteristics is becoming full-fledged and functioning effectively.	2004年底正式组建至今，在全行风险管理、内部控制和公司治理等各领域开展了有效的审计活动，审计质量和审计能力长足进步，审计专业化和职业化水平快速提升，富有工商银行特色的内部审计体系已趋成熟并有效运作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Governance framework	（一）治理架构	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Organizational structure.	组织体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Internal Audit Bureau is set up in the Head Office and 10 internal audit sub-bureaus are established in 10 key cities.	总行设内部审计局，在全国10个重点城市设10个内审分局。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The staff, compensation, financial affairs, training and audit activities in the internal audit system are centrally managed by the Head Office. Each internal audit sub-bureau is responsible for supervisory inspection of four to five branches. Internal audit sub-bureaus do not audit the branches in places where they are located and do not participate in operating or managerial activities, fully isolated from operation and management.	内审系统的人员、薪酬、财务、培训和审计活动等总行统一管理，各内审分局负责４-５家分行的监督检查工作，不审计驻地分行，不参与经营管理活动，与经营管理实行完全的利益隔离。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Reporting line.	报告路径。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit reports to the Board of Directors, accepts supervision, inspection and assessment from the Audit Committee, accepts guidance from the Board of Supervisors and provides feedback to the Management on significant audit information.	内部审计向董事会负责并报告工作，接受审计委员会的监督、检查和评价，接受监事会的工作指导，向管理层提供反馈重要审计信息。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit carries out audit activities under the valid authorization delegated by the Board of Directors, serves as supervisory resources for the Board of Directors and its Audit Committee to effectively perform the fiduciary duty and works with relevant parties to safeguard the effectivenesS of governance while performing their respective duties.	内部审计获得董事会的有效授权开展审计活动，作为董事会及其审计委员会有效履行受托责任的监督资源，与相关各方各司其职，共同维护治理成效。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Roles and functions	（二）职能定位	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Conducting risk-oriented internal audit.	实行以风险为导向的内部审计。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Separated from the original compliance inspection function, internal audit has shifted from account compliance check focused on error detection and correction to risk-oriented risk management audit aimed at value adding, from audit of individual cases or places to bank-wide supervisory assessment of systemic, overall and strategic risks and from post-event investigation and correction to risk analysis and assessment before and during an event and predictive early warning.	从原先的合规性检查职能中脱离出来，由查错纠弊为主的账项合规检查，转向以风险为导向、以增值为目的风险管理审计；由一事一地个案问题的稽核检查，转向对全行系统性、全局性、机制性、战略性风险的监督评价；由事后对问题的查纠，转向事中与事前的风险分析评估与预见预警。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Performing two functions.	履行两项职能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit of ICBC mainly performs two functions: assuring and advising.	工商银行内部审计主要履行确认和咨询两大职能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit of ICBC, as the third line of defense in the Bank’s risk control system, is a relatively independent system of supervision. With a high supervisory tier and an overarching audit perspective, the internal audit’s main responsibility is assuring and assessing adequacy and effectiveness of corporate governance, risk management and internal control of the Bank, assuring and assessing overall, systematic and strategic risks and the efficiency and effectiveness of strategic decision execution and providing pertinent and farsighted audit opinions and recommendations.	工商银行内部审计在全行的风险管控体系中处于第三道防线，是一套相对独立的监督系统，其监督层次高，审计视角综合，主要职责是确认和评价全行公司治理、风险管理和内部控制的充分性和有效性，确认和评价全局性、系统性、战略性风险及战略决策执行的效率与效果，提出有针对性、前瞻性的审计意见和建议。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Adhering to the principle of objectivity and prudence, internal audit has expanded from the assuring function alone to the advising function.	内部审计在坚持客观审慎原则的前提下，已由完全的确认职能，扩展到了咨询的职能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Serving three areas and diverse auditing.	服务三大领域，审计内容多元。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal audit at ICBC is wide-ranging to cover risk management, internal control and corporate governance of the Bank and address both domestic and overseas, off-balance-sheet and on-balance-sheet, traditional and innovative as well as bank-wide and group-wide activities. It can consolidate information of all departments, fields and stakeholders in corporate governance to identify and judge risks and provide recommendations at a higher level and from a more overarching perspective.	工商银行内部审计的工作领域宽泛，涉及全行风险管理、内部控制和公司治理各个领域，境内与境外、表内与表外、传统与创新、全行与集团等各领域均涉足，可以整合各部门、各领域和各治理方的信息，从更高层次和更加综合的视角去识别、判断风险，提出审计建议。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The scope of internal audit has been expanded over years, gradually from such traditional fields as bank-wide credit, finance and IT to group-wide assessment of internal control assessment, assessment of consolidated management and efficiency of strategy execution. A wide array of audit approaches and forms, including specialized audit, assessment, survey and off-site audit, are employed to perform audit functions effectively and meet various needs of all stakeholders in corporate governance.	内部审计的工作领域逐年扩大，逐步由全行信贷、财务、IT等传统业务领域扩展到集团的内部控制评价、并表管理评价、战略执行效率等领域，通过专项审计、审计评价、审计调研、非现场审计等多种方式和途径，深入有效地履行了审计职能，满足了公司各治理相关方的多种需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Methodology and techniques	（三）方法技术	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Off-site audit techniques.	非现场审计技术。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Advanced IT platforms are employed to create risk analysis methods suitable for the Bank’s specific conditions, assemble the off-site analysis team and shape the audit analysis and reporting system, thereby enabling day-to-day analysis and ongoing monitoring of main services and products of the Bank and meeting the objectives of “Remote Screening, Accurate Targeting and Effective Audit”.	利用先进的信息系统平台，建立符合我行实际的风险分析方法，组建非现场分析队伍，形成审计分析报告体系，实现了对全行主要业务、产品的日常分析和持续监测，达到“远程排查、精确制导、有效审计”的目标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Specialized core techniques.	专业核心技术。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A range of specialized core techniques for internal audit has gradually taken shape, including the internal control assessment and analysis technique, the risk analysis and assessment technique, the risk heat mapping technique and the audit results rating technique. In addition, such conventional techniques as sampling assessment, walk-through test, interview technique, modeling technique and computer-aided audit technique are widely applied in audit activities to increase efficiency and ensure quality of auditing.	内部审计所特有的内部控制评价分析技术、风险分析评估技术和风险热图构制技术以及审计结果评级技术等核心专业技术逐步形成；同时，一些常规技术如抽样评估、穿行测试、访谈技术、建模技术、以及计算机辅助审计技术等在审计活动中广泛运用，提高了审计效能，保证了审计质量。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IT systems and data platforms.	信息系统和数据平台。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The business information system and the management information system (AM2009) for internal control effectively support off-site audit and analysis, preliminarily enabling total-process control and real-time management of audit activities. 	内部审计的业务信息系统和管理信息系统(AM2009)，有效支持了非现场审计分析活动的开展，初步实现了对审计业务的全过程控制和实时管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Internal Audit System Applicable to Overseas Institutions	二、适用于境外机构的内部审计制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In recent years, the Internal Audit Bureau has issued the Audit Procedures for Overseas Institutions and the Standards for Internal Audit Services of Overseas Institutions to regulate internal audit work of overseas institutions of ICBC, promote internal audit standards across overseas institutions and comprehensively enhance the service capacity of internal audit.	近年来，内审局通过印发《境外机构审计办法》及《境外机构内部审计服务工作规范》，规范工商银行境外机构内部审计工作，在境外机构层面推广内部审计工作标准，全面提升内部审计的服务能力。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Internal audit charter of Industrial and Commercial Bank of China Limited	（一）中国工商银行股份有限公司内部审计章程	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to improve corporate governance, enhance internal control and optimize the internal audit system, the Internal Audit Bureau formulated the internal audit charter in accordance with the Guidelines on Internal Audit for Banking Financial Institutions promulgated by CBRC, the International Professional Practices Framework promulgated by the Institute of Internal Auditors, China Internal Auditing Standards promulgated by the China Institute of Internal Audit and the Articles of Association of Indusial and Commercial Bank of China Limited, having regard to particular conditions of ICBC. The internal audit charter, comprising eight chapters divided into 53 articles, sets forth basic requirements and provisions on the objectives, organizational structure, powers and duties, reporting procedure, quality control and assessment and accountability in connection with internal audit at ICBC.	为完善公司治理，加强内部控制，健全内部审计体系，内审局依据中国银行业监督管理委员会《银行业金融机构内部审计指引》、国际内部审计师协会《内部审计专业实务框架》、中国内部审计协会《中国内部审计准则》以及《中国工商银行股份有限公司章程》，结合工商银行实际，制定了内部审计章程，对工商银行内部审计的目标、组织体系、职责权限、报告制度、质量控制以及考核问责作出的基本要求和规定，共八章五十三条。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Definition of internal audit	1.内部审计定义	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal audit refers to independent and objective supervision, assessment and advising activities inside ICBC aimed at inspecting, evaluating and improving bank-wide effectiveness of operating activities, risk management, internal control and corporate governance using systematic and standardized approaches and fulfilling the development strategy and business management objectives of the Bank.	内部审计是工商银行内部独立、客观的监督、评价与咨询活动，通过系统化、规范化的方法，检查评价并改善全行经营活动、风险管理、内部控制和公司治理效果，促进全行发展战略和经营管理目标的实现。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Objectives of internal audit	2.内部审计工作目标	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal audit serves the Board of Directors. Its objectives are to:	内部审计服务于董事会，其工作目标是：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Cause to be implemented the economic and financial laws, regulations, policies of the State, rules and standards of regulatory bodies as well as policies and procedures of ICBC;	促进国家经济金融法律法规、方针政策、监管部门规章和工商银行各项规章制度的贯彻执行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Provide opinions and recommendations on the effectiveness of risk management, internal control and corporate governance within the Bank’s risk management framework and cause risks to be controlled at an acceptable level;	在全行风险管理框架内，对风险管理、内部控制和公司治理效果提出意见和建议，促使风险控制在可接受水平。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Cause to be improved the Bank’s business operations and management activities and increase the value of ICBC.	促进全行各项业务运营与管理活动的改善，增加工商银行价值。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Independent and vertical audit department	3.独立垂直的审计部门	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC sets up the internal audit department on an independent and vertical basis that reports to the Board of Directors, accepts guidance from the Board of Supervisors and accepts inspection, supervision and assessment by the Audit Committee.	工商银行设立独立、垂直的内部审计部门，向董事会负责并报告工作，接受监事会的指导，接受审计委员会的检查、监督和评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Responsibilities of internal audit department	4.内部审计部门职责	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit department shall perform the following responsibilities:	内部审计部门应履行以下职责：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Supervise and evaluate the adequacy and effectiveness of procedures and techniques for risk identification, measurement, monitoring, control and reporting;	监督、评价风险识别、计量、监测、控制、报告程序及技术的适用性和有效性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Supervise and evaluate the soundness and effectiveness of the internal control system;	监督、评价内部控制体系的健全性和有效性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Supervise and evaluate the effectiveness of corporate governance procedures;	监督、评价公司治理程序的有效性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Supervise and evaluate the security of IT systems and IT control activities;	监督、评价信息系统的安全性，信息科技控制活动的有效性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Supervise and evaluate the efficiency and effectiveness of financial and operational management and protection of assets;	监督、评价财务及经营管理的效率和效果，各项资产的保护情况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Supervise and evaluate the duty performance by persons in charge of key positions;	监督、评价重要岗位负责人履职情况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Coordinate audit inspections conducted over ICBC by financial regulators, audit authorities, non-governmental audit agencies and other external organizations in China;	协调国家金融监管部门、审计机关及社会审计机构等外部单位对工商银行开展的审计检查工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Properly carry out engagement, re-engagement or replacement of the accounting firm for ICBC in accordance with requirements of the Board of Directors and its Audit Committee; and	按照董事会及其审计委员会的要求，做好工商银行会计师事务所的聘请、续聘或改聘的事务性工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Other items of work required by the Board of Directors and its Audit Committee.	董事会及其审计委员会要求的其他工作事项。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. Scope of application of rules and regulations	5.规章适用范围	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Parent companies and their subsidiaries within ICBC Group shall accept audit, supervision and assessment by the internal audit department of ICBC in accordance with the internal audit charter. 	工商银行集团范围内的母公司及其控制的附属机构均应依照本章程规定接受工商银行内部审计部门的审计监督评价。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Internal audit procedures for overseas institutions	（二）境外机构内部审计办法	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to regulate internal audit work of overseas institutions of ICBC, the internal audit procedures for overseas institutions were formulated in accordance with the Guidelines on Internal Audit for Banking Financial Institutions promulgated by CBRC, the Articles of Association of Industrial and Commercial Bank of China Limited and the Internal Audit Charter of Industrial and Commercial Bank of China Limited.	为规范工商银行境外机构内部审计工作，依据中国银监会《银行业金融机构内部审计指引》、《中国工商银行股份有限公司章程》、《中国工商银行股份有限公司内部审计章程》以及其他相关规定，制定境外机构内部审计办法。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These procedures comprise eight chapters divided into 38 articles, including general provisions, organizational structure, duties and powers, scope of audit, audit procedures, quality control, audit report and supplementary provisions.	《办法》共分为八章三十八条，由总则、组织管理、职责与权限、审计范围、审计程序、质量控制、审计报告和附则组成。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Objectives of internal audit of overseas institutions	1.境外机构内部审计工作的目标	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To promote compliance of overseas institutions with laws, regulations and policies of China and host countries or regions, regulators’ requirements and the rules and procedures of ICBC;	促进境外机构贯彻执行我国和所在国(地区)相关经济金融法律法规、方针政策、监管机构规章以及工商银行各项规章制度；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To give opinions and recommendations on risk management, internal control and corporate governance of overseas institutions, and help control their risks at an acceptance level;	对境外机构的风险管理、内部控制和公司治理效果提出意见和建议，促使其将风险控制在可接受的水平；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To facilitate improvement in business operations and management activities of overseas institutions, increase value and fulfill strategic development and management objectives.	促进境外机构各项业务运营与管理活动的改善，增加价值,实现战略发展与经营管理目标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Principles of internal audit of overseas institutions:	2.境外机构内部审计工作原则 独立性原则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Independence - Audit work shall be independent of all business activities it supervises, inspects and evaluates;	审计工作应独立于其监督、检查、评价的各项业务活动； 客观性原则。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Objectivity - Audit work shall avoid any potential or emergence of conflicts of interest or bias to ensure objective and unbiased audit;	审计工作应避免潜在的或已经出现的利益冲突或偏见，以保持审计的客观公正；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Continuity - Conduct continuous on-site and off-site audits of overseas institutions through collecting main business data and information disclosed by external auditors and regulators;	持续性原则。 通过采集主要业务数据、外部审计和监管机构披露的各种信息，对境外机构开展持续非现场和现场审计工作；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Type-specific management - Provide internal audit management and guidance specific to different types of overseas institutions.	分类管理原则。 对不同类型境外机构的内部审计工作实施分类管理与指导。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Overseas branches’ responsibilities relating to internal audit	3.境外分行履行内部审计的相关职责	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas branches’ responsibilities relating to internal audit mainly include the following:	境外分行履行内部审计的相关职责主要包括：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Take charge of recruitment, compensation and administration of internal auditors;	负责内部审计人员的招聘、薪酬和行政管理；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Assist domestic and overseas regulators, external auditors and the Internal Audit Bureau in audit inspection;	配合境内外监管机构、外部审计和内部审计局的审计检查工作；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Rectify issues detected in audits and supervisory inspections;	落实审计和监管检查中所发现问题的整改工作；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Hear reports from internal auditors on day-to-day compliance inspection.	听取内部审计人员对日常合规性检查情况的报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Responsibilities of the internal audit department (staff) of overseas branches	4.境外分行内部审计部门(人员)的职责	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Responsibilities of the internal audit department (staff) of overseas branches mainly include the following:	境外分行内部审计部门(人员)的职责主要包括：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Independently conduct audits under the leadership of the Internal Audit Bureau without taking the responsibility for designing internal control processes, initiating or approving business matters or performing any other business management functions;	在内部审计局领导下，独立开展审计工作，不应承担设计内部控制流程、发起或批准业务事项等经营管理职能；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Conduct institution-wide risk assessment, develop the annual audit plan for overseas branches, solicit opinion from the branch management and submit the plan to the Internal Audit Bureau for approval;	对所在机构开展风险评估，制定境外分行年度审计计划，征求境外分行管理层意见，报内部审计局审批；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Implement the annual audit plan, submit audit results to the Internal Audit Bureau and report to the branch management on audit results; Promptly report to the Internal Audit Bureau on any matter that may seriously affect fulfillment of its objectives;	组织实施年度审计工作计划，并将审计工作结果报送内部审计局，并向管理层汇报。 如遇可能严重影响其目标实现的重要事项应及时报告内部审计局；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Promptly report to the Internal Audit Bureau on any inspection requirements of regulators in host countries (regions) and external auditors, the conduct and results of domestic and overseas supervisory inspections as well as the conduct and results of external audits and report to branch management on the same;	及时将所在国(地区)监管机构和外部审计的检查要求、境内外监管检查情况和结果、外部审计情况和结果报送内部审计局，并向所在分行管理层汇报；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Communicate with regulators in accordance with supervisory requirements in host countries (regions).	按照所在国(地区)监管要求，与监管机构进行沟通与交流。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. Overseas subsidiaries’ responsibilities relating to internal audit	5.境外附属机构履行内部审计的相关职责	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas subsidiaries’ responsibilities relating to internal audit mainly include the following:	境外附属机构履行内部审计的相关职责主要包括：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Set up independent internal audit roles or departments and provide necessary audit resources;	设立独立的内部审计部门或岗位，配备必要的审计资源；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Cooperate with domestic and overseas regulators, external auditors and the Internal Audit Bureau in their audit inspections;	配合境内外监管机构、外部审计和内部审计局的审计检查工作；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Implement audit findings and rectify problems detected in supervisory inspections;	落实审计发现和监管检查发现问题的整改工作；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Invite Internal Audit Bureau representatives to audit committee meetings as non-voting attendees.	邀请内部审计局列席审计委员会相关会议。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
6. Responsibilities of internal audit departments (staff) of overseas subsidiaries	6.境外附属机构内部审计部门(人员)的职责	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Responsibilities of internal audit departments (staff) of overseas subsidiaries mainly include the following:	境外附属机构内部审计部门(人员)的职责主要包括：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Independently conduct audits in accordance with supervisory requirements and internal audit standards and report on their work to the board of directors (audit committee) of their institution;	按照监管要求和内部审计准则独立开展审计工作，向所在机构董事会(审计委员会)报告工作；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
File with the Internal Audit Bureau the annual audit plan approved by the board of directors (audit committee) of their institution;	及时将经所在机构董事会(审计委员会)批准的年度审计计划报内部审计局备案；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Implement the annual audit plan, file audit results with the Internal Audit Bureau, and promptly communicate with the Internal Audit Bureau on significant matters that may seriously affect fulfillment of their objectives;	组织实施年度审计工作计划，并将审计工作结果报送内部审计局备案，如遇可能严重影响其目标实现的重要事项应及时与内部审计局沟通；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Promptly file with the Internal Audit Bureau any inspection requirements of regulators in host countries (regions) and external auditors, the conduct and results of domestic and overseas supervisory inspections as well as the conduct and results of external audits;	及时将所在国(地区)监管机构和外部审计的检查要求、境内外监管检查情况和结果、外部审计情况和结果报送内部审计局备案；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Communicate with regulators in host countries (regions) in accordance with supervisory requirements in these host countries or regions;	按照所在国(地区)监管要求，与所在国(地区)监管机构进行沟通与交流；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Accept guidance from the Internal Audit Bureau.	接受内部审计局的业务指导。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
7. Internal Audit Bureau’s management of overseas institutions	7.内部审计局对境外机构的管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Internal Audit Bureau, under leadership of the Board of Directors of ICBC, performs the duty of auditing overseas institutions and manages and guides internal audit of overseas institutions.	内部审计局在工商银行董事会领导下，履行境外机构审计职责，管理和指导境外机构内部审计工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With regard to overseas branches, the Internal Audit Bureau is responsible for carrying out vertical management to their internal audit work with a view of ensuring independence and effectiveness of internal audit;	对境外分行，内部审计局负责对其内部审计工作在业务上实行垂直管理，以保持内部审计工作的独立性和有效性；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With regard to overseas subsidiaries, the Internal Audit Bureau is responsible for providing guidance on their internal audit work with a view of enhancing their risk control capacity.	对境外附属机构，内部审计局负责对其内部审计工作进行业务指导，促进其风险控制能力的提升。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Audit Product System of Overseas Institutions	三、境外机构审计产品体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal audit of domestic and overseas institutions mainly includes the following six product lines.	境内外机构内部审计主要包括以下六大产品线。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Audit assessment of internationalization strategy execution	（一）国际化战略执行情况审计评价	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The audit assessment of internationalization strategy execution focuses on the implementation of the internationalization strategy by overseas institutions. It is mainly to objectively evaluate the clarity of objectives and direction of the internationalization strategy, collaboration with domestic institutions and progress of the cross-border Renminbi drive and promote steady improvements in international operating results of the Group.	国际化战略执行情况审计评价，重点关注境外机构落实国际化战略的执行情况，主要从国际化战略目标是否清晰、方向是否明确、境外机构内外联动工作的开展、跨境人民币的进程等方面客观评价境外机构国际化战略的执行情况，促进集团国际化经营业绩的稳步提升。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
