This audit product applies to all overseas branches and subsidiaries.	这一审计产品适用于所有境外分行和境外附属机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Internal control assessment	（二）内部控制评价	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal control assessment of overseas institutions refers to comprehensive assessment of the effectiveness of corporate governance, processes and IT control of overseas institutions that are conducted by the internal control assessment department of ICBC.	境外机构的内部控制评价，是指工商银行内部控制评价部门对境外机构公司治理、流程和信息科技控制有效性所进行的综合评估活动。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This audit product applies to all overseas branches and subsidiaries.	适用于所有境外分行和境外附属机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Operation management audit	（三）经营管理审计	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Operation management audit focuses on the operations and risk management of domestic and overseas institutions. It principally applies to overseas branches.	经营管理审计，主要关注境内外机构的经营与风险管理情况，主要适用于境外分行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It is to objectively evaluate how well overseas institutions fulfill their business and development objectives, including the size of business and development, accomplishment of core targets, collaboration between overseas and domestic institutions and market share, provide recommendations on improvements and cause overseas institutions to achieve their business objectives.	从经营发展的规模、核心指标的完成、内外联动的开展、同业市场的占比等方面，客观评价境外机构经营发展目标的完成情况，提出改进建议，促进境外机构实现经营目标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iv. M&A audit	（四）并购整合审计	sample1-en-sample1-zh
M&A audit refers to assessment of measures taken by the M&A team of ICBC, relevant departments’ post-M&A integrated management of subsidiaries and post-M&A corporate governance and development strategy, risk management and internal control, operation and cultural integration of subsidiaries. It is to reveal potential risk in integration, cause ICBC and its subsidiaries to take reasonable measures and successfully meet M&A objectives.	并购整合审计是指，从工商银行并购整合团队采取的措施、相关部门对附属机构并购后的整合管理情况、并购后附属机构的公司治理与发展战略、风险管理与内部控制、经营情况、文化融合等方面进行评价，揭示整合过程中的潜在风险，促进工商银行及附属机构采取合理措施，顺利实现并购目标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This audit product applies to overseas subsidiaries.	适用于境外附属机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
v. Consolidated management audit	（五）并表管理审计	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Consolidated management audit means assessment of the environment of consolidated management, elements of consolidated management, capital adequacy ratios, large-value risk exposures and inside transactions for the purpose of implementing the CBRC audit requirements regarding group-wide consolidated management and maintaining ongoing monitoring of risk management in group-wide consolidated management. It is to objectively reflect ICBC’s current situation of group-wide consolidated management, reveal potential effects of subsidiary risks on the business safety of ICBC and cause group-wide consolidated management to improve continuously.	并表管理审计是指，为落实银监会对集团并表管理审计的要求，持续关注集团并表管理风险管理，从并表管理环境、并表管理内容、资本充足率、大额风险暴露、内部交易等方面进行评价，客观反映工商银行在集团范围内实施并表管理的现状，揭示附属机构风险对工商银行运营安全的潜在影响，促进集团并表管理工作的不断完善。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This audit product applies to overseas subsidiaries.	适用于境外附属机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vi. Overseas institution executive term-end audit	（六）境外机构高管人员离任审计	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Overseas institution executive term-end audit (“term-end audit”) means independent review, assurance and assessment of the in-tenure performance of duties (including business management activities, internal control management and developments of the business in their charge) by executives of overseas institutions who leave their current roles. It is conducted by the Internal Audit Bureau in accordance with the Term-end Audit Procedures for Senior Management (G.Y.F. [2009] No. 13) after receipt of the notice of term-end audit given by the Human Resources Department of the Head Office.	境外机构高管人员离任审计(以下简称“离任审计”)是指境外机构高级管理人员离开现任工作职位时，针对其任职期内履行职责的情况(包括经营管理行为、内控管理、分管业务发展状况等)所进行的独立审查、鉴证和评价的活动，是内部审计局(以下简称“内审局”)接到总行人力资源部下发的离任审计通知书后，依据《高级管理人员离任审计办法》(工银发[2009]13号)所进行的审计工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Senior management members of all institutions shall accept term-end audit prior to any promotion, transfer, removal, resignation and retirement. 	各级机构高级管理人员在办理提任、调任、转任、免职、辞职、退休等事项前，应当接受离任审计。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IV. Audit Methodology and Techniques for Overseas Institutions	四、境外机构审计方法技术	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Risk assessment	（一）风险评估	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To achieve its strategic and business objectives, a bank has to take risks.	为了实现战略目标和经营目标，银行需要承担相应的风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To mitigate, reduce, spread and transfer risk, appropriate internal controls and reasonable risk management must be put in place to control risk within an acceptable level.	为了规避、减少、分散与转移风险，必须采取适当的内部控制措施和进行科学的风险管理，将风险控制在可接受的范围内。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Model for audit risk assessment	1.审计风险评估模型	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit department is responsible for independently supervising the effectiveness of risk management and internal control of the Bank and providing a reasonable assurance for meeting overall objectives of the Bank.	内部审计部门负责独立地监督银行风险管理和内部控制的有效性，为银行整体目标的实现提供合理保障。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To ensure reasonable and effective allocation of internal audit resources, the internal audit department shall conduct internal audit based on identifying the Bank’s high-risk areas of business and weaknesses of internal control.	为了确保内部审计资源配置的合理性、有效性，内部审计部门需要在识别银行业务的高风险领域和内部控制薄弱环节的基础上，开展内部审计。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Therefore, the audit risk assessment mainly includes assessing the business risk levels and internal controls of the Bank.	因此，对银行业务风险的高低和内部控制情况进行评估构成了审计风险评估的主要内容。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The theoretical model for audit risk assessment may be expressed as follows:	审计风险评估的理论模型可以用以下公式表示：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Inherent risk = probability of risk × impact of risk	固有风险 = 风险发生可能性×风险影响程度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Residual risk = inherent risk (1－effectiveness of control)	剩余风险 = 固有风险× (1－控制有效性)	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Framework for audit risk assessment framework	2.审计风险评估框架	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Audit universe and risk universe constitute the foundation for audit risk assessment.	审计单元与风险宇宙构成了审计风险评估的基础。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
An audit universe refers to a complete product of the audited entity. It is the basic object in internal audit and audit risk assessment and the foundation for audit risk assessment.	审计单元是指被审计机构中一个完整的产品，是开展内部审计工作和审计风险评估的基本对象，是审计风险评估工作的基础。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Each audit universe is defined to have clear intent and extent and independently auditable.	每一个被定义出的审计单元均具有明确的内涵和外延并可以单独进行审计。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The intent of audit universe means the properties of audit universe, including identifiable risk factors and relatively independent control system; the extent of audit universe means the scope of institutions and businesses covered by audit universe.	其中，审计单元的内涵是指审计单元具备的性质，包括可识别的风险因素和相对独立的控制系统；审计单元的外延是指审计单元应具有的机构范围和业务范围。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Risk universe refers to the set of risks present in institutions and businesses of a bank.	风险宇宙是指存在于银行各个机构以及各类业务之中的风险集合。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Whom and what to be assessed, i.e. audit universe and risk universe, must be identified before audit risk assessment is conducted.	在明确了对谁进行评估和对哪些内容进行评估，即在明确了审计单元与风险宇宙的基础上，方可开展审计风险评估。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Audit sampling	（二）审计抽样	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Role and significance of audit sampling	1.审计抽样的意义和作用	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to effectively perform internal audit functions, avoid major omissions in internal audit, ensure the internal audit department accomplishes confirmation, supervision, review and assessment of audit targets with limited resources and arrive at an independent and objective conclusion, the internal audit staff shall select audit objects by means of audit sampling.	为了有效地履行内部审计职能，避免发生内部审计的重大遗漏，保障内部审计部门凭借有限的资源完成对审计对象的确认、监督、审查与评价，得到独立客观的评价结论，内部审计人员在选取审计客体样本时应当采用审计抽样的方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Sampling risk and audit risk	2.抽样风险与审计风险	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Sampling risk refers to the likelihood of inconsistencies between the conclusion the internal audit staff arrive at based on sampling results and the overall characteristics	抽样风险是指内部审计人员依据抽样结果得出的结论与总体特征不相符合的可能性 。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
. Sampling risk is an important factor in the examination risk of internal audit staff. If audit sampling is improper, the conclusion of sampling may derivate significantly from the actual conditions of the audited entity. A higher sampling risk will lead to a higher audit risk.	抽样风险是构成内部审计人员的检查风险的重要因素，如果应用审计抽样不当，抽样结论与被审计单位的实际情况存在较大差异，抽样风险上升，将导致审计风险上升。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
How to reduce sampling risk and further control audit risk is a core element of the audit sampling theory and methodology.	如何降低抽样风险、进而控制审计风险，这是审计抽样理论和方法的核心内容。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Audit risk refers to the likelihood of improper audit conclusion arising from the failure of internal audit staff to detect major deviations or deficiencies in operating activities and internal control of the audited entity	审计风险是指内部审计人员未能发现被审计单位经营活动及内部控制中存在的重大差异或缺陷而做出不恰当审计结论的可能性 。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
. Audit staff shall maintain due professional prudence, pay particular attention to the likelihood of material risk in the audited entity and avoid omission of any material risk where possible. A higher risk level necessitates the implementation of more detailed examination procedures and the use of a sampling method with lower sampling risk, so as to reduce the examination risk to an acceptable level.	审计人员应当保持应有的职业审慎，特别关注审计对象存在重大风险的可能性，尽量避免存在重大风险而未能发现的情况，重大风险水平越高，则应当实施更为详细的检查程序，采用抽样风险较小的抽样方法，以便将检查风险降低到可接受的水平。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Audit sampling methods	3.审计抽样方法	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Basic classification of sampling methods.	(1)抽样方法的基本分类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Audit sampling methods are generally divided between statistical sampling and non-statistical sampling.	审计抽样方法一般分为统计抽样和非统计抽样两种。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Common sampling methods.	(2)样本选取的常用方法。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Statistical sampling and non-statistical sampling are applied to auditing in a wide range of specific forms, resulting in many specific sampling methods.	统计抽样和非统计抽样的方法在审计中有着很多具体的应用，这些应用也形成了很多具体的样本选取方法。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Currently the China Internal Auditing Standards set forth five commonly used sampling methods, namely, random sampling, systemic sampling, stratified sampling, cluster sampling and haphazard sampling.	目前中国内部审计准则主要列举了5种常见的样本选取方法，分别为随机数表选样法、系统选样法、分层选样法、整群选样法及任意选样法。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Audit reporting	（三）审计报告	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal audit reporting is an important part of the internal audit process. It is a significant path towards participating in the governance process and a principal way of meeting internal audit objectives and reflecting the value of work.	内部审计报告是是内部审计工作流程的重要组成部分，是参与治理过程的重要途径，是实现内部审计工作目标和体现工作价值的主要方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Purposes of internal audit reporting	1.内部审计报告目的	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Disclosing audit findings.	（1）披露审计发现。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit report must be accurate and authentic, for any misrepresentation or inaccurate findings will render the report unreliable.	内部审计必须准确地报告事实，因为任何虚假的陈述、不准确的发现都会使报告陷入不可靠的困境。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Disclosing audit findings is intended to draw the attention of the report receiver.	披露审计发现，旨在引起接收报告者的关注。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Analyzing gaps.	（2）分析差距。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Gaps include exceptions and weaknesses.	差距包含例外情况和薄弱环节。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit report shall analyze the causes for deviation from the Bank’s strategic objectives, business objectives, reporting objectives and compliance objectives found during auditing, and also analyze gaps in corporate governance, internal control and risk management and the causes for such gaps.	内部审计报告要对审计所发现的偏离银行战略目标、经营目标、报告目标和合规目标的差距进行原因分析，对公司治理、内部控制、风险管理差距等情况以及发生差距的原因进行分析。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Providing audit recommendations.	（3）提出审计建议。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Compliance audit, risk audit and value-added audit all require internal auditors to provide useful recommendations that help the Board of Directors and the Management to achieve overall objectives and unleash the value added role for the organization.	无论合规性审计、风险性审计还是增值性审计，均需要内部审计师提出帮助银行董事会和管理层实现整体目标的有益建议，实现对组织的增值作用。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
For any obvious violation of laws or regulations detected, an opinion for quick correction must be provided. However, audit recommendations must include necessary feasibility analysis, including the cost efficiency of recommended measures.	发现明显的违法违规行为，一定要提出迅速纠正的意见，但对审计建议则要进行必要的可行性分析，包括实施建议措施的成本和效益分析。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Types of internal audit reports	2.内部审计报告类型	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internal audit reports of commercial banks may be classified into different types according to the nature of internal audit, user of report and objectives of auditing.	商业银行内部审计报告，根据内部审计活动性质、报告使用者、审计目标等的差异，可分为不同的类型。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Business audit report and audit work report.	（1）业务审计报告和审计工作报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The business audit report is a report the internal audit body issues in connection with the adequacy, legality and effectiveness of risk management, internal control, corporate governance and operating activities of the audited entity after conducting necessary audit procedures over the audited business in accordance with the audit plan.	业务审计报告是内部审计机构根据审计计划对被审计业务实施必要的审计程序后，就被审计单位风险管理、内部控制、公司治理和经营活动的适当性、合法性和有效性出具的报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The compliance, risk and value-added audit reports described below as well as interim and final audit reports are all business audit reports.	后面所指的合规型、风险型、增值型审计报告，以及中期和最终审计报告，都是指业务审计报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The audit work report is a written document produced by the internal audit body to comprehensively reflect the performance and overall effectiveness of internal audit work during a designated period.	审计工作报告是内部审计机构综合反映一定时期内部审计工作开展情况和总体效果所产生的书面文件。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The audit work report may be quarterly, interim or annual.	审计工作报告主要包括季度、中期和年度报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Compliance audit report, risk audit report and value-added audit report.	（2）合规性审计报告、风险性审计报告和增值性审计报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The compliance audit risk is an output of the compliance audit conducted by the internal audit body. This type of audit report will still be used for compliance investigation of emergencies and particular matters and implementation of external regulatory requirements.	合规性审计报告是内部审计执行合规性审计任务生成的审计报告，一些突发事件和特定事项的合规情况调查，以及落实外部监管要求，仍将使用这一报告类型。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The risk audit report is the mainstream audit report at present. All reports on the auditing of key businesses and comprehensive audit assessment are risk-based.	风险性审计报告是当前审计报告的主流，重要业务的审计和全面的审计评价等都是以风险为基础编制审计报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The value-added audit report places extra emphasis on enhancing the shareholders’ value fundamentally.	增值性审计报告更加重视从根本上提升股东价值。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Audit advisory services for investment, assessment of strategy execution, performance audit, function audit and process audit are all trials of this type of report.	投资的审计咨询活动、战略执行情况评价、效益审计、功能审计、流程审计等都是这一类型报告的有益尝试。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Interim audit report and final audit report.	（3）中期审计报告和最终审计报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The final audit report must be prepared after an audit project is ended.	审计项目应当在终结审计后编制最终审计报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If the audit period is too long, emergencies give rise to special requirements or the audited items are extraordinarily complicated, the interim audit report shall be prepared and submitted according to the Management’s requirements and internal audit needs.	如果存在审计周期过长、突发事件引起特殊要求、被审计项目内容特别庞杂等情况时应当根据组织适当管理层的要求和内部审计工作的需要编制并报送中期审计报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Use of audit report	3.审计报告的运用	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit report shall be submitted to the Board of Directors and its Audit Committee and the Senior Management.	内部审计报告应当报送董事会及其审计委员会和高级管理层。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After finishing the audit of an ICBC branch or subsidiary, the internal audit department may issue an audit opinion to the audited entity.	内部审计部门完成对工商银行分支机构的审计任务后，可以形成审计意见书发送被审计的分支机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
When detecting any doubtful points during risk monitoring analysis or off-site audit analysis, the internal audit department may issue an internal audit inquiry to the audited entity for its clarification.	内部审计部门可以对风险监测分析和非现场审计分析发现的疑点形成内部审计质询书，发送被审计机构，要求其解答。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The internal audit body shall use internal audit reports as a tool to coordinate different expectations and, through recommendations included in reports, improve the organization’s capability and reduce limitations on auditors’ access to information and audit effectiveness.	内部审计应当将审计报告作为协调不同期望的手段，通过报告建议改进组织的能力并减少审计师在获取信息和实现审计效果方面受到的限制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The head of the internal audit body shall consider their relations with other control and supervisory departments (risk management, compliance, security, legal, morality, environment and external audit) and help them report to the audit committee on material risks and controls.	审计机构负责人应当考虑他们与其它控制与监督部门(风险管理、合规、保卫、法律、道德、环境、外部审计)的关系，并帮助其向审计委员会报告重大风险和控制问题。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Foundation for audit report	4.审计报告的基础	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The basic work that has a decisive impact on the formation and quality of an audit report includes working paper, audit findings and communication.	对审计报告形成和确保报告质量具有决定影响的基础性工作是工作底稿、审计发现和沟通。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Ineffectiveness or disorderliness of such work will immediately translate into inherent inadequacies of the audit report, in which case the audit report is doomed to fail no matter what remedial actions are taken subsequently. In contrast, audit findings that are highly relevant to the audit purpose, working paper that is complete, detailed, clear and consistent as well as proper and thorough communication will lead to an easier process of audit report preparation, increasing the likelihood of producing a high-standard report.	这些工作的无效无序将直接导致审计报告的先天不足，之后无论采用什么补救措施，都不会改变审计报告的失败命运；相反，与审计目的高度相关的审计发现、完整翔实且清晰统一的工作底稿、恰当而充分的沟通，将会使审计报告编制过程更加轻松，并且易于诞生一份高水平的报告。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
CHAPTER THREE IT SYSTEMS AND REGULATIONS OF ICBC	第三章 工商银行信息科技系统与制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section One Introduction to the IT Hierarchy of ICBC	第一节 工商银行信息科技体系介绍	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Since its foundation, ICBC has always adhered to the principle of “technology-driven” and “technology-led” development, pushed forward with corporate IT development and continuously improved core competitiveness of the Bank.	建行以来，中国工商银行始终遵循“科技兴行”、“科技引领”发展方针，大力推动企业信息化建设，持续提升我行的核心竞争力。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
On September 1, 1999, ICBC launched the “9991” Program (data concentration program), a milestone in its IT development history that opens up a new era of centralized technology development.	1999年9月1日，中国工商银行启动了信息化建设历史上具有里程碑意义的工程——“9991”工程（数据集中工程），从而开启了集约化科技体系建设的新时代。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
During ten years, a series of major IT projects have been completed, including data concentration, integration of data centers, restructuring of core application systems and host disaster recovery; CB2000, NOVA, NOVA+ and other core application systems were researched and developed independently; and the system of centralized IT management has been set up. These achievement reach a leading position domestically and an advanced level internationally, vigorously promote the bank-wide innovation and reform and represent great milestones in the information-based building of ICBC.	十年间，完成了数据集中、数据中心整合、核心应用系统重构、主机灾备等一系列重大科技工程，自主研发了CB2000、NOVA 、NOVA+等核心应用系统，建立了集约化的信息科技管理体系，保持了国内行业的领先优势，达到国际先进水平，有力推动了全行业务创新和经营改革的进程，谱写出中国工商银行信息化建设的辉煌篇章。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Status Quo of Science & Technology R&D and Operating Capacity	一、科技研发运行能力现状	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Current situation of R&D capacity	1.研发能力现状	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has established an R&D system that mainly relies on the software development center, supplemented by branches.	工商银行已建立起软件开发中心为主，各分行为辅的研发项目研发体系。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Towards the development objectives and central tasks of ICBC, R&D and promotion of application products have been accelerated, the “1031” Program has been substantially completed, new breakthroughs are encouraged in innovation in key areas of business, and a variety of leading products have been launched, including personal wealth management, bank cards and E-banking, providing strong supports for business development and delivering good results.	围绕工商银行发展目标和中心任务，加快应用产品研发推广，基本完成“1031”工程建设，支持重点业务领域应用创新的新突破，推出个人理财、银行卡、电子银行等领域的一系列拳头产品，为业务发展提供了有力支持，取得了良好成效。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The number of patent grants obtained by the Bank has increased steadily year by year, reaching 183 as of May 2012.	我行获得国家专利授权数量逐年稳步提升，截至2012年5月,共获国家专利授权183项。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Current situation of production and operating capacity	2.生产运行现状	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has established a framework of IT systems in which the Data Center (Shanghai) serves as the operating center and branches are client terminals.	工商银行已经建立以数据中心（上海）为生产中心、各分行为客户终端的信息系统运行架构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, to intensify system stability and improve disaster tolerance, ICBC has realized local and inter-city backup for core business platforms of the host. Local synchronous backup for business data is provided at the Data Center (Shanghai), and an inter-city disaster recovery center has been established at the Data Center (Beijing). The recovery time objective (RTO) of less than 2 hours and the recovery point objective (RPO) of less than 2 minutes are met.	同时，为加强系统稳定性，提高灾难容错能力，经过多年建设，工商银行已经实现了主机核心业务平台的同城和异地双备份，即在数据中心（上海）同城建立了生产数据的同步备份，在数据中心（北京）建有异地灾难备份中心，实现RTO（恢复时间目标）小于2小时、RPO（恢复点目标）小于2分钟的设计目标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The disaster recovery systems of ICBC for its core business reach Grade 6 of the SHARE－92 national standard, the first in China’s banking industry.	工商银行核心业务灾备体系在国内同业中首家均达到国际SHARE－92的第6级标准。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

(1) Function as the bank-wide production and operating center responsible for central maintenance and management of the Bank’s operations and ensure continuity and stability of the Bank’s IT systems;	（1）全行生产运行中心, 履行全行生产运行统一维护和管理职能，确保全行信息系统的持续稳定运行；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Central planning and management of bank-wide disaster recovery; and	（2）全行灾备的统一规划和管理；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Ensure security and stability of third-party systems and branch systems under custody of ICBC.	（3）确保工商银行托管的第三方系统以及代管的分行系统的安全稳定运行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. Data Center (Beijing)	5.数据中心（北京）	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Acceptance and adaptability test;	（1）验收和适应性测试；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Planning and technical management of the basic architecture, including systems, networks, equipment and information security; and	（2）系统、网络、设备、信息安全等基础架构的规划和技术管理；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Responsible for bank-wide technology management and R&D of automatic technology platforms.	（3）承担全行科技管理、系统自动化技术平台的研发工作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

(1) Development of application products of the Head Office;	（1）总行应用产品开发；	sample1-en-sample1-zh

(1) Branch-wide operation;	（1）辖内生产运行；	sample1-en-sample1-zh

(4) Branch marketing supports.	（4）支持分行市场营销。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Science & Technology Management System	三、科技管理体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Science & technology rules and regulations	（一）科技制度体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In 2002, the Head Office formulated the Administrative Regulation on the Production and Operation of Information Systems. After years of continuous optimization and improvement, a stable framework has been established under the Regulations on Information Technology Management, including planning, preparation, revision, review, publication, training and implementation of rules and regulations.	2002年，总行组织制定了《信息系统生产运行管理制度》，并经过多年来不断例行化的持续优化和完善，已形成了较为稳定的《信息科技管理制度》体系架构，建立起了制度规划、编制、修订、评审、发布、培训、执行等管理过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Regulations on Information Technology Management mainly covers information system management, project management as well as security and general management, and is classified into administrative measures, implementation rules, management handbooks, workbooks and operation manuals.	《信息科技管理制度》主要涵盖信息系统运行管理、项目管理、安全及综合管理三大领域，分为管理办法、实施细则、管理手册、工作手册、操作手册等类型。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The bank-wide Regulations on Information Technology Management (2012 edition) consists of 34 administrative measures, 60 implementation rules, 52 management handbooks, totaling 146. It was released to the whole bank in early January 2012 and became effective on 1 March 2012.	2012版全行性《信息科技管理制度》共包括34个管理办法、60个实施细则、52个管理手册，合计146个，已于2012年1月初向全行发布，并于2012年3月1日起正式执行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Regulations on Information Technology Management would be revised annually in principle. Any adjustments made between annual revisions will be released by the Head Office in the form of interpretations. Meanwhile, notices, guidelines and instructions will be issued from time to time according to relevant work requirements.	《信息科技管理制度》原则上每年集中修订一次，执行过程中需要调整的内容，总行以制度条款解释说明的形式进行发布，同时还会结合相关工作要求不定期地下发有针对性的通知、指引、提示等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Technical standards	（二）技术规范体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Technical standards of ICBC are grouped into seven categories: application, information, security, system, network, infrastructure and general standards. The specification system three for each category includes tier-2 and tier-3 breakdowns.	工商银行的技术规范总体上分为应用、信息、安全、系统、网络、基础设施、通用七大类，每大类的规范体系树中根据各分类属性进行了第二层和第三层的细分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. The application category is further divided into design and development, testing and maintenance.	1．应用大类下分为设计开发、测试、运维。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Design and development are subdivided into general, host and development platform; testing is subdivided into test design and test technique. Maintenance is subdivided into general, host and open platform.	设计开发划分为综合、主机、开发平台；测试划分为测试设计、测试技术；运维划分为综合、主机、开放平台。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. The information category is divided into data architecture, information management and data exchange.	2．信息大类分为数据架构、信息管理、数据交换。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Data architecture is subdivided into data model & database design and data distribution. Information management is subdivided into data life cycle management, data quality management and metadata management.	数据架构划分为数据模型与数据库设计、数据分布；信息管理划分为数据生命周期管理、数据质量管理、元数据管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. The security category is divided into general, application, system and network.	3．安全大类下，分为综合、应用、系统、网络。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The general sub-category is subdivided into classified protection. Application or system is subdivided into host and open platform.	综合下有等级保护；应用、系统下划分为主机、开放平台。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. The system category is divided into host and open platform.	4．系统大类下，分为主机、开放平台。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The host or open platform is subdivided into storage, monitoring, automation and general.	主机、开放平台下划分为：存储、监控、自动化、综合。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. The network category is divided into architecture design, general technology and resource allocation.	5．网络大类下，分为架构设计、通用技术、资源分配。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Architecture design is subdivided into network security area design, network structure design, network routing design as well as comprehensive wiring and communication line design. General technology is subdivided into basic network design, application network technology and network value-added service technology. Resource allocation is subdivided into network equipment naming and IP address allocation.	架构设计划分为网络安全区域设计、网络结构设计、网络路由设计、综合布线及通信线路设计；通用技术划分为基础网络设计、应用网络技术、网络增值服务技术；资源分配划分为网络设备命名、IP地址分配。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
6. The infrastructure category is subdivided into computer room, equipment and outlets.	6．基础设施大类下分为机房、设备和网点。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
7. The general category includes the Code for Preparation of Technical Standards and the Overall Framework of Technical Standards. The tier-2 division is not made.	7．通用大类下包括《技术规范编写规范》和《技术规范总体框架》，未做第二层划分。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Information security	（三）信息安全体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has gradually established an ICBC-specific system of information security regulations and standards according to the E-banking developments and drawing upon information security standards and best practices at home and abroad, so as to guide and motivate ICBC information security system development and protect the security of information and information systems.	工商银行从银行电子化建设的实际出发，借鉴国内外的信息安全标准和业界最佳实践，已逐步构建了一套具有工商银行特色的信息安全制度和规范体系，以指导和推动工商银行信息安全体系建设，保障信息及信息系统安全。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Figure 3-2 Information Security Framework of ICBC	图3－2 中国工商银行信息安全体系框架	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The information security framework of ICBC, as illustrated in Figure 3-2, is three-tiered: basic security standards, security management regulations and security technical standards. Standards and regulations relating to each of the three tiers are described briefly below.	工商银行的信息安全体系如图3-2所示，包括基础安全规范、安全管理制度和安全技术规范三个层面，以下就这三个层面涉及的规范和制度内容进行简单的介绍。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Basic security standards	1.基础安全规范	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Basic security standards are the foundation for the information security framework of ICBC and provide guidance on formulation of management regulations and technical standards relating to information security.	基础安全规范是构建工商银行信息安全体系架构的基础，是为相关信息安全管理制度和技术规范的制定起指导性作用的基础规范。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Basic security standards are principally the Security Standards for Information and Information Systems and the Implementation Standards for Classified Security Protection of Information and Information Systems.	主要包括《信息及信息系统安全体系规范》和《信息及信息系统安全等级保护实施规范》两个规范。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Information security management regulations.	2.信息安全管理制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Information security management regulations, under the guidance of basic security standards, clarify the organizational structure, roles and responsibilities and security management process requirements relating to information and information systems.	信息安全管理制度，是在基础安全规范的指导下，明确了信息及信息系统安全管理的各级组织架构、职责和安全管理过程要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Information security management regulations principally include the Management Measures on Security of Information and Information Systems, the Implementation Rules for Information Security Management of Application Systems, the Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Systems, the Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Internet Access and the Implementation Rules for Anti-leak Management of Client-side Information.	信息安全管理制度主要包括《信息及信息系统安全管理办法》和《应用系统信息保护管理实施细则》、《客户端系统安全管理实施细则》、《客户端互联网访问安全管理实施细则》、《客户端信息防泄漏管理实施细则》等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Head Office also formulated the Implementation Rules for Security Management of Information Systems and relevant management handbooks.	总行还在信息科技专业制定了《信息系统安全管理实施细则》及相应的管理手册。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Security technical standards	3.安全技术规范	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Security technical standard, under the guidance of basic security standard, are technical standard specializing in security classification, computer room security, host system security, open platform system security, network security and application security.	安全技术规范，是在基础安全规范的指导下，针对安全定级、机房安全、主机系统安全、开放平台系统安全、网络安全和应用安全等方面分专业细化形成的安全技术规范。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Two Introduction to FOVA	第二节 FOVA系统介绍	sample1-en-sample1-zh
FOVA is a comprehensive business processing system independently developed by ICBC in line with its strategy for overseas business development and for the purpose of improving overseas institutions’ business processing capacity.	FOVA系统是工商银行根据本行境外机构业务发展策略，为提升境外机构业务处理能力，自主研发的一套功能丰富、技术先进、运行安全、维护方便的综合业务处理系统。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
FOVA is characterized by broad-ranging functions, advanced technology, security of operation and convenience of maintenance. Designers of FOVA took into full account the business characteristics of overseas institutions. Its functions cover substantially all operations of ICBC overseas institutions.	FOVA系统在设计时充分考虑了境外机构业务特色，功能基本上覆盖了工商银行境外机构所有业务处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Systems mainly include core banking sub-systems based on the host architecture and various front-end systems, terminal systems, channel systems and other auxiliary systems based on peripheral open platforms.	系统主要包括基于主机架构的核心银行子系统以及基于外围开放平台的各种前置系统、终端系统、渠道系统以及其他业务辅助系统。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This section will provide a description of the FOVA architecture and functions.	本节将对FOVA的系统架构以及系统功能进行介绍。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Architecture of FOVA	一、FOVA系统架构	sample1-en-sample1-zh
FOVA builds on the core system based on the host platform. Other peripheral systems are based mainly on UNIX, Windows and other open platforms and communicate via gateway systems and the host platform. The gateway handles communication and data conversion between host and open platforms.	FOVA系统是围绕基于主机平台的核心系统建立起来的，其他外围应用系统主要是以UNIX、Windows等开放平台为基础，并通过网关系统和主机平台进行通讯，由网关完成主机和开放平台之间的通讯和数据转换。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
FOVA supports overseas retail and wholesale banking, includes complete technical and business platforms and provides a wide array of banking service delivery channels.	FOVA系统支持境外零售业务和批发业务，建立了完整的技术平台和业务平台，提供丰富的银行业务受理渠道。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As FOVA and the domestic NOVA system use the uniform technical architecture, domestic and overseas host application systems can be interconnected to provide a solid foundation for domestic-overseas collaboration of ICBC.	由于FOVA系统和境内使用的NOVA系统采用统一的技术体系架构，可以实现境内外主机应用系统之间的互连互通，为工行境内外机构联动业务的发展提供了坚实的基础。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The two systems allow synchronized maintenance of parameter tables, synchronized updating of domestic and overseas exchange rates, remittance between domestic and overseas branches, global cash management and agency account opening between domestic and overseas institutions.	两者之间可以进行参数表的同步维护、境内外外汇牌价的同步更新、境内外分行之间的汇款业务处理、全球现金管理业务办理、境内外互相代理开户等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
FOVA applications include core banking system, documentation system, treasury market business system, Internet banking system, mobile banking system, bank card system, credit management system, customer marketing system, customer relationship management system, customer reconciliation system and operational risk monitoring system. FOVA provides a multi-time zone, multi-language, multi-home currency, multinational and 7×24-hour system architecture.	FOVA系统应用包括核心银行系统、单证业务系统、资金市场业务系统、网上银行系统、电话银行系统、银行卡系统、信贷管理系统、客户营销系统、客户关系管理系统、客户对账系统、操作风险监控系统等，具有支持多时区、多语言、多本币、多国情和7×24小时不间断运行的系统架构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
FOVA and NOVA share equipment and the operating system, but use different databases and application middleware. Therefore, from the logical and partially physical perspectives, FOVA and NOVA are independent of each other.	FOVA系统和NOVA系统共用设备和操作系统，但数据库和应用中间件是进行了区分，所以从逻辑上和局部的物理上来看，FOVA系统和NOVA系统是相互独立，互不影响的。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
FOVA builds on the IBM mainframe platform, employs large-scale relational database and middleware, supports massive parallel processing and centralized data storage and processing, and meanwhile adopts the load balancing technology, providing an efficient and stable operating platform that can process massive business transactions at the same time and serving as a stable and flexible technical platform for overseas business expansion of ICBC.	FOVA系统基于IBM大型机平台，采用大规模关系型数据库及中间件，支持大规模并行处理和数据集中存储以及处理，同时还采用负载均衡技术，使得系统具备高效、稳定的运行平台，具有同时处理大量业务交易的能力，为工商银行境外机构的业务拓展搭建了一个稳定、灵活的技术平台。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Functions of FOVA	二、FOVA系统功能	sample1-en-sample1-zh
FOVA supports customer information management, accounting, deposit, loan, remittance, bank card, precious metals, derivatives, global markets, international settlement and trade finance and agency services, covering front-office, middle-office and back-office activities. The system provides over-the-counter (OTC), ATM, POS, Internet banking, telephone banking, self-service banking and other service delivery channels and offers such auxiliary features as generating reports and statements.	FOVA系统支持客户信息管理、会计核算、存款、贷款、汇款、银行卡、贵金属业务、衍生产品业务、金融市场、国际结算及贸易融资、代理业务等各项业务处理，覆盖银行前中后台业务管理，提供柜面、ATM、POS、网上银行、电话银行、自助渠道等服务渠道，并具备生成业务报表和客户对账单的辅助业务功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It also supports parameter setting features, flexibly meets differentiated functional requirements and allows different institutions to realize different functions through parameter setting with respect to interest accrual method, interest settlement cycle, fee calculation method and billing period, taxation method and taxation cycle.	系统支持参数化设置特性，灵活实现对系统差异化功能要求，不同机构可以通过参数设置实现计息方式和结息周期、费用计算方式和收费周期、计税方式和计税周期等方面不同的业务功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
FOVA has basically established a comprehensive business processing system that provides relatively complete functions.	FOVA已基本建成一个业务功能相对完善的综合业务处理系统。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Core banking system of FOVA	（一）FOVA核心银行系统	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The core banking system of FOVA consists of online business features and batch business features.	FOVA核心银行系统可以分为联机业务功能与批量业务功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The online business features include functional modules such as customer information processing, internal accounting management processing, deposit processing, loan processing, remittance processing and bank card processing; the batch business features include batch business processing and report processing modules. Main features are described below by business modules.	其中联机业务功能包括客户信息业务处理、会计内部管理业务处理、存款业务处理、贷款业务处理、汇款业务处理、银行卡业务处理等功能模块；批量业务功能包括批量业务处理、报表处理等功能模块，下面按不同业务模块对主要功能进行介绍。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Customer information	1.客户信息	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The customer information module of FOVA represents an archival database established for customers that maintain accounts with the Bank and for tellers of the Bank.	FOVA系统客户信息模块是为在银行开立账户，办理各类业务的客户以及本行柜员建立的档案数据库。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
By recording comprehensive, complete and detailed customer information, this module provides a reasonable basis for decision making with respect to accounting and management of the Bank’s operating activities.	它通过综合、完整、详细地记录客户信息，为银行经营活动的核算和管理提供科学合理的决策依据。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Basic customer information includes basic data provided by customers during account opening and records on subsequent customer activities with the Bank.	客户基本信息包括客户在银行开立账户时提供的基本信息资料和日后在银行办理各类业务过程中形成的活动记录。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to the type of customer, it is divided into corporate information module and personal information module.	按办理业务的主体不同，可分为公司信息模块和个人信息模块。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The customer information module is a basic business module of FOVA that provides basic customer data for other business functions.	客户信息模块是FOVA系统的基础业务模块，为其他业务功能提供基础客户信息数据。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Accounting	2.会计核算	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As the core module of the system, the accounting module provides general ledger accounting and ledger accounting features, offers flexible provisioning methods and periods and supports different accounting requirements of many countries.	会计核算部分作为系统的核心模块，提供总帐核算和分户核算的功能，灵活的计提方式和周期，支持全球多个国家不同的会计核算处理要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It can realize such functions as teller management, parameter management, accounting elements management, cashier management, opening and closing of internal off-balance-sheet accounts, maintenance and management of internal off-balance-sheet accounts, internal account transfer, off-balance-sheet account settlement, log management, account reconciliation & check, and inquiry and management of general ledger gain/loss inquiry management. This module also supports daily calculation of exchange gains/losses, provisioning and conversion of foreign currency gains/losses to home currency.	它可以实现柜员管理、参数管理、会计要素管理、现金出纳管理、内部表外户开销户、内部户表外户维护管理、内部户转账、表外户结算交易、日志管理、轧账、总账损益查询管理等功能，并支持每日汇兑损益计算、计提和外币损益结转本币的处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Deposit	3.存款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The deposit module supports deposit products and agency products processing.	存款模块支持存款产品和代理产品处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The deposit module of FOVA includes demand deposits, settlement (check) accounts, time deposits, small savings for lump-sum withdrawal, principal deposit and interest withdrawal, call deposit, Elite Club Card, Peony E-era Card and joint accounts. It offers such agreement products as bank statement, balance transfer and adjustment, agency services, negotiated amount transfer and Easy Mortgage, supports account overdraft and freezing, supports branch-specific setting of account number rules, supports reserved account numbers and also provides the notes management module.	FOVA系统存款业务模块包括活期储蓄存款、结算(支票)账户、定期存款、零存整取、存本取息、通知存款、理财金卡、牡丹e时代卡、联名账户等各类业务产品的处理，提供对账单、余额调剂、代理业务、协定金额转账、智按易等协议产品，支持账户透支、冻结等功能，支持按分行设置满足本地需要的帐号规则，支持预留账号，同时还提供了票据管理模块。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Loan	4.贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The loan module of FOVA includes bilateral loans, syndicated loans (with ICBC as participants), consumer loans and housing loans, provides interface with the credit management system and implements rigid control of credit risk.	FOVA系统贷款业务模块提供双边贷款、银团贷款(我行作为参贷行)、消费贷款、住房贷款等业务品种办理，具有与信贷管理系统对接的功能，实现了信贷风险刚性控制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This module supports general loans and unsecured loans and provides such features as loan disbursement and repayment, downgrading to bad debts, write-off of bad debts and reversal of accounting operations, as well as treatment of pledge and mortgage. In addition to traditional equal principal and equal amount payments, this module also supports diversified repayment methods such as irregular repayment schedules that allow self-defined payments in any amounts at any time. This module supports loan refinance, downgrading to bad debts, write-off of bad debts and recovery of bad debts.	支持普通贷款和授信贷款，提供贷款发放、归还、转呆坏账、呆账核销、账务冲正等功能，提供质押和抵押的处理；支持多种还款方式，除传统的等本、等额外，还支持自定义任意时间任意金额的不规则还款计划；支持贷款转按揭、转呆坏账、呆坏账核销及归还贷款呆坏账等处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In the meantime, it also supports future disbursement, postponed repayment and other individualized services, and offers loan sales, fund aid and other business processing methods.	同时还支持远期放款、延期供款等个性化的业务处理要求，提供售卖贷款、资助资款等业务处理方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. Remittance	5.汇款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The remittance module of FOVA supports inward and outward remittance in RMB and foreign currencies between overseas branches and domestic branches of ICBC, other overseas branches and other banks, supports advance FX settlement remittance, remittance reservation and intra-system cross-border remittance. It also supports promissory notes, drafts, notes purchase and clean collection.	FOVA系统汇款模块支持境外分行与工行系统内国内分行、其他境外分行、以及系统外其他银行之间外币及人民币的汇出和汇入汇款处理，支持预结汇汇款、预约汇款、系统内跨境汇款等业务处理，同时支持本票、汇票、买票、光票托收、光票代收等票据业务的处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The intra-system remittance of ICBC allows point-to-point processing without routing message through the SWIFT system. Furthermore, fund clearing is automatically conducted in sync with message processing, which significantly cuts manual processing steps, increases remittance processing speed and reduces remittance costs.	工商银行系统内汇款实现了点对点处理，报文不需要经过SWIFT系统，而且资金清算随报文处理同步自动完成，不仅大大减少了人工处理环节，提升了汇款处理速度，同时也节约了汇款成本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The system also supports the needs of differentiated automatic transfer between different overseas institutions based on parameter setting.	系统同时还支持按参数设置灵活实现不同境外机构的差异化自动转汇需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
6. Debit Card	6.借记卡	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The bank card service module of FOVA enables debit card issuance and acquiring for China UnionPay and local banking organizations, supports issuance of registered debit cards and unregistered debit cards and supports issuance of ICBC (Macau) UnionPay dual-currency chip cards. Its main features include card issuance, OTC and ATM inquiry, OTC and ATM deposits and withdrawal, POS-based consumption, POS preauthorization and POS-based product return. The system also supports overseas-domestic collaboration, through which the debit card issued by overseas branches may be used at counters, ATMs and POS terminals of domestic branches and other overseas branches for deposits, withdrawals and consumptions.	FOVA系统银行卡业务模块实现了银联及当地银行组织借记卡的发卡和收单功能，支持发行记名借记卡和非记名借记卡，支持发行工银澳门银联芯片双币卡，主要实现功能包括发卡、柜面和ATM查询、柜面和ATM存取款、POS消费、POS预授权、POS退货等，系统同时还支持境内外联动业务处理，境外分行发行的借记卡可以在国内和其他境外分行柜面、ATM、POS等渠道进行存取款和消费等交易。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
7. Batch processing	7.批量	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The core system of FOVA provides day-end, month-end and year-end batch processing features. Day-end batch processing mainly includes analysis of logs, retrospective bookkeeping for internal accounts, upgrading the general ledger balance and accrual amounts, provisioning, exchange gain/loss settlement and carry-over, conversion of foreign currency gain/loss to home currency, generation of internal account details, trial balancing, general ledger and ledger reconciliation and generation of bank statements and day-end report data. The month-end batch processing mainly includes upgrading general ledger and generating month-end report data. Year-end batch processing mainly includes upgrading general ledger, year-end final accounts (exchange gain/loss carry-over and profit/loss carry-over) and generation of year-end report data.	FOVA核心系统提供了日终、月终、年终的批量处理功能，日终批量主要是解析日志、补记内部户、更新总账余额和发生额、计提、汇兑损益结算和结转、外币损益折算本币、内部户明细生成、试算平衡、总分核对、对账单及日终报表数据生成等功能，月终批量主要是更新总账、生成月终统计报表数据等功能，年终主要是更新总账、年终决算(汇兑损益结转、损益结转)、年终报表数据生成等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to runtime, batch processing is divided into day-time batch processing, day-end batch processing, periodic batch processing, provisioning batch processing and interest accrual batch processing.	按照运行时间，批量主要可以分为日间批量、日终批量、周期批量、计提批量、计息批量等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
8. Reconciliation with customers	8.客户对账	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The customer reconciliation module of FOVA provides reconciliation by customer (integrated bank statement) or designated account. It also supports provision of temporary bank statements to customers.	FOVA系统客户对账模块提供按客户对账（综合对账单）、按指定账户对账两种方式，同时还支持向客户提供临时对账单。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The integrated statement includes balances of all accounts (full amount display for joint accounts), transaction details, reminder to maturity and reminder to overdue payments during the reconciliation period.	客户综合对账单内容包括签订客户信息下对账周期内所有账户的余额（联名账户全额显示）、明细及定期到期提醒、欠费提醒等信息。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The designated account statement includes the balance of designated account (full amount display for joint accounts), transaction details, reminder to maturity and reminder to overdue payments during the reconciliation period.	指定账户对账单内容包括协议里的对账账户在对账周期内的余额（联名账户全额显示）、明细及定期到期提醒、欠费提醒等信息。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The temporary statement may be issued on the current day. The start date of reconciliation may be any day in the past, and the closing day of reconciliation should not be later than the current system date.	临时对账单可以实现当日出单，对账起始日可以为历史任何一天，对账截止日需不大于当前系统日期。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It is not subject to reconciliation period restrictions, providing convenience for flexible inquiry about historical records.	不受对账周期限制，方便客户灵活查询历史记录。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
9. Reports	9.报表	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The report module of FOVA provides a variety of business reports, including basic accounting reports (e.g. balance statement and daily balance), transaction list reports (e.g. list of authorized transactions, list of general ledger-ledger reconciliation errors and list of large-sum deposits and withdrawals), business statistics reports (e.g. foreign exchange trading statement and time deposit statement), customer receipt reports (interest advice and automatic debiting receipts), monthly reports, quarterly reports, semiannual reports and annual reports.	FOVA系统报表模块提供了各种业务报表，包括日常使用的基本会计报表(例如余额表、日计表等)、业务清单报表(例如授权交易清单、总分核对错误清单、大额存取款业务清单等)、业务统计报表(例如外汇买卖交易量统计表、定期存款统计表等)、客户回单报表(利息通知单、自动扣费的回单等)、月报表、季报表、半年报表、年报表等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Some accounting reports also support display by local items, regulatory items and Head Office items. 	部分会计报表还支持按本地科目、监管科目、总行科目三套不同的科目体系分别展现。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Parameter management	（二）参数管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The parameter management system mainly has three functions: system management, parameter inquiry and maintenance, and statistical monitoring.	参数管理系统的主要功能包括系统管理、参数查询与维护和统计监控三部分功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
System management functions are operated by the system administration tellers of the Head Office and provide such features as parameter list management, data dictionary management, institution inquiry, teller inquiry, error code management and day-end service management.	系统管理功能由总行系统管理柜员操作，提供了参数表管理、数据字典管理、机构查询、柜员查询、错误代码管理、日终服务管理等功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The parameter inquiry and maintenance function is the principal function of the overseas parameter management system, serving as the Bank’s primary means to maintain host parameters of most core banking systems.	参数查询与维护功能是境外参数管理系统的主要功能，作为全行维护大部分核心银行系统主机参数的主要途径。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Parameter maintenance adopts a three-step approval process (application, examination and approval), which provides good security for parameter maintenance.	参数维护采用申请、复核、审批三级审核流程，为参数维护提供良好的安全性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The statistical monitoring function, operated by the monitoring tellers of the Head Office and overseas branches, includes statistical features and monitoring features. Specifically, statistical features include statistics on parameter list changes, statistics on teller workload and maintenance quality, statistics on errors and generation of month-end statements download. Monitoring features include process monitoring, teller monitoring and monitoring of key parameter lists.	统计监控功能由总行和境外分行监控柜员操作，包括统计和监控两部分功能，其中统计包括参数表变动情况统计、柜员业务量和维护质量统计、错误统计以及生成月终报表下载等交易；监控包括流程监控、柜员监控和重点参数表监控。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Credit card system	（三）信用卡系统	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The credit card system of ICBC, based on the host bank card system, provides program sharing and specific service features through the common business module and the specific business module, enabling credit card/account management, application approval management, authorization management, transaction management, chargeback/retrieval management and credit card authorization management.	中国工商银行信用卡系统以主机银行卡系统为基础，通过业务公用模块和特色模块分别实现程序共享和特色业务功能，实现了信用卡卡片/帐户管理、申请审批管理、授权管理、交易管理、拒付调单管理和信用卡代授权管理等业务功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The system supports VISA, Master, Amex and China UnionPay standard credit cards, either magnetic stripe-based or chip-based.	支持发行VISA、Master、Amex及中国银联标准信用卡，介质类型包括磁条和芯片。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The system also supports the following operations regarding credit cards: accounting, clearing, authorization, risk management, marketing strategy development, marketing, customer services and overdraft recovery.	系统支持信用卡如下业务处理：核算、清算、授权、风险管理、营销策略制定、市场营销、客户服务、透支催收等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iv. Local clearing system	（四）本地清算系统	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The local clearing platform mainly enables interconnection between FOVA and overseas institutions’ local clearing systems (or software).	本地清算平台主要实现FOVA系统与各境外行本地清算系统（软件）对接处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The local clearing platform mainly deals with local inter-bank remittance and clearing. Its primary features include communication processing, message conversion, accounting treatment, statistical statement, remittance message sending and remittance message receiving.	在业务功能上本地清算平台主要承担当地跨行汇款、清算业务，主要功能有通讯处理、报文转换、账务处理、报表统计、汇款发报处理、汇款收报处理等功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
As clearing houses in different countries or regions differ significantly in terms of their requirements on local inter-bank clearing, overseas institutions use different business modes. Branches in Sydney, Almaty, Frankfurt and New York have their specific modes.	由于各个国家和地区的清算组织对当地跨行清算要求差异较大，各境外行按照不同的业务处理模式实现，有悉尼、阿拉木图、法兰克福、纽约等多种分行模式进行业务处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
v. Global cash management system	（五）全球现金管理系统	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The global cash management system provides customers with global cash management services based on the interconnection between NOVA and FOVA and also through its interconnection with partnering banks by multiple means of direct inter-bank link and SWIFTNet.	境外全球现金管理系统利用我行NOVA、FOVA系统的互联互通，以及通过银银直联、SWIFTNet等多渠道与合作行互联，为客户提供全球现金管理服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers can create one-point connection with the lead bank to meet its group-wide fund management.	客户通过一点式接入主办行，实现其集团内部资金统一管理的需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The system supports two business modes: Overseas institutions are lead managers and domestic institutions or partnering banks are co-managers; and domestic institutions or partnering banks are lead managers and overseas institutions are co-managers. The system mainly provides the following features: centralized collection/disbursement, debiting/crediting advice, general account report, account information report, account information inquiry, cross-border cash pooling and nominal cash pooling.	支持境外机构作为主办行、国内机构或合作银行作为协办行以及国内机构或合作银行作为主办行、境外机构作为协办行两种业务模式，主要包括如下功能：集中收付款、借贷记通知、综合账户报告、账户信息报告、账户信息查询、跨境资金池、名义资金池等业务处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vi. Document business	（六）单证业务	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The document business module deals with international settlement and trade finance. In addition to such traditional services as L/C, collection, L/G, acceptance and forfaiting, this module also covers business types including overseas refinancing, import bill advance, inward bill purchased under collection, export bill financing, packing loans and T/T financing, and also adds interest prepayment and interest deferral.	单证业务模块处理国际结算和贸易融资业务，除提供信用证、托收、保函、承兑、福费廷等传统业务功能以外，还增加了海外代付、进口押汇、进口代收押汇、出口发票融资、打包放款、TT融资等业务品种，增加了利息先收和利息后收两种方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With regard to business processing, overseas institutions only need to handle front-office operations, acquiring and customer services, while documents are transmitted via the imaging system to the documents center, which then makes accounting treatment in combination with FOVA and sends relevant receipts and cover letters back to the overseas institutions for subsequent processing.	在业务处理上，境外机构只需要负责前台业务受理、收单和客户服务等，业务单据通过影像系统传送到单证中心进行处理，并由单证中心联动FOVA系统进行帐务处理，将有关回单、面函返回境外机构进行后续处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
GCMS, FOVA and the documents center are interconnected to apply rigid control upon credit application, approval and transaction processing with regard to trade finance.	实现了GCMS、FOVA、单证中心系统的三方联动，对贸易融资业务的信贷申请、审批和业务办理进行流程上的刚性控制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vii. Capital market (SUMMIT FT)	（七）资金市场（SUMMIT FT）	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This system, dedicated to the financial market business, is an advanced and strong system that integrates front-office, middle-office and back-office operations.	该系统是专门用于处理金融市场业务，集前、中、后台于一身的功能较为先进和强大的处理系统。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The system not only processes day-to-day financial market transactions, but also allows real-time data exchange with external systems and provides advanced risk pricing models that facilitate pricing, valuation and risk estimation of various financial instruments.	不但能对银行金融市场业务进行日常交易的处理外，还能根据情况与外系统进行实时的数据交换，并提供了较为先进的风险定价模型，可以方便的对各种金融工具进行价格计算、市值评估和风险估量。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
This module supports derivative transactions, stocks, futures, capital market (e.g. foreign exchange trading and money market lendings), fixed-income products (e.g. bonds) and structured products (MUST).	该业务模块支持衍生交易、股票、期货交易、资金市场（如外汇买卖、货币市场拆借等）、固定收益产品（如债券等）、结构性产品（MUST）。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
viii. Credit management	（八）信贷管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The credit management module provides credit management system supports for loans and trade finance.	信贷管理模块实现为贷款和贸易融资类业务提供信贷管理系统支持。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The credit management module (GCMS) is a basic platform independently developed by the Head Office according to the plan for the fourth-generation application system architecture. The module covers global corporate customers, institutional customers, personal customers and counterparties, supports asset business operations of domestic and overseas institutions, risk control management and business decision making and analysis and implements central management of the global asset business.	信贷管理模块（GCMS）是总行按照第四代应用系统架构规划，自主设计研发的覆盖全球公司客户、机构客户、个人客户、交易对手，支持境内外机构资产业务操作、风险控制管理、经营决策分析，实施全球资产业务统一管理的基础平台。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The module provides standardized and procedure-based operation and management of all credit asset businesses of overseas institutions in a single platform, realizes organic exchange and secure sharing of domestic and overseas information, provides abundant integrated information resources, allows business information exchange between domestic and overseas institutions and implements global credit lines to group customers and centralized risk management.	该模块将境外机构所有信贷资产业务都在同一平台上标准化、流程化操作及管理，实现了境内外信息有机交互、安全共享，提供集成丰富的信息资源，实现境内外机构业务信息联动，实施集团客户全球统一授信和风险集中管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Principal features of GCMS include system management, customer management, product management, business handling, post-loan management, statistical inquiry management and full lifecycle management of asset businesses.	GCMS主体核心功能包括系统管理、客户管理、产品管理、业务办理、贷后管理、统计查询管理，并围绕着资产业务的全生命周期进行管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ix. Internet banking system	（九）网上银行系统	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Internet banking system provides personal Internet banking, corporate Internet banking and internal management features. The personal Internet banking module mainly provides such features as account management, registered account transfer, outward transfer, outward remittance, time deposits, online loans, online foreign exchange market, bill payment, credit card services, online mutual funds, online precious metals and customer services. The corporate Internet banking module provides such features as account management, collection service, payment service (online transfer, bulk transfer and remittance etc.), time deposits, online loans, foreign exchange trading, cash pooling and customer services.	网上银行系统提供个人网银及企业网银和内部管理功能，其中个人网银主要提供账户管理、注册账户转账、对外转账、汇出汇款、定期存款、网上贷款、网上汇市、缴费站、信用卡服务、网上基金、网上贵金属、客户服务等功能；企业网银提供账户管理、收款业务、付款业务（联机转账和批量转账业务、汇款业务等）、定期存款、网上贷款、外汇买卖、资金池、客户服务等功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
x. Telephone banking system	（十）电话银行系统	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Telephone banking services include account inquiry, transfer, foreign exchange trading, time deposits and agency bill payment.	电话银行业务包括账户查询业务、转账业务、外汇买卖业务、定期存款业务、代理缴费业务等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition to self-help voice services, calls made for manual services by customers in all countries/regions are answered by professional customer service representatives at the E-banking Center (Guangzhou) and the ICBC Credit Card Center (International).	除丰富的自助语音业务外，各国家/地区客户转接人工服务的电话根据业务类型分别由电子银行中心（广州）和工银信用卡中心（国际）两大中心的专业客服代表接听。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has two types of customer service phone numbers for overseas telephone banking services. One is the global customer service hotline “80080095588”, and the other is the local service phone number, both available on a 24-hour basis.	工商银行境外电话银行客服号码包括两种，一种是全球统一客服号码“80080095588”，另外一种是境外行当地服务电话，两类电话均提供24小时对外服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
xi. ATM and POS system	（十一）ATM、POS系统	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The ATM and POS system is mainly designed for ATM and POS services for ICBC Peony Cards (Peony Moneylink Card, Peony Credit Card and Peony International Card), UnionPay cards, overseas VISA cards, MASTER cards, AE cards, DINER cards and JCB cards. The system provides cardholders with ATM-based withdrawals, deposits, transfers, password modification and balance check and POS-based consumptions.	ATM、POS系统主要为工商银行牡丹卡（牡丹灵通卡、牡丹贷记卡、牡丹国际卡等）、境内银联卡以及境外VISA、MASTER、AE、DINER、JCB外卡的ATM、POS业务而设计，系统为持卡人提供在自动柜员机进行取款、存款、转账、修改密码、查询余额,在POS上进行消费等功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
xii. Asset custody accounting valuation system	（十二）资产托管会计估值系统	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The system adopts the simple and flexible configurable design according to the asset custody business characteristics in international markets and the global custody mode. It supports multi-regional deployment and multi-mode custody.	根据国际市场上资产托管业务的特点和全球化托管模式的要求，采用简易灵活的可配置式的设计，支持多地区部署，多托管模式并存。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
System features mainly include parameter management, securities information management, delivery management, corporate action management, message sending/receiving management, fund clearing management, details inquiry, accounting valuation and statement generation.	系统功能主要包括：参数管理、证券信息管理、交收管理、公司行动管理、报文收发管理、资金清算管理、台账查询、会计估值、报表生成等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The system supports basic custody services and value-added services. Basic custody services include custody of customers’ assets, customer order delivery and fund clearing. Value-added services include accounting and asset valuation of customer investment and submission of regulatory reports. Local custody and sub-custody are supported.	系统支持托管基本服务和增值服务，基本托管服务包括客户资产的保管，客户指令交收、资金清算等，增值服务包括客户投资的会计核算、资产估值，各类监管报表报送等，并支持本地托管和次托管模式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Three Science & Technology Regulations for Overseas Institutions	第三节 境外机构科技制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Overview of Science & Technology Regulations for Overseas Institutions	一、境外机构科技制度概况	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In 2011, the Head Office formulated science & technology management regulations for overseas institutions and incorporated them into annual routine revision, under the Bank’s framework for IT management rules and regulations, regarding IT work characteristics of overseas institutions. These regulations are revised annually.	2011年，总行结合境外机构科技工作特点，在全行信息科技管理制度体系框架下，组织编制了境外机构科技管理制度，并纳入每年例行化修订。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The 2012 edition of science & technology management regulations for overseas institutions currently in force consists of 20 sets of measures, 25 sets of rules and 13 handbooks, totaling 58 documents. The specific framework is illustrated in the figure below.	正在执行的2012版境外机构科技管理制度共包含20个办法、25个细则、13个手册，合计58个，具体架构情况见下图。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Notes: 1. Yellow means relevant regulations are applicable to overseas institutions only, totaling 14; and	注：1、黄色表示相关制度为单独适用于境外机构，共14个；	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Green means relevant regulations are applicable to both domestic and overseas institutions, totaling 44.	2、绿色表示相关制度为境内、境外单位共同适用，共44个。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Operation Management	二、运行管理类	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Service Level Management Measures and Implementation Rules for the Service Level Management MEasures (Overseas Institutions) (Trial)	（一）《服务水平管理办法》、《服务水平管理办法实施细则（境外机构）（试行）》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to regulate service level management of overseas institutions, ensure and improve the quality of information system services of overseas institutions, meet predetermined service level requirements and increase the satisfaction of information system users, the Implementation Rules for the Service Level Management Measures (Overseas Institutions) (Trial) was formulated in accordance with the Service Level Management Measures.	为了规范对境外机构的服务水平管理工作，保证和改进境外机构信息系统服务的质量，达到既定的服务水平要求，以提高信息系统用户的满意度，依据《服务水平管理办法》，制定了《服务水平管理办法实施细则（境外机构）（试行）》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These implementation rules define the management process of establishment, implementation, evaluation and continuous improvement of the service level of overseas institutions.	此实施细则定义了对境外机构服务水平的确立、实施、评价和持续改进的管理过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Availability Management Measures and Implementation Rules for Availability Management Measures	（二）《可用性管理办法》、《可用性管理办法实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to further clarify duties on availability management of information systems, regulate availability management, enhance the performance of information systems with respect to normal functioning and response capability and ultimately achieve and improve the service quality required for information systems, the Availability Management Measures and the Implementation Rules for Availability Management Measures were formulated.	为了进一步明确信息系统的可用性管理工作的职责，规范可用性管理工作，加强信息系统发挥正常功能和响应能力的性能，从而达到和提高信息系统服务水平所规定的服务质量，特制定了《可用性管理办法》及《可用性管理办法实施细则》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These measures and implementation rules define the management process of putting forward availability requirements on information systems, identifying objectives, plans implementation and monitoring. 	此管理办法及实施细则中定义了对信息系统的可用性需求提出、目标确定、计划实施和监控的管理过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Event Management Measures and Implementation Rules for Event Management Measures - Security Events (Overseas Institutions) (Trial)	（三）《事件管理办法》、《事件管理办法安全事件实施细则（境外机构）（试行）	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Event Management Measures was formulated in order to strengthen management of information system events, regulate fault events and monitor event handling procedures and effectively cope with events arising from the operation of information systems in a timely manner.	为了加强信息系统的事件管理，规范生产故障事件及监控事件处理流程，及时、有效地处理信息系统运行中发生的各类事件，制定了《事件管理办法》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These measures define the management process of reporting, acceptance, handling and feedback regarding events (excluding events in the process of R&D). Events are classified according to the level, extent or duration of impact, type of system or emergency level.	此管理办法中定义了对事件（不包括研发过程中的事件）报告、受理、处理、反馈的管理过程，事件可按影响程度、影响范围、影响时段和涉及系统类别、紧急程度进行分级。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to further clarify overseas institutions’ duties regarding security events, strengthen management of security events and increase efficiency of event handling, the Implementation Rules for Event Management Measures - Security Incidents (Overseas Institutions) (Trial) was formulated in accordance with the Event Management Measures.	为进一步明确境外机构在安全事件过程中的职责，加强安全事件管理，提高处理效率，依照《事件管理办法》，制定了《事件管理办法安全事件实施细则（境外机构）（试行）。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These implementation rules define the management process of reporting, handling, feedback and tracking of security events in the information technology field of overseas institutions of ICBC.	此实施细则中定义了工商银行对境外机构内部的信息技术领域安全事件的报告、处理、反馈和跟踪的管理过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Covered events are divided into security events and counterfeit E-banking.	涉及安全事件和假冒电子银行事件两个方面。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Security events within the responsibility of data centers are managed in accordance with the Implementation Rules for Event Management Measures - Security Events.	须由数据中心处理的安全事件按照《事件管理办法安全事件实施细则》进行管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iv. Implementation Rules for Event Management Measures – Production Fault Events	（四）《事件管理办法生产故障事件实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to further clarify roles and responsibilities regarding production fault events and enhance event management, the Implementation Rules for Event Management Measures - Production Fault Events was formulated in accordance with the Event Management Measures.	为进一步明确生产故障事件处理过程中各岗位的职责，加强事件管理，提高事件处理效率，依照《事件管理办法》，制定了《事件管理办法生产故障事件实施细则》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These implementation rules define the management process of reporting, acceptance, handling and feedback of production fault events.	此实施细则中定义了对生产故障事件的报告、受理、处理、反馈的管理过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
v. Implementation Rules for Event Management Measures – Service Demand Events	（五）《事件管理办法服务需求事件实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to further clarify duties of all entities with respect to the handling of service demand events, enhance management of service demand events and increase the efficiency of service demand event handling, the Implementation Rules for Event Management Measures – Service demand Events was formulated in accordance with the Event Management Measures.	为了进一步明确各单位在服务需求事件处理过程中的职责，加强服务需求事件管理，提高服务需求事件处理效率，依照《事件管理办法》，制定了《事件管理办法服务需求事件实施细则》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These implementation rules define the management process of application, approval, acceptance and handling of service demand events in the production systems.	此实施细则中定义了对生产系统发生服务需求事件的申请、审批、受理、处理的管理过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vi. Problem Management Measures and Implementation Rules of Problem Management Measures – Production Problems	（六）《问题管理办法》、《问题管理办法生产问题实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to enhance problem management of information systems, regulate problem handling procedures, analyze the primary causes for all events in an in-depth manner and put in place essential precautions and solutions to prevent recurrence of events, the Problem Management Measures and the Implementation Rules of Problem Management Measures – Production Problems were formulated.	为了加强信息系统的问题管理，规范问题处理流程，深入分析各类事件的根本原因，落实根本防范和解决措施，防范事件的再次发生，制定了《问题管理办法》及《问题管理办法生产问题实施细则》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These measures and implementation rules define the management process of reporting, acceptance, handling and feedback of all problems about production environment.	此管理办法及实施细则中定义了对生产环境发生的各类问题的报告、受理、解决和反馈的管理过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
vii. Change Management Measures and Implementation Rules of Change Management Measures – Production Changes	（七）《变更管理办法》、《变更管理办法生产变更实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In order to enhance change management of information systems of ICBC, improve service demand response, regulate handling procedures, allocate resources reasonably and effectively and prevent risk, the Change Management Measures and the Implementation Rules of Change Management Measures – Production Changes were formulated.	为了加强工商银行信息系统的变更管理和服务需求响应，规范处理流程，合理、有效调配资源，防范风险，制定了《变更管理办法》及《变更管理办法生产变更实施细则》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These measures and implementation rules define the management process of application, acceptance, preparation for implementation, formulation of plan, approval, implementation, check, verification, examination and feedback with respect to production changes as well as response preparation, formulation of plan, approval, handling, check, verification, examination and feedback with respect to service demand.	此管理办法及实施细则中定义了生产变更的申请、受理、实施准备、方案制定、审批、实施、复核、验证、检查和反馈以及服务需求响应准备、方案制定、审批、处理、复核、验证、检查和反馈等的管理过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
viii. Emergency Management Measures, Implementation Rules for Emergency Management Measures – Non-disaster Preparation Emergency and Implementation Rules for Emergency Management Measures – Disaster Preparation Emergency	（八）《应急管理办法》、《应急管理办法非灾备应急实施细则》、《应急管理办法灾备应急实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Emergency Management Measures was formulated in order to regulate emergency management of information systems of ICBC, effectively respond to all emergencies, recover external services quickly and ensure security, stability and continuity of information systems.	为了规范工商银行信息系统应急管理工作，有效应对各种紧急情况，快速恢复对外服务，保障信息系统安全、稳定、持续运行，制定了《应急管理办法》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These measures define the management process of formulation of the emergency response plan, emergency drill, triggering of emergency response and emergency handling.	此管理办法中定义了对应急预案编制、应急演练、应急启动、应急处理的管理过程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

The Implementation Rules for Emergency Management Measures – Disaster Preparation Emergency was formulated in accordance with the Emergency Management Measures in order to regulate environmental management of the disaster backup and recovery system, routine maintenance and the triggering process of disaster recovery, ensure that key operations of the Bank can be restored to normal status as soon as possible after any disaster event takes place and minimize the loss the Bank incurs due to disaster events.	为规范灾难备份及恢复系统的环境管理、日常维护及灾难恢复启动流程，确保当灾难事件发生时能够尽快恢复我行关键业务的正常运行，最大限度地降低灾难事件给我行造成的损失，依照《应急管理办法》，制定《应急管理办法灾备应急实施细则》。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

V. Regulations on Information Security Management Applicable to Overseas Institutions	五、适用于境外机构的信息安全管理类制度	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC always attaches great importance to the protection of information security. In recent years, with regard to security management, a series of directive documents have been issued to provide guidance on security of information systems of ICBC, including the Standard for the Security Framework of Information and Information Systems, the Guidelines on Security Classification of Information and Information Systems and the Implementation Measures on Classified Protection of Information and Information Systems.	工商银行一贯重视信息安全保障工作，近年来在安全管理方面制定和颁布了《信息系统信息及信息系统安全体系规范》、《信息及信息系统安全定级指南》和《信息及信息系统安全等级保护实施办法》等一系列指导工商银行信息系统安全建设的指导性文件。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Based on these framework documents, ICBC formulated the Management Measures on Security of Information and Information Systems and the Management Measures on the Electronic Documents Security Control System of ICBC with respect to information and information systems and security management of electronic documents, respectively, setting out the management procedures, duties and requirements under different work scenarios.	以这些纲领性文件为核心，工商银行针对信息及信息系统、电子文件的保密管理分别制定了《信息及信息系统安全管理办法》、《中国工商银行电子文件安全控制系统管理办法》等管理制度，对不同工作场景下的管理流程、职责和要求分别进行了规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Management Measures on Security of Information and Information Systems	（一）《信息及信息系统安全管理办法》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Management Measures on Security of Information and Information Systems describe the general requirements and duties of relevant departments on security management of information and information systems.	《信息和信息系统安全管理办法》描述了相关部门在信息和信息系统安全管理方面的职责和总体要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In accordance with the measures, a series of implementation rules applicable to the whole bank were formulated, including the Implementation Rules for Management of Application System Information Protection, the Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Systems, the Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Internet Access and the Implementation Rules for Client-side Information Leak Protection Management. Function-specific rules and handbooks were also developed based on actual conditions.	依据该办法主要制定适用于全行的《应用系统信息保护管理实施细则》、《客户端系统安全管理实施细则》、《客户端互联网访问安全管理实施细则》、《客户端信息防泄漏管理实施细则》等实施细则，各专业也结合实际情况制定了一些本专业适用的细则和手册。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Implementation Rules for Management of Application System Information Protection	。 1.《应用系统信息保护管理实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These rules were formulated for the purpose of enhancing management of application system information protection, regulating the process of information security management, establishing and improving the mechanism for information security management, clarifying security management duties, preventing information security risk and ensuring security of information displayed to users in the Bank’s application systems.	该细则的目标在于加强应用系统信息保护管理，规范信息的安全管理过程，建立、健全信息安全管理机制，明确安全管理职责，防范信息安全风险，确保我行应用系统中面向用户展示信息的安全。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These rules define roles and responsibilities of departments with respect to information protection of application systems in line with the internal organizational structure of ICBC.	细则根据工商银行的内部组织架构，对各部门在应用系统信息保护工作的职责及分工进行了定义。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
These rules also set out the main grounds and methods for information security classification and, based on information security classification, classify information displayed in systems into ordinary protection class and extra protection class.	规定了信息保护级别划分的主要依据和方法，并且在信息安全等级划分的基础上，将系统展示信息分为普通保护级和重点保护级。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to such classification, these rules develop the security policy database for information displayed in systems and require that the information displayed in all application systems should be protected in accordance with the information security policies.	根据这些级别，细则中分别拟定了系统展示信息安全策略库，并要求各应用系统展示信息的保护应依据信息安全策略来进行实施。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Implementation Rules for Management of Application System Information Protection defines the management and procedures of information protection in the whole life cycle of application systems, including requirement defining, design, development and use.	《应用系统信息保护管理实施细则》根据应用系统的整个生命周期，对需求定义、设计、开发、投入使用等各个阶段中，信息保护的管理及实施流程均分别进行了规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Systems	2．《客户端系统安全管理实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Systems require that only ICBC-authorized operating systems and application software can be installed on the client side, users are prohibited from installing or using any unauthorized software on the client side, and the installation of multiple operating systems and virtual machine software shall be strictly controlled.	《客户端系统安全管理实施细则》要求：客户端只能安装、使用工商银行授权使用的操作系统和应用软件，禁止用户在客户端上安装、使用各类非授权软件；并严格控制安装多操作系统和虚拟机软件。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Client-side unauthorized software management refers to prohibiting users from installing or using unauthorized software by managerial and technical means and keeping a record of user attempts to use unauthorized software.	客户端非授权软件管理指通过管理和技术手段禁止用户安装和运行非授权软件，并记录尝试使用非授权软件的用户行为。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Unauthorized software refer to operating systems and application software that are not authorized by the Head Office, including operating systems used without authorization, free software, purchased software and pirated software.	非授权软件指未经过总行授权使用的操作系统和应用软件，包括未经批准就使用的操作系统、各类免费软件、自行购买的软件、盗版软件等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In accordance with relevant provisions of the Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Systems, all entities shall restrict the installation of software at the production terminals by centralizing the power to manage system administrator IDs. Unauthorized software management on the office client-side shall be carried out through comprehensive management measures, including “black and white lists”.	根据《客户端系统安全管理实施细则》中的相关规定，各单位应该通过上收系统管理员账号等管理措施限制生产终端的软件安装；通过“黑白名单”等综合管理措施，实施办公客户端的非授权软件管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition, these rules also define the technical measures for “black and white lists”, strategy management procedures and exception management procedures.	同时，该细则还定义了“黑白名单”的控制实现技术措施、策略管理流程和例外管理流程。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Client-side hardware peripherals management refer to controlling and recording the use of hardware peripherals by managerial and technical means, including USB ports, CD-ROM devices, floppy devices, Bluetooth devices, infrared devices, modem devices and 1394 Port.	客户端硬件外设管理指通过管理和技术手段控制、记录USB端口、光驱设备、软驱设备、蓝牙设备、红外设备、调制解调设备、1394端口等硬件外设的使用。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The client-side intrusion protection management refers to protecting the client side from Intranet and Internet intrusion by using the client-side intrusion protection software.	客户端入侵防护管理是指通过客户端入侵防护软件保护客户端免遭来自内网或外网的非法网络入侵。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
All entities shall analyze their client-side intrusion protection logs and make clear whether their client side is often in a high-risk network.	各单位应分析本单位客户端的入侵防护日志，了解本单位客户端是否经常处于高风险网络。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Internet Access	3.《客户端互联网访问安全管理实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internet access security management refers to restricting employers’ access to high-risk websites by technical and managerial means, automatically filtering viruses in visited web pages, limiting the time of Internet access and strengthening information security management.	互联网访问安全管理指通过各种技术和管理控制措施限制员工访问高风险网站，自动过滤正在访问网页的病毒，限制上网时间，强化信息安全管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Internet access is managed also on the basis of “black and white lists”. Mobile computers distributed by all entities shall be used only for business purposes of ICBC.	互联网访问同样采取“黑白名单”的管理方式，各单位配发的移动电脑仅供工商银行生产办公使用。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The SEP software must be installed in all mobile computers connected to the Bank’s production and office networks. Only white list websites are accessible if mobile computers are carried away from office premises of the Bank.	接入行内生产办公网络的移动电脑需安装办公SEP软件，在离行后只能访问白名单网站。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If employees have to access Internet for work purposes, they should access Internet from the client side under the Internet cyber bar environment.	员工因工作需要访问互联网的，通过互联网网吧环境的客户端访问。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If SEP software is used to control the mobile computers’ access to VPN, only authorized network resources are accessible.	通过SEP软件控制移动电脑在接入VPN移动办公网络时，只能访问被授权访问的网络资源。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In addition, Data Leak Prevention (DLP) devices are installed at production Internet ports and cyber cafe ports of ICBC to filter and audit sensitive information in the Internet port traffic, so as to avoid divulgation of sensitive information.	同时，通过在工商银行生产互联网出口、网吧出口等位置部署信息泄漏防护设备（DLP设备）实现对互联网出口网络流量中敏感信息的过滤审计，避免敏感信息非法外泄的可能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Information	4.《客户端信息防泄漏安全管理实施细则》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
