The office client-side information security management is to protect information from leakage by means of sensitive information scanning of client hard disks, examination of offline client-side data transmission, monitoring of outgoing emails, control of mobile storage devices and password-based protection of mobile computer hard disks.	办公客户端信息防泄漏安全管理通过对客户端硬盘进行敏感信息扫描、对离线客户端数据传输进行检查、对外发邮件的监控管理、移动存储设备的使用控制、移动电脑硬盘实施密码保护管理等方式实现信息泄漏的安全防护。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Implementation Rules for Security Management of Client-side Information defines the management requirements, scanning strategy, irregularity handling and exceptions management with respect to office client-side information security.	《客户端信息防泄漏安全管理实施细则》定义了办公客户端信息防泄漏的管理要求、扫描策略、违规处理及例外管理情况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Such rigid control measures as office client-side sensitive information scanning and offline data transmission are made in place by installing the DLP software on the office client side.	通过在办公客户端部署DLP信息泄漏防护工具客户端软件，实现在办公客户端的敏感信息扫描、离线数据传输等硬控制措施。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
During scanning of sensitive information in client-side hard disks, information stored in the office client-side hard disks is scanned according to the preset inspection strategy.	客户端硬盘敏感信息扫描通过预先设定的检查策略，对办公客户端硬盘上存储的内容进行扫描。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, with regard to client-side information security protection, the client-side printing, recording and plain text-based data copying to USB devices and data transmission during Internet access without being connected to the Intranet of ICBC are inspected according to preset inspection strategy. A record will be kept of violations of information security management requirements and a warning notice will be given to the relevant positions to prevent leakage of sensitive information.	同时，客户端信息泄漏防护通过预先设定的检查策略，对客户端打印、刻录和向U盘明文拷贝数据的情况，以及在未接入工商银行内网时的互联网访问过程中数据传输的情况进行检查，对其中违反信息防泄漏安全管理要求的行为进行记录，并向相关岗位发出报警通知，防范敏感信息泄漏。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Implementation Rules for Information Leak Protection Management requires that if external emails include sensitive information or deemed to be unknown document types that are not automatically identifiable by the password protection, encryption or other information security management systems, such mails will be automatically blocked and an email containing the context for key words of strategy violation will be issued to the information security management position for the sender.	《信息防泄漏管理实施细则》中规定外网邮件中包含敏感信息或包含密码保护、加密等信息防泄漏管理系统判定为无法自动识别的不明类型文件时，系统自动阻断该邮件，并向发件人所属的信息安全使用管理岗发出一封包含违反策略关键字上下文内容的邮件。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Meanwhile, the system will provide “release” and “block” hyperlinks in the foregoing warning email for the information security management position to process the automatically blocked email.	同时，系统在上述告警信息邮件中提供“放行”、“阻断”的链接按钮，供信息安全使用管理岗对系统阻断邮件进行处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The information security management position shall make judgment according to the context or attachment provided in the warning email that may contain confidential information or violate relevant rules and release or block the email as appropriate.	信息安全使用管理岗要根据告警邮件中可能涉密、违规的上下文、附件内容等进行判断，实施放行或拦截操作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If the sender need re-send an automatically blocked email due to work needs, the Statement of External Email Control and Prevention Exceptions shall be filled out within five days and submitted to the supervisor for approval. If such exception is approved, the email may be re-sent and released by the information security management position.	在邮件被阻断后，发件人如确因工作需要，需继续发送被系统阻断的邮件，应在5日内填写《外网邮件防控例外事件说明表》，并提交本单位主管领导审核，审核同意后再次发送该邮件并由信息安全使用管理岗进行放行操作。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
NOTES mailboxes that cannot be included in the external email security management for special reasons may be managed on the basis of black and white lists.	对于因特殊工作需要无法纳入到外网邮件信息防泄漏管理的NOTES邮箱，可按照白名单方式管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
White-listed emails shall be approved and registered.	白名单邮箱应该审批并备案。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The IT departments shall regularly monitor, analyze and improve the strategy and effectiveness of external email leakage control and prevention.	信息科技部门对于外网邮件的防控策略和防控效果定期监测、分析并完善。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The office client-side removable storage security management function is realized through the Electronic Document Security Management (DSM) system.	办公客户端移动存储安全管理功能通过电子文件安全控制（DSM）系统实现。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Removable media usable on the internal client side and those usable on the external client side are differentiated to strictly isolate information exchange between removable media and avoid possible leakage of sensitive information.	通过区分行内客户端上可以使用的移动介质和行外客户端上可以使用的移动介质，严格隔离信息的移动介质间交换，杜绝敏感信息的可能外泄情况。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
To avoid the risk of information leakage due to loss of client-side computers, password protection must be provided for the local hard disks of office client-side mobile computers so that the hard disk password must be entered prior to access to hard disk data when the client-side computer is started up.	为避免因客户端电脑丢失等原因带来的信息泄漏风险，需要对移动办公客户端电脑的本地硬盘采取密码保护措施，在客户端电脑启动时需要输入硬盘访问密码方可正常读取硬盘上的数据内容。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Management Measures on the Electronic Document Security Management System of ICBC	（二）《中国工商银行电子文件安全控制系统管理办法》	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The Electronic Document Security Management (DSM) system must be installed on the office client side of ICBC.	工商银行办公客户端必须安装DSM电子文档安全管理系统。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The electronic document security management system enables encrypted storage of electronic documents containing business secrets and important information, which cannot be reproduced or printed by valid users without authorization or viewed by invalid users. Any operations regarding electronic documents containing business secrets and important information will be audited. In addition, the electronic document security management system provides authorization and encryption/decryption interfaces. It may be combined with application systems and automatically authorizes encryption according to application system needs and customizes the security protection strategy.	电子文件安全控制系统实现了涉及商业秘密和重要信息电子文件加密存储，合法用户未经授权无法复制、打印，非法用户无法浏览，对商业秘密和重要信息电子文件操作行为进行审计。 此外，电子文件安全控制系统提供授权和加解密接口，可以和应用系统结合，自动根据应用系统需求进行授权加密，定制安全保密策略。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The electronic document security management system, as the platform for centralized management of the Bank’s business secrets, enables full-lifecycle management of the Bank’s electronic documents ranging from generation to use and then destruction.	电子文件安全控制系统作为全行商业秘密统一管理平台，实现了全行电子文件从产生到使用直至销毁的全周期保密管理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Employees shall, in compliance with the Management Measures on the Electronic Document Security Management System of ICBC (Trial) (G.YB.F. [2010] No. 297), apply authority control through the electronic document security management system when transmitting through NOTES emails, releasing through internal information bulletins, sharing among computers and storing any electronic documents containing business secrets and important information of ICBC in mobile or Internet-linked computers.	员工应严格按照《中国工商银行电子文件安全控制系统管理办法（试行）》（工银办发[2010]297号）要求，在通过NOTES邮件传递、内部信息园地发布、集中文档机共享以及用于移动办公或连接互联网的计算机内存储的涉及工商银行商业秘密和重要信息电子文件使用电子文件安全控制系统进行权限控制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
CHAPTER FOUR OVERSEAS PRODUCT SYSTEM OF ICBC	第四章 工商银行境外产品体系	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Being committed to providing customers with a full range of quality financial services and most excellent financial products, ICBC has actively extended its overseas competitive product lines and conducted product innovation according to the needs of customers and market in recent years.	近年来，工商银行坚持以提供全面优质金融服务、让客户用上最卓越金融产品为己任，积极延伸境内优势产品线，根据客户与市场需求开展产品创新，不断完善产品体系、优化产品功能与设计，推出具有较强市场竞争力的优势产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It kept improving product mix, optimized product functions and design, and launched competitive advantageous products in the market. By the end of 2011, ICBC had established 239 branches and outlets in 33 countries and regions outside China, and provided more than 300,000 individual and corporate customers in the markets outside the Chinese Mainland with diversified financial products and services, covering nearly 3,000 products in 11 categories such as deposits, loans, bankcards, e-banking, fund settlement, investment banking, asset management, private banking, asset custody and global cash management. ICBC depends on many channels, including operating outlets, internet banking, telephone banking and self-service terminals, to serve customers and satisfy their various financial needs.	截至2011年底，工商银行已在除中国以外的33个国家和地区设立了239个分支机构，向中国大陆境外市场30余万个人及企业客户提供着广泛的金融产品与服务，构建了涵盖存贷款、银行卡、电子银行、资金结算、投资银行、资产管理、私人银行、资产托管、全球现金管理等十一大类共计近3000个产品的产品体系，通过营业网点、网上银行、电话银行、自助终端等多种渠道服务客户，满足客户全方位的金融需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section One Deposit Products	第一节 存款产品	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Demand Deposits	一、活期存款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Demand deposit means a deposit product without a definite term that can be withdrawn at any time. Demand deposits are divided into demand deposits in savings account and demand deposits in current account.	活期存款是一种不限存期，支持随时存取的存款产品，活期存款可以分为储蓄活期存款和往来活期存款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Among them, deposits in current account may be entitled to apply for individual cheque, and corporate deposits in current account shall have the overdraft function.	其中，往来存款可申请个人支票，对公往来存款账户可具有透支功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
T he individual and corporate customers with idle funds and having high requirements on fund liquidity.	适用于有闲置资金，并对资金流动性要求较高的个人客户和企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. High convenience.	1.使用方便。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Demand deposits can be used in such businesses as cash deposit and withdrawal, transfer and settlement, and are convenient for customers to use.	活期存款可用于现金存取、转账结算等业务，便于客户使用。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Strong liquidity.	2.流动性强。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Demand deposits have strong liquidity as they can be withdrawn anytime via such channels as outlets and self-service terminals.	活期存款可随时通过网点、自助终端等渠道进行支取，资金流动性强。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Time Deposits	二、定期存款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Time deposit mean a bank deposit with term and interest rate specified by ICBC and the depositor in advance at the time of deposit, and the principal and interest thereof shall not be withdrawn before the due date.	定期存款是工商银行与存款人双方在存款时事先约定期限、利率，到期后支取本息的存款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Time deposits are divided into lump-sum time deposits, call deposits, irregular time deposits and installment time deposits depending on the differences in terms of rules on term and way of withdrawal.	根据期限约定、取款方式等方面的差别，定期存款又可以分为整存整取、通知存款、不规则定期存款、零存整取等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Among them, lump-sum deposit means a bank deposit whose term is prescribed at the time of deposit and principal is deposited on a lump-sum basis, and which can be withdrawn wholly or partly; call deposit means a bank deposit which does not specify a term at the time of deposit but specifies a notice period for withdrawal, and at the time of withdrawal, the depositor shall notify the operating outlet in advance within the specified period to specify the date and amount of withdrawal and withdraw the principal and interest depending on the deposit certificate; irregular time deposit means the time deposit business with different interest rates depending on the amount, currency and term of deposits; installment time deposit means a bank deposit business that a customer regularly deposits a specified amount and withdraws principal and interest on the due date.	其中整存整取存款是指在存款时约定存期，一次存入本金，全部或部分支取本金和利息的业务；通知存款是指在存入款项时不约定存期，但约定支取存款的通知期限，支取时按约定期限提前通知营业机构，约定支取存款的日期和金额，凭存款凭证支取本金和利息的业务；不规则定期存款是指根据客户存入金额、币种及存期的不同，给予客户不同利率的定期存款业务；零存整取存款是指为客户提供的一种定期存储一定金额，到期一次支取本息的业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The individual and corporate customers with idle funds but having no high requirements on fund liquidity.	适用于有闲置资金，并对资金流动性要求不高的个人客户和企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Relative high interest rate.	1.利率相对较高。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The interest rate of time deposits is higher than that of demand deposits, and the longer deposit term, the higher interest rate.	定期存款利率高于活期存款，存款存期越长，利率越高。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Stipulated renewal.	2.可约定转存。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A customer may stipulate the renewal term at the time of deposit, and the principal and after-tax interest of a time deposit can be automatically renewed on the due date according to the renewal term.	客户可在存款时约定转存期限，定期存款到期后的本金和税后利息将自动按转存期限续存。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Being used as collateral to obtain loans.	3.可质押贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
When a customer has a time deposit, if he is in urgent need of funds but is unwilling to withdraw the time deposit in advance or bear the interest cost for bank loan, he may apply for a time deposit-collateralized loan to obtain funds.	当客户持有定期存款时，如果急需资金，并且不希望提前支取定期存款或支付银行贷款的利息成本，则可以办理定期存款质押贷款，以及时获得资金。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Two Loan Products	第二节 贷款产品	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Personal Housing Loans	一、个人住房贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal housing loan means a loan granted by ICBC to a personal customer for purchase of housing, who shall use the house with property right as collateral for repayment of the loan.	个人住房贷款是指工商银行向个人客户发放的, 用于购买住房，并以其所购产权房为抵押物作为偿还贷款的担保的一种贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The personal customers who hope to obtain loans for housing purchase, and have good credit records, repayment will and ability. 	希望通过贷款资金购买住房，具有良好的信用记录和还款意愿及能力的个人客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Flexible repayment methods.	1.还款方式灵活。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC provides a number of repayment methods, including equal total payments, equal principal payments, weekly debt service, step-up repayment method, step-down repayment method and method of repayment as customer wishes.	工商银行提供等额本息、等额本金、按周还本付息、递增还款法、递减还款法、随心还款法等多种还款方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Convenient and prompt loan services.	2.贷款服务便捷。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC provides such unique repayment services as determination of repayment date freely, provision of grace period for repayment and change of repayment date, and the borrowers may flexibly select them according to their needs.	工商银行提供自主确定还款日、享受还款宽限期、变更还款日等特色还款服务，借款人可根据需求灵活选择。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Personal Consumer Loans	二、个人消费贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal consumer loan means a loan granted by ICBC to a personal customer for the purpose of consumption, including purchase of automobile and housing decoration.	个人消费贷款是指工商银行向个人客户发放的，有指定消费用途的贷款，用途主要有购车、住房装修等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The borrower shall provide property mortgage, pledge or third party guarantee to the lending bank as his loan guarantee condition; the borrowers with good credit may obtain unsecured loans.	借款人需提供贷款银行认可的财产抵押、质押或第三人保证方式作为贷款担保条件；对于资信良好的借款人也可以信用方式获得贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The personal customers who hope to obtain loans for satisfying their consumption needs, and have good credit records, repayment will and ability. 	希望通过申请贷款资金满足消费需求，具有良好的信用记录和还款意愿及能力的个人客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Flexible guarantee methods.	1.担保方式灵活。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The borrowers may adopt a number of guarantee methods including mortgage, pledge and security of guaranty.	可采用抵押、质押、保证担保等多种方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Wide purposes of loans.	2.贷款用途广泛。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal consumer loans can be used to meet such consumption purposes as purchase of automobile, housing decoration, purchase of durable consumer goods, educational expenses, tourist spending and medical expenses.	可满足购车、住房装修、购置耐用消费品、教育支出、旅游和医疗等消费用途。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Personal Business Loans	三、个人经营贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal business loan means a personal guarantee loan granted by ICBC to a personal customer for his capital turnover needed in legal operating activities.	个人经营贷款是指工商银行向个人客户发放的，用于客户合法经营活动所需资金周转的个人担保贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The personal customers who hope to obtain loans for capital turnover in their legal operating activities, and have good credit records, repayment will and ability.	希望通过申请贷款资金用于合法经营活动中的资金周转，具有良好的信用记录和还款意愿及能力的个人客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点与优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Flexible guarantee methods.	1.担保方式灵活。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The borrowers may adopt a number of guarantee methods including mortgage, pledge and security of guaranty.	可采用抵押、质押、保证担保等多种方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Convenient and prompt loan services.	2.贷款服务便捷。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC provides such unique repayment services as determination of repayment date freely, provision of grace period for repayment and change of repayment date, and the borrowers may flexibly select them according to their needs.	工商银行提供自主确定还款日、享受还款宽限期、变更还款日等特色还款服务，借款人可根据需求灵活选择。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IV. Fixed Asset Loans	四、固定资产贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Fixed asset loan is a loan granted by ICBC and used in the customers’ construction, expansion, upgrade, development or purchase of fixed assets.	固定资产贷款是指工商银行发放的，用于借款人新建、扩建、改造、开发、购置固定资产投资活动的贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A fixed asset loan takes the borrowers’ comprehensive income as the repayment source.	固定资产贷款以借款人综合效益做为还款来源。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customers with demand for fixed asset investment.	有固定资产投资需求的企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. To fund the borrower’s large-value investment expenditure on purchase of fixed assets.	1.满足借款人购置固定资产投资的大额支出。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Having a flexible term that can cover the construction period of a fixed asset.	2.期限灵活，覆盖固定资产建设期。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
V. Project Financing	五、项目融资	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Project financing means the loans granted by ICBC for the borrower’s construction of large-sized infrastructure and industrial projects.	项目融资是指工商银行向借款人用于建设大型的基础设施和工业项目发放的贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The borrower of project financing is generally the legal person of the project specially set up for construction and operation of the project or for the project financing.	项目融资借款人通常是为建设、经营该项目或为该项目融资而专门组建的项目法人。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Repayment sources mainly include sales income, subsidy income or other income generated from the project; generally, there is no other repayment source.	还款资金来源主要依赖该项目产生的销售收入、补贴收入或其他收入，一般不具备其他还款来源。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customers with demand for project construction. 	有项目建设需求的企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Flexible term.	1.期限灵活。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC’s project financing is generally medium and long-term loans and the short-term project loans used in the temporary fund turnover for a project.	工商银行项目融资一般是中长期贷款，也有用于满足项目临时周转使用的的短期项目贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Flexible repayment.	2.还款灵活。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customized repayment plans may be drafted according to cash flows.	按照现金流情况量身制订还款计划。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Various portfolios.	3.组合多样。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC may issue banker’s acceptance drafts and non-financing guarantee and provide international trade financing under project financing according to customer needs.	根据客户需求，可在项目融资项下签发银行承兑汇票、开立非融资类保函、办理国际贸易融资等业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VI. Real Estate Loans	六、房地产贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Real estate loan means a medium and long-term loan granted by ICBC for a borrower’s real estate development.	房地产贷款是指工商银行为借款人提供的用于房地产开发的中长期贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Real estate loans mainly include residential housing development loans, commercial housing development loans and legal person commercial housing mortgage loans.	主要包括住房开发贷款、商用房开发贷款和法人商业用房按揭贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Housing development loan means a loan granted by the lender to the borrower for the development and construction of residential housing and its supporting facilities.	住房开发贷款是指贷款人向借款人发放的用于商品住房及其配套设施开发建设的贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Commercial housing development loan means a loan granted by the lender to the borrower for the construction of commercial projects such as hotels (restaurants), office buildings, shopping malls and their supporting facilities.	商用房开发贷款是指向贷款人向借款人发放的用于宾馆（酒店）、写字楼、大型购物中心及其配套设施等商用项目建设的贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Legal person commercial housing mortgage loan means a loan granted by the lender to the borrower for purchase of commercial buildings and office buildings for self use.	法人商业用房按揭贷款是指贷款人向借款人发放的购置商业用房和自用办公用房的贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Real estate development companies and project companies.	房地产开发公司和项目公司。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Diversification.	1.品种多样。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC's real estate loans include housing development loans, commercial housing development loans, legal person housing mortgage loans, and other real estate loans, which can meet the fund needs of customers for different types of real estate development and construction.	目前工商银行已开展的房地产贷款有住房开发贷款、商用房开发贷款、法人客户楼宇按揭贷款、其他房地产贷款等贷款品种，能够满足客户不同类型房地产开发建设的资金需要。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Long term.	2.期限较长。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Among the real estate loans of ICBC, commercial housing development loans and legal person commercial housing mortgage loans have a long term and can meet customers’ long-term fund needs.	工商银行的房地产贷款中，商用房开发贷款、法人商业用房按揭贷款等品种期限较长，可满足客户长期用款需要。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VII. Working Capital Loans	七、流动资金贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Working capital loan is a RMB or foreign currency loan granted by ICBC to satisfy the borrower’s temporary or seasonal fund requirements in the course of production and operation, and ensure its smooth production and operation activities.	流动资金贷款是工商银行为满足借款人在生产经营过程中临时性、季节性的资金需求，保证生产经营活动的正常进行而发放的本外币贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Working capital loans include operating capital loans, bridge loans and legal person account overdraft.	包括营运资金贷款、搭桥贷款、法人账户透支等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Operating capital loan means a loan granted by the lender to satisfy the borrower’s demand for reasonable and continuous use of funds in daily operations, taking the borrower’s future comprehensive income and other legal income as its repayment sources.	营运资金贷款是指贷款人为满足优质借款人日常经营中合理的资金连续使用需求，以其未来综合收益和其他合法收入等作为还款来源而发放的贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Bridge loan means a transitional loan granted by the lender to satisfy the borrower’s temporary fund demands in daily business activities, taking the specific non-operating cash flows generated by the borrower in the future as the repayment sources.	搭桥贷款是贷款人为满足借款人日常业务活动中阶段性的资金需求，以未来所获的特定的非经营性现金流作为还款来源而发放的过渡性贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Account overdraft means a financing product by which a customer obtains the short-term credit funds within the limit authorized by ICBC.	账户透支是指客户在工商银行为其核定的额度内，通过账户透支方式取得短期信贷资金的融资业务产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customers with demand for working capital.	有周转性流动资金需求的企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Strong liquidity and flexible term.	1.流动性强、期限灵活。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Convenient procedures and strong turnover.	2.手续简便、周转性较强。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Low financing costs.	3.融资成本较低。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Satisfying the borrowers’ temporary, short and medium-term working capital demands.	4.满足借款人临时性、短期和中期流动资金需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VIII. Aircraft and Vessel Financing	八、飞机船舶融资	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Aircraft and vessel financing means the financing services provided by ICBC to meet the borrower’s fund demands in purchase, leasing, repair and use of aircraft and vessel.	飞机船舶融资是指工商银行为满足借款人在飞机船舶购置、租赁、维修、使用中的资金需求而提供的融资服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Aircraft and vessel financing generally takes the cash flows from the use of aircraft and vessel assets as the primary repayment source, and collateralized aircraft and vessel as the secondary repayment sources.	飞机船舶融资一般以飞机船舶资产使用产生的现金流作为第一还款来源，以飞机船舶资产抵押作为第二还款来源。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers that have loan demands and are able to provide aircraft and vessel as collaterals. 	有借款需求并可提供飞机船舶作为抵、质押物的客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Aircraft and vessel loans are flexible and diversified.	灵活多样。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
According to different demands of borrowers, ICBC can provide them with such products or services as direct purchase financing, asset mortgage financing, prepayment financing, operating lease financing, finance leasing financing, rents receivable factoring and guarantee. 	根据借款人不同需求，提供直接购置融资、资产抵押融资、预付款融资、经营租赁融资、融资租赁融资、应收租赁款保理、保函等产品或服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IX. International Trade Finance	九、国际贸易融资	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
International trade finance means the on and off-balance sheet short-term credits under international trade granted by ICBC for both trading parties based on the specific settlement method. It is divided into import trade finance (buyer’s financing) and export trade finance (seller’s financing) depending on the nature of business.	国际贸易融资是指以特定结算方式为基础，由工商银行为贸易双方提供的国际贸易项下的表内外短期信贷业务，根据业务性质分为进口贸易融资（买方融资）、出口贸易融资（卖方融资）两大类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Import trade finance is a short-term financing product provided for the importers based on the settlement methods of L/C, collection and T/T, including import bill advance under L/C, import T/T financing, import collection, import factoring, shipping guarantee and import prepayment financing.	进口贸易融资是为进口商提供的基于信用证、托收、T/T结算方式的短期融资产品，包括进口信用证项下押汇、进口T/T融资、进口托收、进口保理、提货担保、进口预付货款融资等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Export trade finance is a short-term financing product provided for the exporters based on the settlement methods of L/C, collection and T/T, including packing loans, bill purchased, export invoice financing, export factoring and export order financing.	出口贸易融资是为出口商提供的基于信用证、托收、T/T结算方式的短期融资产品，包括打包贷款、出口押汇、出口发票融资、出口保理、出口订单融资等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Enterprises qualified for international trade activities.	具有从事国际贸易活动资质的企业。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Flexible procedures and short term.	1.办理灵活、期限短。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With flexible procedures and short term, international trade finance may be obtained depending on the trade background and documents.	凭贸易背景和单据获得融资，业务办理灵活、期限较短。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Credit enhancement.	2.信用增级。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers may enhance their bargaining power and position in trade relations by bank financing, to effectively promote their trade.	客户可通过银行融资信用，提升贸易关系中自身议价能力和地位，有效促成贸易往来。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Diversification.	3.品种多元化。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Financing products, combined with various settlement methods such as L/C, collection and T/T financing, can meet the financing needs of customers under various settlement modes.	融资产品与信用证、托收、T/T融资等多种结算方式相结合，满足客户各种结算模式下的融资需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Wide coverage.	4.覆盖面广。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The product runs through each stage of foreign trade and can provide customers with solutions for their trade financing demands.	贯穿于进出口贸易的各阶段，为客户在贸易中各环节的融资需求提供解决方案。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
X. Syndicated Loans	十、银团贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A syndicated loan means a RMB or foreign currency loan or credit granted by two or more banks, via the lead bank or the correspondent bank, to the borrower at the specified time and according to the proportion and the same loan conditions under the same loan agreement.	银团贷款是指由两家或两家以上银行基于相同贷款条件，依据同一贷款协议，按约定时间和比例，通过牵头行或代理行向借款人提供的本外币贷款或授信业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Generally giant enterprises and groups.	一般是特大型企业、企业集团等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Large financing amount and long term. The lending banks can provide a large amount of credit through cooperation, as an individual bank can not provide a large-value loan due to the restriction of credit line.	1.筹资金额大、期限长，各贷款行合作能够提供巨额的信贷资金，避免单独一家银行受授信额度的限制无法提供大额贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Low financing costs.	2.筹资成本较低。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Lending banks bear credit risks in proportion to their respective loans so as to diversify loan risks.	3.贷款行按约定比例分别承担各自部分贷款的信用风险，从而分散了贷款的风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
XI. Discounted Bills	十一、票据贴现	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Discounted bills include promissory bills discounted by a bank, commercial acceptance draft discount and discounted bills with interest paid under agreement.	票据贴现包括银行本票贴现、商业承兑汇票贴现及票据协议付息贴现。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Discounted bills means the bearer (customer) negotiates by endorsing a promissory note issued by another bank with the discount bank (ICBC) before the note becomes due, and the discount bank makes payment in advance after deducting the discount interest.	银行本票贴现是指持票人（客户）持他行开立的本票到期前向贴现行（工商银行）背书转让，贴现行扣除贴现利息后向其提前支付票款的行为。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Commercial acceptance bill discount means the bearer negotiates by endorsement a commercial acceptance bill with the discount bank before the draft becomes due, and the discount bank makes payment in advance after deducting the discount interest.	商业承兑汇票贴现指持票人在商业承兑汇票到期日前向贴现行背书转让,贴现行扣除贴现利息后向其提前支付票款的行为。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Discounted bills with interest paid under agreement means the bearer applies to the discount bank for negotiation by endorsing a bill that it legally holds before it becomes due, and the discount interest shall be borne by the interest payer specified in the agreement, and the discount bank makes payment in advance to the bearer according to the par value or the related amount under the agreement.	票据协议付息贴现指持票人在其合法持有的票据到期前，以背书转让的方式向贴现行申请贴现，贴现利息由协议约定的付息方承担，贴现行按票面金额或在协议条件下的相关金额向持票人提前支付票款的业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Discounted bills is divided into non-repurchase discounted bills and repurchase discounted bills depending on the agreement signed by the bearer and the bank at the time of discount on whether the bill can be repurchased before it becomes due.	根据持票人在办理贴现时与银行在票据到期日前是否可回购赎回的约定，票据贴现又分为不可回购型票据贴现和可回购型票据贴现。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The target customers of promissory bank note/commercial acceptance bill discount are those who hold unmatured notes and hope to dispose of them before the notes become due.	银行本票/商业承兑汇票贴现目标客户为持有未到期票据，希望在到期前变现的客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The target customers of discounted bills with interest paid under agreement are those who hold unmatured notes and hope to dispose of them before the notes become due, and there is an agreement on the payment of discount interest by the buyer or seller.	票据协议付息贴现目标客户持有未到期票据，希望在到期前变现的客户，并根据协议约定买方或卖方支付贴现利息的客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers may dispose of notes in advance to obtain funds according to the par value or the related amount under the agreed conditions.	客户可按票面金额或协议条件下的相关金额提前获得票款，融通资金。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
XII. Acquisition Loans	十二、并购贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Acquisition loan means a loan granted by ICBC to satisfy the needs of the acquirer or its special-purpose subsidiary for payment in an acquisition transaction, taking the cash flows generated by the enterprise after acquisition, comprehensive income or other income of the acquirer as the repayment sources.	并购贷款是指工商银行为满足并购方或其专门子公司在并购交易中用于支付并购交易价款的需要，以并购后企业产生的现金流、并购方综合收益或其他合法收入为还款来源而发放的贷款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Acquisition mentioned herein means the merger or actual control of an existing and going-concern target enterprise by acquiring existing shares, purchasing new shares, acquiring assets or taking over debts.	此处并购是指企业通过受让现有股权、认购新增股权，或收购资产、承接债务等方式实现合并或实际控制已设立并持续经营的目标企业的交易行为。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Enterprises with demand for cross-border acquisition. 	具有跨境并购需求的企业。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Flexible guarantee methods.	1．担保方式灵活。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The borrowers may adopt a number of guarantee methods including mortgage, pledge and security of guaranty.	可采用抵押、质押、保证担保等多种方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Evident network advantages.	2.网络优势明显。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has a large number of branches and outlets which are reasonably distributed, have complete facilities, and cover each sector of the national economy. It also has the most advanced customer information system network and wide social relation network.	工商银行拥有数量众多、布局合理、设施完备的覆盖国民经济各行业的分支机构网络，最先进的客户信息系统网络和广泛的社会关系网络。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Three Settlement Products	第三节 结算产品	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Remittance	一、汇款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Remittance is a settlement product with which ICBC pays a specified sum to the payee on demand.	汇款是工商银行应汇款人的要求，将指定的款项支付给收款人的一种结算产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Remittance is generally divided into inward remittance and outward remittance, or divided into domestic remittance and cross-border remittance, of which cross-border remittance is divided into SWIFT remittance and ICBC cross-border remittance.	汇款一般分为汇入汇款和汇出汇款，按是否跨境分为境内汇款和跨境汇款。 其中跨境汇款产品又可分为SWIFT汇款和工行跨境汇款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Domestic remittance refers to the remittance within ICBC and inter-bank remittance conducted via domestic bank clearing system.	1.境内汇款是通过境内的银行清算体系进行的工商银行系统内和跨行汇款产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. SWIFT remittance refers to the global remittance realized by banks depending on the global communication network of SWIFT, which is mainly to meet the global remittance needs of bank customers.	2．SWIFT汇款是银行间利用SWIFT组织的全球通讯网络实现的全球汇款产品，主要满足银行客户的全球汇款需要。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. ICBC cross-border remittance refers to the cross-border remittance between worldwide institutions of ICBC depending on the clearing network of ICBC.	3．工行跨境汇款是利用工商银行自有的清算网络实现的工商银行全球机构之间的跨境汇款产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Domestic remittance is mainly used for personal and corporate customers provided that the remitter and the remittee are located within the territory of the same country.	1. 境内汇款主要应用于收、付款人均处于同一国家境内的个人和对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. SWIFT remittance is mainly used for personal and corporate customers of cross-border remittance who have no special requirements on remittance.	2. SWIFT汇款主要应用于无特殊汇款要求的办理跨境汇款的个人和对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. ICBC cross-border remittance is applicable to the personal and corporate customers of cross-border remittance, on condition that there are branches or correspondent banks of ICBC in the places of both receipt and payment. 	3.工行跨境汇款适用于收付款地都有工商银行或其代理行，要求办理跨境汇款的个人和对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Domestic remittance is realized by the ICBC clearing system or the domestic inter-bank clearing system, which can meet customers' rapid collection needs.	1.境内汇款通过工商银行系统内或境内银行间清算体系实现，能满足客户快速的收款需要。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. SWIFT remittance has a wide coverage as a majority of the banks in the world have participated in the clearing network with the SWIFT as the medium, with which remitters can freely select the receiving banks.	2．SWIFT汇款覆盖范围广，全球大部分银行均已参加以SWIFT为中介的清算网络，汇款人可较为自由地选择收款银行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. ICBC cross-border remittance is realized by the ICBC clearing system, enjoying the advantages of rapid collection, low remittance cost and wide service channels. 	3.工行跨境汇款通过工商银行系统内清算体系实现，具有到账速度快、汇款成本低、服务渠道广的优势。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Personal F/X remittance settled in advance	二、个人预结汇汇款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal F/X remittance settled in advance means a specific remittance method by which the remitter may convert the foreign currency to RMB at the specified rate of ICBC quoted on the date of remittance so that the remittee will receive the remittance in RMB, when the remitter handles remittance with ICBC with the remittee located in the territory of China.	个人预结汇汇款是指汇款人在工商银行办理收款人所在地为中国境内的汇款业务时，可按工商银行当日预结汇汇款的指定结汇汇率将所汇款项结成人民币、以人民币形式解付收款人的特定汇款方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal customers of remittance to the remittees in China, who have demand for exchange settlement and intend to lock up exchange rate fluctuation risk in advance.	有向中国境内收款人汇款，收款人有结汇需求、需要提前锁定汇率波动风险的个人客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Lock up exchange rate fluctuation risk in advance.	1.提前锁定汇率波动风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
A remittee who has an account with an outlet of ICBC in China may directly receive the inward remittance in RMB, so as to ward off the losses possibly incurred by exchange rate fluctuation to the remittee.	收款人在中国境内工商银行网点开有账户，可直接收到以人民币入账的汇入款项，避免了汇率波动可能给收款人造成的损失。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Convenient remittee procedures.	2.收款人手续简便。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The fund remitted by a remitter is denominated in a foreign currency, but the remittee’s recording currency is RMB, so as to relieve the remittee of the troubles in handling exchange settlement formalities at a bank counter.	汇款人汇出的资金为外币，但收款人入账的金额为人民币，免去了收款人到银行柜面办理结汇手续的麻烦。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Banker’s Promissory Note	三、银行本票	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Banker’s promissory note is a note issued by ICBC promising to unconditionally pay a specified sum of money to the payee or the bearer at sight.	银行本票是工商银行签发的，承诺在见票时无条件支付确定金额给收款人或者持票人的票据。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Promissory bank note business includes such procedures as issue, payment, clearing, refund and loss report (cancellation of loss reporting).	银行本票业务包括出票、付款、结清、退款、挂失（解挂）等业务环节。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal and corporate customers handling various intra-city settlements.	办理各种同城款项结算的个人或对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. High credit.	1.信用度高。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It is secured by the credit of ICBC, and is issued and paid by the bank.	以工商银行的信用为付款保证，由银行签发并付款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Safe and convenient.	2.安全方便。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The note is payable at sight within the specified regions by presenting to ICBC for payment.	在指定区域内均可向工商银行提示付款，银行见票即付。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC also provides such services as return or loss reporting of related notes to guarantee customers’ fund safety.	工商银行还同时提供相关票据的退票、挂失等服务，保障客户的资金安全。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IV. Check	四、支票	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Check is a negotiable instrument issued by a drawer and the bank entrusted with check deposit business shall unconditionally pay the specified sum of money to the payee or the bearer at sight.	支票是出票人签发的，委托办理支票存款业务的银行见票无条件支付确定金额给收款人或者持票人的票据。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The cash checks and the ordinary checks used in withdrawal of cash must comply with domestic regulations on cash management.	签发现金支票和用于支取现金的普通支票，必须符合本国现金管理的规定。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The identity certificates of the payee must be legitimate and valid.	对于收款人为个人的现金支票，收款人的身份证明证件必须合法有效。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Checks are divided into cash checks, transfer checks and ordinary checks.	支票分为现金支票、转账支票和普通支票。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Cash checks can be only used in withdrawal of cash; transfer checks can be only used in transfer, including transfer by endorsement; checks not bearing the word of “Cash” or “Transfer” are ordinary checks, which can be used in either withdrawal of cash or transfer.	现金支票只能用于支取现金，转账支票只能用于转账，但可背书转让；支票上未印有“现金”或“转账”字样的为普通支票，普通支票既可用于支取现金也可用于转账。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标用户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate and personal customers with settlement accounts in ICBC.	在工商银行开立结算账户的对公客户和个人客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Easy-to-use, convenient and flexible.	1.使用方便，手续简便、灵活。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Checks may be transferred many times by endorsement and become a negotiable payment instrument.	2.可通过背书方式多次转让，成为流通的支付工具。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
V. Draft	五、汇票	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Draft is an instrument issued by ICBC at the request of a customer, which indicates the currency and par value, and is held and carried by the customer and may be used in non-local payment or withdrawal.	汇票是指工商银行根据客户要求签发，标明币种和票据面额，由客户持有、携带，并到异地办理支付或取款的一种银行票据。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
When a customer needs to make payment to a non-local individual or institution, the customer may draw a draft in ICBC, and then carry the draft to withdraw or pay to other individual or institution at the destination, as the payment method for transactions.	当客户需要向异地个人或者机构支付款项时，可在工商银行开立汇票，之后将票据携带至目的地提款或者交付其他个人及机构，作为交易款项的支付方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal or corporate customers unwilling to carry cash but having the demand for remittance or payment by way of drafts or under the circumstances where the payee is uncertain.	不愿随身携带现金或收款人不确定，具有以票据形式进行汇款或支付需求的个人或对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. High applicability.	1.使用范围广泛。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Drafts can be carried with individuals and receivable on demand.	票随人走，人到款到，凭票收款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Safe and convenient.	2.安全方便。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The drafts are payable on demand within ICBC and its banking partners.	工商银行及其合作银行范围内见票即付。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC also provides such services as return, loss reporting or stopping of payment of related notes to guarantee customers’ fund safety.	工商银行还同时提供相关票据的退票、挂失、止付等服务，保障客户的资金安全。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Cost-effective.	3.价格低廉。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The issue and collection with acceptance of drafts are cost-effective.	票据的开立和托收兑付的费用相对低廉。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VI. Collection	六、托收	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Collection is a settlement method by which a customer sends related bills, including checks and drafts, to ICBC and entrusts it with collection from the payer.	托收是指客户将支票、汇票等有关单据交送工商银行，委托工商银行向付款人收取款项的一种结算方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Collection is divided into clean collection and documentary collection.	托收业务分为光票托收和跟单托收。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Clean collection means a customer provides such financial instruments as bank draft, banker’s promissory note, personal check or traveler’s check which are not accompanied with any shipping documents, and submits them to ICBC (collecting bank) for collection.	1.光票托收是指客户仅提供银行汇票、银行本票、公司支票、私人支票、旅行支票等等金融票据而无需附有任何货运单据，交托工商银行（托收行）代收款项。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Clean collection is categorized into sight crediting collection (cash letter) and final crediting collection (collection).	光票托收分为立即贷记托收方式（CASH LETTER）和最终贷记托收方式（COLLECTION）。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Under the sIght crediting collection, ICBC sends bills to the designated collecting bank, which, at the request of ICBC, forthwith credit to the account of ICBC by way of T+1; in case that the balance of the payer’s account is insufficient and falls within the recourse period stipulated by the commercial paper law or related laws and regulations of each country, the collecting bank shall reserve the right of recourse against ICBC.	立即贷记托收方式，即工商银行寄送票据至指定代收行，代收行收到工商银行委托后以T+1方式立即贷记工商银行账户，但遇付款人账户余额不足等情况以及在各国票据法或有关法律规定的追索期内对工商银行保留追索权。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Under the final crediting collection (also known as crediting after payment), ICBC, as the entrusting bank, directly sends bills to the issuing bank/paying bank, and the latter reimburses ICBC by withholding money from the payer’s account, and reserves the right of recourse against ICBC within the recourse period prescribed by the commercial paper law or relevant laws of each country.	最终贷记托收方式又称收妥入账，即工商银行作为委托行直接寄送票据给出票行/付款行，出票行/付款行从付款人账户扣款后偿付工商银行，在各国票据法或有关法律规定的追索期内对工商银行保留追索权。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In case of the final crediting collection, ICBC may choose a correspondent bank, which has signed a clean collection agreement with ICBC, to send documents and collect funds.	最终贷记托收方式项下，工商银行也可选择和工商银行签订光票托收协议的代理行代为寄送票据和收款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Documentary collection means a customer delivers the documents, such as financial documents, accompanied with transport documents, to ICBC for collection.	2.跟单托收是指客户将金融票据随附有货物单据等其他合同要求的单据交托工商银行代收款项。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Documentary collection is categorized into import collection and export collection.	跟单托收可分为进口代收和出口托收。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Import collection means an overseas bank entrusts ICBC with collection, and ICBC delivers the collection documents sent by the overseas bank to the customer, and handle payment, acceptance or dishonor according to the customer’s instructions.	进口代收是指境外银行委托工商银行代收其托收款项的结算业务，工商银行将他行寄来的代收单据转交客户，根据客户提示办理付款、承兑或拒付。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Export collection means the payee (exporter), after transportation of cargo, delivers financial documents and cargo documents against the export to ICBC, and entrusts ICBC to collect money from the payer.	出口托收是指收款人（出口商）出运货物后，将出口项下的金融票据及货运单据递交工商银行，委托工商银行向付款人收取货款的一种托收方式。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Import and export enterprise customers using collection in settlement and individual or corporate customers collecting money by bill clearing. 	采用托收方式进行结算的进出口企业客户，以及通过票据结算方式收取款项需要的个人或对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Clean collection	1.光票托收	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Conveniently and readily used in overseas collection by various bills.	（1）方便快捷，可用于收取各种以票据形式收取的境外支付款项。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Very safe.	（2）安全性较高。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Import collection	2.进口代收	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) More convenient procedures and lower expenses as compared to L/C settlement.	（1）与信用证结算方式相比，手续更简便费用更低廉。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Eligible to enjoy the import collection bill financing services provided by ICBC to fill in the short-term fund gap, and arrange for processing or sale of import cargo as early as practicable so as to improve the efficiency of fund operation.	（2）可享受工商银行提供的进口代收押汇融资服务以解决短期资金融通问题，尽早取得进口货物安排加工或销售，提高资金营运效率。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Export collection	3.出口托收	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) More convenient procedures and lower expenses as compared to L/C settlement.	（1）与信用证结算方式相比，手续更简便费用更低廉。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Eligible to enjoy the export collection bill financing services provided by ICBC to receive payment in advance so as to fill in the short-term fund gap.	（2）可享受工商银行提供的出口托收押汇融资服务以预先收到货款，解决短期资金融通问题。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VII. Global Cash Management	七、全球现金管理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Global cash management means a series of financial product mixes, including internal fund transfer, collection, payment, account management, account information, investment and financing, provided by ICBC to assist corporate customers achieving effective global cash management. It provides customers with full-spectrum and comprehensive global cash management solutions, such as internal global cash management and external cash flow control, to help them efficiently manage receivables and payables, collect and allocate internal funds, timely and accurately obtain cash flow information, enjoy diversified investment opportunities and improve return on capital.	全球现金管理是指工商银行为协助企业客户进行有效全球现金管理而提供的内部资金调拨、收款、付款、账户管理、账户信息、投资、融资等一系列金融服务的组合产品，为客户提供从内部全球现金管理到外部现金流控制的全面、综合化的全球现金管理解决方案，帮助客户高效管理应收、应付款，归集、调剂内部资金，及时、准确获取现金流信息，提供多样化投资机会，提高资本投资回报率。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Global cash management mainly includes centralized collection and payment, cross-border physical fund pool and cross-border nominal fund pool.	主要包括集中收付款、跨境实体资金池、跨境名义资金池等产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Centralized collection and payment is a product designed to help domestic and overseas customers of ICBC flexibly handle fund collection and payment and improve their fund operation efficiency.	集中收付款产品是指帮助境内外客户灵活办理资金收付业务，提高资金使用效率的产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Cross-border physical fund pool is a product provided to cross-border group customers to utilize and manage the funds of their member units worldwide.	跨境实体资金池是指为跨国集团企业客户提供的、统一使用和管理世界各地集团内成员单位的资金的产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Cross-border nominal fund pool is a fund sharing product provided to cross-border group enterprises, with interest calculated on a consolidated basis.	跨境名义资金池是指为跨国集团企业客户提供的基于合并计息的资金共享产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Centralized collection.	1.集中收款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Enterprises intending to improve fund operation efficiency, promptly recover sales and labor income or centralize funds of branches.	希望提高资金使用效率，迅速回笼销售款、劳务费或归集分支机构款项的企业。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Centralized payment.	2.集中付款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Enterprises intending to send payment instructions by the counter of a bank, internet banking, bank-enterprise interconnection or SWIFT channels and managing their global payments in a uniform manner.	希望统一通过一家银行柜面、网上银行、银企互联或SWIFT渠道发送支付指令，统一管理全球付款的企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Cross-border fund pool.	3.跨境资金池。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Multinational enterprises which have many branches at home and abroad and need to allocate and manage their global funds, as well as overseas enterprises which need to calculate interest of funds in their fund pool accounts in a consolidated manner.	在境内、外建立多个分支机构，需要统一调剂、管理全球资金的跨国企业客户以及需要对资金池内账户进行合并计息的境外企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Centralized collection and payment has the features of “one-point link with customers, acceptance of many payment instructions and automatic processing by system”.	1.集中收付款产品具有“客户一点连接，支持多种支付指令，系统自动处理”的特点。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It allows the collection and payment between NOVA/FOVA and the accounts opened with global cash management banks partnering with ICBC.	支持NOVA\FOVA和全球现金管理合作行账户之间的收付。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Cross-border physical fund pool allows the existence of multiple currencies, the fund allocation between accounts of domestic and overseas banking partners, multi-tier account system, a number of centralization and allocation methods and many centralizations and allocations.	2.跨境实体资金池支持多币种，支持境内外、合作行账户之间资金调拨，支持多级账户体系，支持多种归集、下拨方式，支持多个归集下拨场次。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Cross-border nominal fund pool can improve customers’ interest income and expense, strengthen their internal management, reduce their debts and lower fund transfer costs.	3.跨境名义资金池能够改善客户利息收支状况，加强客户内部管理，减少客户外债，减少资金划转成本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VIII. Letter of Credit (L/C)	八、信用证	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
L/C is an instrument issued by ICBC to the exporter according to the instructions of an importer, representing its guarantee to perform the obligation of payment against documents upon maturity.	信用证是指工商银行根据进口商的指示向出口商开出的，凭规定单据履行到期付款义务的保证性文件。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
L/C is divided into sight L/C and usance L/C depending on the payment period.	根据信用证付款期限的不同可分为即期信用证和远期信用证。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Sight L/C means the issuing bank promises to effect payment within a reasonable period (not more than five working days starting from the next working day upon receipt of documents) after an exporter delivers to the bank sight drafts and documents complying with L/C requirements according to the provisions of L/C; usance L/C is a L/C that the bank promises to effect payment on the future due date after the beneficiary submits documents.	前者指出口商根据信用证的规定，将符合信用证要求的即期汇票及单据交银行后，开证行保证在收到单据后合理的期限内（不超过自收到单据次一工作日起算的五个工作日）付款的信用证；后者指银行保证在受益人交单后承诺在远期到期日予以付款的信用证。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
L/C is divided into sight payment L/C, deferred payment L/C, acceptance L/C and negotiation L/C depending on the way of payment.	根据信用证兑付方式的不同可分为即期付款信用证、延期付款信用证、承兑信用证和议付信用证四种。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Among them, negotiation L/C is categorized into freely negotiable L/C and restricted negotiable L/C depending on whether there are restrictions on negotiation.	其中议付信用证根据是否限制议付又可分为：自由议付信用证和限制议付信用证。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Freely negotiable L/C is a L/C that the issuing bank allows any bank to negotiate the drafts and/or documents of an exporter; restricted negotiable L/C is a L/C that the issuing bank only authorizes the designated bank to negotiate the drafts and/or documents of an exporter.	自由议付信用证指开证行允许任何银行对出口商的汇票和单据进行议付的信用证；限制议付信用证指开证行只允许指定银行对出口商汇票和单据进行议付的信用证。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
L/C is divided into confirmed L/C and unconfirmed L/C depending on whether it is promised to be confirmed by another bank.	根据信用证是否由另一家银行保证兑付可分为保兑信用证和不保兑信用证。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In case of a confirmed L/C, another bank promises to effect payment against the bills complying with the terms and conditions of L/C; in case of unconfirmed L/C, no other banks promise to effect payment against the bills satisfying the terms and conditions of L/C.	前者指开出的信用证由另一家银行保证对符合信用证条款规定的单据履行付款；后者指开出的信用证未经其他银行保证对符合信用证条款规定的单据履行付款。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
L/C can also be divided into transferable L/C and nontransferable L/C depending on whether it is marked “Transferable”.	根据信用证是否注明“可转让”字样可分为可转让信用证和不可转让信用证。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Importers and exporters which perform settlement by way of L/C.	采用信用证方式进行结算的进出口贸易客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Convert commercial credit into bank credit so as to facilitate trade process and improve the safety and convenience of trade payment and collection.	1.使商业信用转换为银行信用，从而促使贸易的顺利进行，使贸易资金收付更具安全性和便利性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Provide supporting financing products, such as import bill advance, buyer’s usance L/C, L/C agency payment, delivery against bank guarantee and bill of lading endorsement, in related trading areas depending on L/C, so as to meet customers’ trade financing needs.	2.以信用证为依托，在相关贸易环节上提供进口押汇、买方远期信用证、信用证代付、提货担保、提单背书等配套融资产品，满足客户的贸易融资需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Four Agency Products	第四节 代理产品	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Payroll Payment Agency Service	一、代发工资	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Payroll payment agency service is an agency service provided by ICBC, according to the entrustment of applicants, to pay wages, welfare expense, labor protection fee, pension fund and such other remuneration and welfare to the accounts of the employees at the request of the applicants.	代发工资业务是指工商银行接受代发工资单位委托，代理代发工资单位向其员工账户发放工资、福利费、劳动保护费、养老金等工薪福利的一项代理业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customers which need to pay wages, welfare expense, labor protection fee, pension fund and such other remuneration and welfare to their employees. 	适用于具有向其员工账户发放工资、福利费、劳动保护费、养老金等各类工薪福利需求的对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Variety of salary currencies.	1.工资币种多样。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Salaries can be paid in HKD, Pataca, Thailand Baht, Indonesia Rupiah, USD, Yen and Euro, etc.	代发工资的币种可以是港币、澳门元、越南盾、印尼盾、美元、日元、欧元等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Multiple channels.	2.办理渠道丰富。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Applicants may handle payroll payment by internet banking and counters conveniently and readily. 	代发工资单位可以通过网上银行和柜面两大渠道办理代发工资业务，方便快捷。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Agency Settlement	二、代理结算	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Agency settlement products are the products designed by ICBC to handle agency settlement according to the entrustment of customers, depending on ICBC’s settlement channels, system platform and payment instruments.	代理结算产品是指工商银行受客户的委托，借助工商银行的结算渠道、系统平台和支付工具等资源，代理其办理结算业务的产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Agency settlement includes inter-bank settlement, bank-futures company transfer and BSP agency business.	代理结算包括代理同业结算、银期转账、代理BSP业务等多项代理结算类业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Inter-bank agency settlement means the payment settlement, including bank draft, remittance, collection and collection with acceptance, handled by ICBC according to the entrustment of other banks.	（1）代理同业结算是指工商银行接受其他银行的委托、代为办理的银行汇票、汇兑、委托收款、托收承付等支付结算业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Bank-futures company transfer means the real time two-way fund transfer between the settlement accounts of investors and margin accounts of futures companies provided by a bank depending on its real time internetworking with future companies.	（2）银期转账是指通过银行与期货公司的实时联网，提供投资者结算账户与期货公司保证金账户间双向实时资金转账的业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) BSP agency business means the agency fund clearing business provided by a bank to the aviation association for its members to book or return airline tickets.	（3）代理BSP业务是指是面向航空协会提供的，在其为会员办理机票订购、退票等业务时所进行的代理资金清算业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Financial institutions and enterprises which have the need for fund settlement via ICBC.	金融同业机构、企业等有由工商银行代为进行资金结算需求的客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Provide customers with convenient and fast fund clearing services and reconciliation services depending on the outlet and settlement network advantages of ICBC.	1.可以发挥工商银行的网点优势和结算网络优势，为客户提供便利、快捷的资金清算服务及对账服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Increase fee-based business income, improve the quality of on-balance-sheet asset and liability business of the bank while reducing the risks arising from operation and management.	2.增加中间业务收入，改善银行表内资产负债业务的质量，降低经营管理中的风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Five Bank Card Products	第五节 银行卡产品	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Debit Card	一、借记卡	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Debit card is a bank card issued by ICBC, which has no overdraft function and can be used in consumption/withdrawal after the customer deposits money in the card. Debit card, which is divided into magnetic strip card and magnetic strip and chip combined card, provides personal customers with such daily financial services as personal settlement, e-banking, investment and wealth management.	借记卡是指工商银行发行的，客户先存款后消费（或取现），不具有透支功能的银行卡，可为个人客户提供个人结算、电子银行、投资理财等日常金融服务，包含磁条与磁条芯片复合两种介质类型。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Debit cards can also be categorized into single-currency (local currency of the card issuing bank), dual-currency (RMB and local currency of the card issuing bank) and multi-currency debit cards by the currency supported, or categorized into ordinary debit card and Elite Club account card by target customer, of which the former is issued to personal customers, and the latter to the high and medium-end personal customers.	根据支持的币种分为单币种（发卡行本地币种）、双币种（人民币、发卡行本地币种）以及多币种借记卡；根据发行目标客户分为普通借记卡和理财金账户卡，其中普通借记卡面向所有个人客户发行，理财金账户卡面向中高端个人客户发行。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal customers who need to handle various businesses using the debit cards, and meet the local conditions for issue of debit cards.	需要使用借记卡办理各项业务，且符合当地借记卡发卡条件的个人客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Comprehensive account and multifunctional card.	1.综合账户，一卡多能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It supports various savings deposits, including demand and time deposits, and can manage several accounts with one card. In addition to the local currency of the place of the card issuing bank, the debit card can deposit other currencies, manage comprehensive accounts and realize multiple functions.	可支持办理各类型储蓄存款，包括活期、定期等，实现一卡管理多账户；同时，除可存入发卡行本地币种外，还可存入其它币种，充分体现综合账户、一卡多能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Handle within the system and enjoy fee preference.	2.系统内办理，手续费优惠。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Handling business with the debit card at any outlet or channel of ICBC may enjoy preferential fees.	在工商银行全球任何网点和渠道持卡办理业务可以享受相应的收费优惠。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Real time transfer and remittance.	3.转账汇款，实时到账。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
If a debit card holder transfers, by password or signature, funds to a local or non-local account of ICBC through such channels as operating outlet, self-service equipment, internet banking or telephone banking, the funds will be received on a real time basis.	持卡客户使用密码或者签名通过工商银行营业网点、自助设备、网上银行和电话银行等渠道，向同城或异地工商银行账户转账，所转款项可实时到账。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Enjoy various convenient services depending on e-banking channel.	4.借助电子银行渠道，享受各项便捷服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers may handle various businesses by self-service equipment, internet banking and telephone banking and enjoy round-the-clock unrestricted self-banking services.	客户可持卡在自助设备、网上银行和电话银行上办理各类业务，享受24小时无限制的自助服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. Support investment and wealth management services and help customers achieve appreciation of assets.	5.支持投资理财服务，力助客户资产升值。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers may utilize debit cards to handle various wealth management businesses, including, fund, foreign exchange trading, stock, treasury bond, insurance and precious metal, to facilitate investment and wealth management.	客户可通过借记卡办理基金、外汇买卖、股票、国债、保险、贵金属等各类理财业务，使投资理财之路变得更加通畅。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers may also utilize debit cards as loan and repayment accounts and apply for various loan businesses.	客户还可将借记卡作为贷款放款和还款账户，申办各种贷款业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
6. Exclusive VIP services.	6. 专属贵宾服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Elite Club account card holders may enjoy a series of VIP services provided by ICBC, including exclusive VIP channel, exclusive fee preference and expert services for wealth management.	理财金账户卡持卡客户可以专享工商银行提供的专属贵宾通道、专享费用优惠、专家理财服务等一系列贵宾服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Credit Card	二、贷记卡	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit card is a bank card issued by ICBC to grant a certain credit line to the card holder and allow the card holder to overdraw free of interest within a specified period. Deposits in the card are interest-free and the card can be used at home and abroad.	贷记卡（信用卡）是工商银行给予持卡人一定信用额度、持卡人可在信用额度内先消费后还款、按规定享有免息还款期待遇、存款无息、境内外通用的银行卡。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit cards are divided into dual-currency credit cards and single-currency credit cards.	贷记卡按账户币种分为双币贷记卡和单币贷记卡。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers who have overdraft demand.	存在透支消费需求的客户群体。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. High applicability.	1.使用范围广。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Debit card can be used in all the outlets and chartered merchants of ICBC as well as the chartered merchants, self-service ATM terminals and such other business places with the logs of corresponding card organizations.	贷记卡可在工商银行各网点和特约商户，以及带有卡片对应卡组织标识的特约商户和自动取款机等受理点使用。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit card is settled in the local currency of the card holder and a certain designated foreign currency, and has the functions of overdraft, transfer and withdrawal.	以持卡人本地货币和某一指定外币结算，具有透支消费、转账结算、存取现金等功能。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Overdraft free of interest.	2.透支消费免息。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
In case of overdraft within the credit limit, the card holder may enjoy a certain period of repayment free of interest if he pays up all the arrearage prior to the repayment date specified in the bank statement.	对于信用额度内的消费透支，持卡人在对账单规定的还款日期前全部还款，即可享受一定的免息还款期。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Merchant Acquiring	三、商户收单	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Merchant acquiring means the fund settlement services provided by ICBC to merchants for consumption, transfer, preauthorization and confirmation of preauthorization, as well as such services as authorization, clearing, dishonor, transfer of bill, return of bill and risk control in the process of business operation.	商户收单是工商银行向商户提供的消费、转账、预授权、预授权确认等业务的资金结算服务，以及在业务过程中出现的授权、清算、拒付、调单、退单和风险管控等服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Merchants allowing consumers to make payment and settlement by bank cards.	适用于接受消费者通过银行卡进行消费支付结算的商户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Accept a number of brands	1.受理多种品牌	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It accepts such brands as China UnionPay, VISA, Master, JCB, American Express and Diners cards.	受理品牌包括银联、VISA、MASTER CARD、JCB、运通和大莱。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Provide a number of acceptance methods	2.提供多种受理方式	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC provides various bank card acceptance methods, including magnetic strip card payment, chip card payment, contact payment and contactless payment.	工商银行提供多种银行卡受理方式，既支持受理刷磁条卡支付，也支持芯片卡支付，同时支持接触式和非接触式支付。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Support a number of consumption types	3.支持多种消费类型	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC supports the acquiring of a number of consumption types, including ordinary consumption, quick consumption, credit authorized consumption, offline consumption, consumption by installment payment and preauthorized consumption.	工商银行支持普通消费、快速消费、信用授权消费、离线消费、分期付款消费、预授权消费等多种消费类型的收单。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Provide clearing and reconciliation services	4.提供清算及对账服务	sample1-en-sample1-zh
After clearing with a merchant, ICBC will transfer the bank card payment funds to the account designated by the merchant and provide the merchant with reconciliation vouchers.	工商银行与商户进行清算后，将银行卡支付资金划拨至商户指定账户，并向商户提供对账凭证。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Six Guarantee and Commitment Products	第六节 担保承诺产品	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Guarantee	一、担保	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Guarantee means a written commitment made by ICBC, as a guarantor, in the form of letter of guarantee or standby L/C, to the guaranteed party at its request, promising to perform the repayment responsibility in case the guaranteed party fails to repay debts or perform obligations according to the contract signed by the guaranteed party and the beneficiary.	担保是指工商银行作为担保人，应被担保人的申请，以保函或备用信用证等书面形式向受益人承诺，当被担保人未按其与受益人签订的合同约定偿还债务或履行义务时，由工商银行代其履行偿付责任的法律行为。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Guarantee is divided into financing guarantee and non-financing guarantee by the nature of fundamental trading contracts.	按基础交易合同性质划分，担保业务分为融资类担保和非融资类担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Financing guarantee means the guarantee provided by ICBC for the responsibilities or obligations of the guaranteed party under the financing transactions.	1.融资类担保是指工商银行为被担保人在融资性交易项下的责任或义务提供的担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Financing guarantee mainly includes:	主要包括：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Loan guarantee;	（1）借款担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Guarantee for issue of negotiable securities (including ordinary corporate bonds and convertible bonds but excluding stocks);	（2）发行有价证券（包括企业普通债券、可转换债券等，不包括股票）担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Overdraft guarantee;	（3）透支担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(4) Guarantee for deferred payment;	（4）延期付款担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(5) Financial leasing guarantee;	（5）融资租赁担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(6) Guarantee for compensation trade repaid in spot exchange; and	（6）以现汇偿还的补偿贸易担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(7) Other guarantee products stipulated by local laws and regulations and defined by ICBC.	（7）符合当地法律法规和工商银行融资类担保定义的其他担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Non-financing guarantee means the guarantee provided by ICBC for the responsibilities or obligations of the guaranteed party under the non-financing transactions. Non-financing guarantee mainly includes:	2.非融资类担保是指工商银行为被担保人在非融资性交易项下责任或义务提供的担保。 主要包括：	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Guarantee under trade or project, mainly include bid guarantee, performance guarantee, advance payment guarantee, quality warranty and maintenance guarantee, payment guarantee, retention guarantee, guarantee for marine accident and customs guarantee.	（1）贸易或工程项下的担保。 包括投标担保、履约担保、预付款担保、质量及维修担保、付款担保、留置金担保、海事担保、关税担保等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Guarantee for compensation trade repaid in kind; and	（2）以实物偿还的补偿贸易担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Other guarantee products stipulated by local laws and regulations and defined by ICBC.	（3）符合当地法律法规和工商银行非融资类担保定义的其他担保。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customers that desire to obtain credit support from banks.	希望银行提供信用支持的企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers may use a bank’s credit guarantee to develop their operating activities.	客户可以利用银行信用担保支持其经营活动的开展。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Standby Facility	二、备用贷款	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Standby facility means a legally binding credit commitment made by ICBC that allows the borrower to draw down loans according to the contractual terms and conditions, in order to meet the borrower’s contingent financing demand within a period of time to come.	备用贷款是指工商银行为满足借款人未来一定时期内或有融资需求，向其出具的具有法律约束力、允许其在需要时按照合同约定条件提取贷款的信贷承诺。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With little probability of being drawn down by customers, standby facility is granted for use only when needed and is mainly used as credit support for customers’ issue of bonds and commercial papers.	备用贷款在发放时预计客户提款可能性较小，仅做为备用，主要是用于客户在发行债券、商业票据等行为时提供信用支持。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customers that desire to obtain credit support from ICBC.	需要工商银行提供信用支持的对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Customers may use bank credit to cut their direct financing costs.	客户可利用银行信用降低其对外直接融资成本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Commitment	三、承诺	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Commitment is a credit facility of ICBC to grant loans to customers from time to time upon their request within the valid commitment period and the conditions, amount and interest rate specified in legally binding formal agreements signed between ICBC and loan customers, and collect commitment fees from these customers.	承诺是指工商银行与借款客户达成的一种具有法律约束力的正式协议，银行在有效承诺期内，按照双方约定的条件、金额和利率等，随时准备应客户需求提供贷款，并有权向借款客户收取承诺费的一种授信业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Loan commitments are divided into irrevocable commitments, commitments revocable anytime and unconditionally and conditionally revocable commitments, depending on whether they are revocable or not and the revocation conditions.	按照是否可撤销及撤销条件，贷款承诺业务划分为不可撤销、随时无条件可撤销和有条件可撤销三类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Irrevocable commitment means a commitment that cannot be revoked by ICBC without approval of the customer.	不可撤销承诺，是指不经客户允许，工商银行不得随意撤消的承诺。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Commitment revocable anytime and unconditionally means a loan commitment that can be revoked by ICBC unconditionally at any time without providing a prior notice, or the loan commitment that can be effectively and automatically revoked for reasons of the borrower’s credit deterioration.	随时无条件可撤销承诺，是指工商银行可在任何时候且不需要事先通知就可以无条件取消的承诺或者由于借款人信用状况恶化，可以有效地自动取消的贷款承诺。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Conditionally revocable commitment means a commitment with the revocation terms other than those specified for the preceding two commitments.	有条件可撤销承诺，是指具有前两类承诺约定的撤销条款以外的其他撤销条款的承诺。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Syndicated loan commitment is a special commitment whereby several banks sign a legally binding contract or agreement with a corporate or personal customer to define their respective rights and obligations and grant a specific amount of credits to the customer within an agreed effective period in future according to the terms and conditions already agreed upon.	银团贷款承诺的一种特殊形式是贷款承诺，即由多家银行与企业和个人客户签订具有法律约束力的合同或协议，明确权利义务，在未来约定的有效期内，按照商定的条款为客户提供约定数额信贷支持的承诺。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Individual or corporate customers that need credit support from ICBC. 	需要工商银行提供信用支持的个人客户或企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Provide credit support for customers, ensure customers to obtain financing in future, and help improve customers’ credit rating. Section Seven	为客户提供信用支持，为客户提供未来可获得融资资金的保证，起到提高客户资信等级的作用。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Asset Custody Products	第七节 资产托管产品	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Asset Custody for QFII	一、QFII资产托管	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Asset custody for qualified foreign institutional investor (QFII) means a custodian service that an institution of ICBC within the territory of China is entrusted by a foreign investor or a foreign lead custodian bank in China with custody of the property managed by an asset manager on behalf of an investor and supervision of the manager’s operation so as to prevent custodian asset risks.	QFII（合格境外机构投资者）资产托管是指工商银行在中国境内的机构接受中国境外投资者或境外主托管行的委托，对投资者委托资产管理人管理的财产进行保管并监督投资管理人运作，防范委托资产风险的托管服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC also provides such services as investment clearing, accounting, asset appraisal and information disclosure according to investors’ asset operation characteristics.	工商银行还根据投资者的资产运作特点提供相应的投资清算、会计核算、资产估值、信息披露等服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
QFIIs, which engage in investment business within the territory of China with approval of the competent authorities in charge of relevant industries of China, and need to put their funds under custody according to laws and regulations, or the fund companies, securities companies, insurance companies, commercial banks and pension funds intending to engage in custodian business.	适用于获得中国政府相关行业主管部门批准的合格境外机构投资者在中国境内投资开办业务，按照法律规定必须对其资金进行托管或者自己有意愿开办托管业务的基金公司、证券公司、保险公司、商业银行、养老基金等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. As one of the banks first running QFII custody business in China, ICBC is familiar with China’s securities market policy and QFII system, and has successfully assisted a large number of customers exploring their business in China.	1.工商银行是中国境内最早开办QFII托管业务的银行之一，熟悉中国证券市场政策及QFII制度，成功协助大批客户拓展中国市场业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. ICBC is the largest custodian bank in China and has ranked first for 12 consecutive years in terms of the market share of assets under custody.	2.工商银行是中国境内最大的托管银行，托管资产份额连续12年保持市场第一。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. ICBC is a professional custodian bank with its own advanced custody business system, and the first bank in China passing the SAS70 certification. Its custodian services have come up to the international standards.	3.工商银行是具有专业水平的托管银行，拥有自主研发的先进托管业务系统，是中国国内首家通过SAS70认证的银行，托管服务达到国际标准化要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. As a leading commercial bank in the world, ICBC has a rapid clearing network, adequate RMB funds and strong A share settlement capacity, and can provide efficient and diversified services for QFII customers.	4.工商银行是最具实力的商业银行之一，拥有快速的清算网络、充裕的人民币资金和强大的A股结算能力，能为QFII客户提供高效全面的服务支持。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Asset Custody for QDII	二、QDII资产托管	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Asset custody for qualified domestic institutional investor (QDII) means a custodian service that an institution of ICBC within the territory of China is entrusted by a domestic investor with custody of the property managed by an asset manager on behalf of an investor and supervision of the manager’s operation so as to prevent custodian asset risks.	QDII（合格境内机构投资者）资产托管是指工商银行在中国境内的机构接受中国境内投资者的委托，对投资者委托资产管理人管理的财产进行保管并监督投资管理人运作，防范委托资产风险的托管服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC also provides such services as investment clearing, accounting, asset appraisal, information disclosure as well as exchange settlement and sales, and inward and outward remittance of funds relating to overseas investment by QDIIs, in consideration of investors’ asset operation characteristics.	工商银行还根据投资者的资产运作特点提供相应的投资清算、会计核算、资产估值、信息披露以及与QDII境外投资相关的结售汇、资金汇出入等服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

Its internal control of custodian services has come up to the international standards.	2.工商银行是具有专业水平的托管银行，拥有自主开发的先进托管业务系统，是中国国内首家通过SAS70审计认证的银行，托管服务内控水平达到国际标准化要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. ESCROW custody	三、ESCROW托管	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ESCROW custody means an asset custody business that ICBC is commissioned by fund assignment trustor and the takeover trustor to manage cross-border funds, effect payment when the stipulated events occur or the stipulated conditions are fulfilled, and supervise and disclose information on the cross-border fund use.	ESCROW托管是指工商银行受资金让与委托人、受让委托人委托，保管跨境资金，当约定的事件发生或约定的条件实现时支付资金，并对跨境资金使用情况进行监督和信息披露的一种资产托管业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ESCROW custody includes but is not limited to the commodity transactions, service transactions, equity transfer, M & A and debt restructuring between the assignment trustor and the takeover trustor.	包括但不限于让与委托人与受让委托人之间发生商品交易、服务交易、股权转让、兼并收购、债务重组等事项所产生的ESCROW托管。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Enterprises intending to conduct cross-border restructuring, expansion or asset disposal, M & A, enterprises intending to conduct cross-border transactions, and payment of commodities, services or funds, and foreign investment banks, risk investment companies, private equity companies and large multinational enterprises. 	有意进行跨境重组、扩张或者出卖资产、合并及收购的企业客户，需要进行跨境交易买卖，支付货物、服务或资金的企业客户，中国境外的投资银行、风险投资、私募基金公司，大型跨境企业等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
