Its internal control of custodian services has come up to the international standards.	1.工商银行是具有专业水平的托管银行，拥有自主开发的先进托管业务系统，是中国国内首家通过SAS70审计认证的银行，托管服务内控水平达到国际标准化要求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. ICBC has a wide customer service network and widely distributed branches and outlets that can provide custodian services anytime and anywhere.	2.工商银行具有广泛的客户服务网络，分布广泛的分支机构和网点可为客户提供随时随地的托管服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Section Eight Investment Banking Products	第八节 投资银行产品	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Credit Investigation	一、资信调查	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit investigation is an investment banking product that ICBC issues a credit investigation report for the trustor to investigate and objectively reflect the credit status of the investigated party, the investigated asset and the investigated market as required by the trustor.	资信调查是指工商银行为委托人出具资信调查报告，调查并客观反映委托人所要求的被调查人、被调查资产、被调查市场的资信状况的投资银行产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Credit investigations include entity investigation, asset investigation, market investigation and grouped credit investigation.	资信调查包括单位调查、资产调查、市场调查和组合资信调查四大类。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Entity investigation	1.单位调查	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Entity investigation means the service provided by ICBC to investigate the investigated entity’s registration information, correspondent banks, financial and operating status according to the entrustment of the trustor, and issue an entity investigation report to the trustor.	单位调查是指工商银行接受委托人委托，对被调查单位的注册信息、往来银行、财务状况及经营情况等进行调查，并向委托人出具单位调查报告的业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Asset investigation	2.资产调查	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Asset investigation means the service provided by ICBC to investigate the investigated entity’s asset type, ownership and value according to the entrustment of the trustor, and issue an asset investigation report to the trustor.	资产调查是指工商银行接受委托人委托，对被调查单位资产的类型、权属及价值等状况进行调查，并向委托人出具资产调查报告的业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Market investigation	3.市场调查	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Market investigation means the service provided by ICBC to investigate the information on a certain region or industry according to the entrustment of the trustor, and issue a market investigation report to the trustor.	市场调查是指工商银行接受委托人委托，就某一地区、行业等情况进行调查，并向委托人出具市场调查报告的业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Grouped credit investigation	4.组合资信调查	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Grouped credit investigation means the service provided by ICBC to group the investigation contents above according to the entrustment of the trustor, and submit a special investigation report to the trustor.	组合资信调查是指工商银行接受委托人委托，对以上各项调查内容进行按需组合，并向委托人提交专项调查报告的业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Enterprises with the demand for credit investigation.	具有资信调查业务需求的企业客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Worldwide service network.	1.遍布全球的服务网络。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has numerous service institutions which may provide convenient and rapid credit investigation services to customers.	工商银行服务机构众多，可为客户提供便捷的资信调查服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Rich business resources.	2.丰富的业务资源。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has the largest corporate customer base in the world and may fully meet customers’ investigation demand.	工商银行拥有全球最大的企业客户群资源，可充分满足客户的调查需求。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

IV. Investment and Financing Advisory	四、投融资顾问	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Investment and financing advisory means the individualized financial advisory services provided by ICBC to help customers optimize financing structure, including but not limited to the optimization of financing term structure, cost and currency.	投融资顾问是指工商银行为帮助客户优化融资结构而提供的个性化财务顾问服务，服务内容包括但不限于融资期限结构优化、成本优化、币种优化等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Investment and financing advisory is divided into general financing advisory, project financing advisory and structured financing advisory by the specific service content.	根据具体服务内容的不同，投融资顾问可分为一般融资顾问、项目融资顾问和结构化融资顾问。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. General financing advisory means the services, such as financial diagnosis, asset restructuring, financial instrument selection, external rating consultation, credit enhancement and debt service planning and cash flow and account management planning, provided by ICBC to customers when they apply for bank loans.	1.一般融资顾问是指工商银行在客户申请银行贷款的过程中，为其提供的财务诊断、资产重整、金融工具选择、外部评级咨询、信用增级与偿债方案设计、现金流与账户管理方案设计等顾问服务的业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Project financing advisory means various consulting services relating to project financing provided by ICBC according to the entrustment of the project sponsor, investor or project company, to design and assist in implementation of the shareholder investment plan, financing currency and maturity plan, credit enhancement plan, debt service plan, cash flow and account management plan and project franchise plan for the project, in order to diversify project risks and reduce financing costs.	2.项目融资顾问是指工商银行接受项目发起人、投资者或项目公司的委托，提供与项目融资相关的各项咨询服务，对项目的股东投资方案、融资币种和期限方案、信用增级方案、偿债方案、现金流与账户管理方案、项目特许权方案等进行设计并协助其落实，以达到分散项目风险、降低融资成本的目的。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Structured financing advisory means the investment banking business that ICBC takes advantage of equity, fixed-income, derivative or other financial products based on the debt products, to meet customers’ complex financing demands, including adjustment of capital structure, optimization of debt term and reduction of financing costs.	3.结构化融资顾问是指工商银行为达到调整客户资本结构、优化客户负债期限、降低客户融资成本等目的，以债务类产品为基础，组合使用股权类、固定收益类、衍生类或其他金融产品，满足客户复杂融资需求的投资银行业务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Enterprises, public institutions, governmental bodies and other social organizations intending to investment in the projects of resources development, infrastructure construction and manufacturing, and other customers with demand for investment and financing business.	拟对资源开发、基础设施建设、制造业等项目进行投资的企事业单位、政府机构和其他社会组织，以及其他有投融资业务需求的客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

Most life insurance products also have the functions of savings or investment, thereby preserving and increasing the asset value of customers.	大部分人寿保险产品还兼备储蓄或投资功能，使客户资产保值增值。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh

A fund pools money of numerous investors, and entrusts a fund manager with joint investment, so as to further give play to the scale advantages of funds and reduce investment costs.	基金将众多投资者的资金集中起来，委托基金管理人进行共同投资，有利于发挥资金的规模优势，降低投资成本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Fund is managed and operated by a fund manager depending on its large group of investment research fellows and strong information network. Section Ten Treasury Transaction Products	第十节 资金交易产品	sample1-en-sample1-zh
I. Paper Precious Metals Transactions	一、账户贵金属交易	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Paper precious metals transaction means an individual customer exchanges USD for precious metals (ounce) or RMB for precious metals (gram) that cannot be overdrawn by counter or e-banking of ICBC within the specified transaction time.	账户贵金属交易是指个人客户在规定的交易时间内，通过工商银行柜面或电子银行渠道进行的不可透支的美元兑贵金属（盎司）或人民币兑贵金属（克）的交易。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
There are six kinds of investment products, i.e. USD paper gold, RMB paper gold, USD paper silver, RMB paper silver, USD paper platinum and RMB paper platinum.	目前投资品种包括以下六类：美元账户黄金、人民币账户黄金、美元账户白银、人民币账户白银、美元账户铂金、人民币账户铂金。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Individuals who have certain knowledge on the movement of precious metal market and are willing to reap high return on investment by bearing certain risks. 	对贵金属市场走势具有一定认识、愿意并有能力在承担一定风险的基础上获取较高投资回报的个人客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Low transaction costs.	1.交易成本低。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Free of account opening fee, handling charge, and storage, transport and authentication fees of physical gold.	无开户费、交易手续费、实物黄金储藏、运输、鉴别费。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Long transaction time.	2.交易时间长。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
E-banking transaction is available from 7:00 a.m. every Monday to 4:00 a.m. every Saturday.	电子银行渠道每周一早7：00至周六早4：00连续提供交易服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Low transaction threshold.	3.交易起点低。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Take USD paper gold for example, the threshold of every transaction is merely 0.1 ounce, increasing at a tranche of 0.01 ounce.	以美元账户黄金为例，每笔交易起点仅为0.1盎司，以0.01盎司递增。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Wide transaction channels.	4.交易渠道广。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Such transaction channels as counter service, mobile banking (WAP), personal internet banking and telephone banking are available.	可支持柜面服务、手机银行（WAP）、个人网上银行、电话银行多渠道交易。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. Real time clearing of transaction funds.	5.交易资金实时清算。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Funds are cleared and transferred on a real time basis, and are allowed to be traded many times in one day.	资金实时清算，即时到账，当天可多次交易。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
6. Flexible transaction methods.	6.交易方式灵活多样。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
There are two transaction methods available for selection, i.e. real time transactions and entrusted transactions. 	有实时交易和委托交易两种交易方式可供选择。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
II. Spot Foreign Exchange Transactions	二、即期外汇买卖	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Spot foreign exchange transaction means that a customer conducts the spot exchange transaction of different currencies by the foreign exchange trading system (including operating outlets, telephone banking, internet banking, mobile banking and self-service terminals) of ICBC.	即期外汇买卖是指客户在规定的交易时间内，通过工商银行外汇买卖交易系统（包括营业网点、电话银行、网上银行、手机银行、自助终端等)，进行不同币种之间的即期外汇交易。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Individuals who have certain knowledge on the movement of foreign exchange market and are willing to reap return on investment by bearing certain risks and those who have demand for currency exchange and need to exchange one currency for another, as well as enterprises and institutions with demand for currency exchange.	对外汇市场走势具有一定认识、愿意并有能力在承担一定风险的基础上博取投资回报和有实际换汇需求、需要将现有的一种货币兑换为另一种货币的个人客户，以及具有换汇需求的企业和机构等。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Personal spot exchange trading	1.个人即期外汇买卖	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Long transaction time.	（1）交易时间长。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
E-banking transaction is available from 7:00 a.m. every Monday to 4:00 a.m. every Saturday.	电子银行渠道每周一早7：00至周六早4：00连续提供交易服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Flexible transaction methods.	（2）交易方式多样。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
There are real time transactions and entrusted transactions available for selection.	有即时交易和委托交易两种。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Of them, entrusted transactions are categorized into take-profit entrustment, stop-loss entrustment and two-way entrustment.	其中委托交易包括获利委托、止损委托和双向委托三种。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
The time limit of entrusted transaction offer is up to 120 hours.	委托交易挂单时限宽泛，最长可挂单120小时。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Low transaction threshold.	（3）交易起点金额低。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Generally, a customer may engage in personal foreign exchange trading in ICBC with merely USD100 or equivalent in other currencies.	通常只需100美元或等值其它货币，便可在工商银行进行个人外汇买卖交易。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(4) Wide transaction channels.	（4）交易渠道广。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Such transaction channels as counter service, mobile banking (WAP), personal internet banking and telephone banking are available.	可支持柜面服务、手机银行（WAP）、个人网上银行、电话银行多渠道交易。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(5) Real time clearing of transaction funds.	（5）交易资金实时清算。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Funds are cleared and transferred on a real time basis, and are allowed to be traded many times in one day.	资金实时清算，即时到账，当天可多次交易。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(6) Various transaction currencies.	（6）交易币种多样。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Tradable currencies generally include USD, Yen, HKD, GBP, Euro, Canadian Dollar, Swiss Francs, Australian Dollar, New Zealand Dollar, Singapore Dollar, South Korea Won and local currencies.	可交易币种一般包括美元、日元、港币、英镑、欧元、加拿大元、瑞士法郎、澳大利亚元、新西兰元、新加坡元、韩元等币种和当地货币。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Corporate spot exchange trading	2.对公即期外汇买卖	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(1) Simple, clear and understandable trading structure.	（1）交易结构简单清晰，易于理解。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(2) Flexible transaction methods.	（2）交易方式多样。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
There are real time transactions and entrusted transactions available for selection.	有即时交易和委托交易两种。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Of them, entrusted transactions are categorized into take-profit entrustment and stop-loss entrustment.	其中委托交易包括获利委托和止损委托两种。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
(3) Various transaction currencies.	（3）交易币种多样。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Tradable currencies generally include USD, Yen, HKD, GBP, Euro, Canadian Dollar, Swiss Francs, Australian Dollar, New Zealand Dollar, Singapore Dollar, South Korea Won and local currencies.	可交易币种一般包括美元、日元、港币、英镑、欧元、加拿大元、瑞士法郎、澳大利亚元、新西兰元、新加坡元、韩元等币种和当地货币。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
III. Forward Foreign Exchange Transactions	三、远期外汇买卖	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Forward foreign exchange transaction means that ICBC signs a forward foreign exchange trading contract with an eligible customer to clear funds on a certain date in future according to the stipulated foreign exchange currency, amount, exchange rate and term.	远期外汇买卖是指工商银行与具有一定资质的客户签订远期外汇买卖合约，约定在未来的某一日根据预先约定的外汇币种、金额、汇率和期限进行资金清算的产品。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customers aiming at hedging or investment.	以套期保值或投资为目的的对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Relatively simple structure that is easy to be understood by customers.	1.结构相对简单，易于客户理解。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Relative mature products allowing customers to hedge exchange rate risks based on their future foreign exchange income and expenditure and anticipation of exchange rate market.	2.产品较为成熟，客户可以根据未来的外汇收支状况和对汇率市场的预期规避汇率风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Free of such trading fees as options fee and handling fee so as to save trading costs for customers.	3.不存在期权费、手续费等交易费用，为客户节约了交易成本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Design products tailored to the individualized demands of customers.	4.可以根据客户个性化需求进行产品设计。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
IV. Foreign Exchange Swap Transactions	四、掉期外汇买卖	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Foreign exchange swap transaction means that both trading parties agree to swap a certain amount of currency A for currency B at a certain exchange rate (generally market exchange rate), and swap currency B for same amount of currency A on a future date at the specified price.	掉期外汇买卖是交易双方约定以一定数量货币A按照一定汇率（一般为市场汇率）交换货币B，并在约定的未来日期以约定价格用货币B反向交换同样数量的货币A。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customers with domestic and foreign currency fund management demand and hedging demand.	出于自身本外币资金管理需求和有套期保值需求的对公客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Simple, clear and understandable trading structure.	1.交易结构简单清晰、易于理解。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Customers may hedge exchange rate risks based on their current and future foreign exchange income and expenditure and anticipation of exchange rate market.	2.客户可根据当前及未来的外汇收支状况和对汇率市场的预期规避汇率风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Design products tailored to the individualized demands of customers.	3.可以根据客户个性化需求进行产品设计。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
V. Interest Rate Swap	五、利率掉期	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Interest rate swap means a financial contract whereby a customer and ICBC agree to calculate and swap interest within a specified period in future based on the contracted principal and interest rate.	利率掉期是指客户与工商银行约定在未来一定期限内，根据约定的本金和利率计算利息并进行利息交换的金融合约。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
It generally refers to the swap of fixed and floating interest rates.	通常表现为固定利率与浮动利率的交换。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Financial institutions and non-financial institutions which need to hedge interest rate risk, increase return on assets and flexibly manage assets and liabilities.	有规避利率风险、增加资产收益、灵活管理资产负债需求的金融机构和非金融机构。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Match the maturity of assets and liabilities and manage the basic variance risks incurred by fixed and floating interest rates.	1.匹配资产负债期限，管理固定利率与浮动利率的基差风险。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Hedge the market risks incurred by interest rate fluctuation or enjoy the income of interest rate fluctuation, reduce enterprise financing costs or increase return on investment.	2.规避利率波动的市场风险或享受利率波动的收益，降低企业融资成本或提高投资收益。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Turn to the method with lowest financing costs by interest rate swap based on the comparative advantages of enterprises or financial institutions in financing, so as to attain the objective of reducing financing costs.	3.结合企业或者金融机构融资时的比较优势，通过利率互换转换为融资成本最低的方式，达到降低融资成本的目的。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Take advantage of the arbitrage opportunities in the financial market and the combination of basic products and interest rate swap transactions to improve return on investment and wealth management.	4.利用金融市场存在的套利机会，通过基础产品和利率互换交易的组合，提高投资理财收益。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
5. ICBC may design customized products for customers to meet their needs and reduce or lock up financing costs. 6. Continuous dynamic management.	5.工商银行可以为客户进行个性化的产品设计，满足客户需求，降低或锁定融资成本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC may regularly provide assessment reports on interest rate swap and render subsequent dynamic management services according to market situation and customer demand.	6.持续的动态管理,工商银行可以定期提供利率掉期交易的评估报告，结合市场行情和客户需求提供后续的动态管理服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
VI. Bond Transactions and Settlement Agency	六、债券交易及结算代理	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Bond transactions and settlement agency business means that ICBC's institutions within the territory of China, as bond settlement agents, handle bond transactions and settlement for customers at their request.	债券交易及结算代理业务是指工商银行在中国境内的机构作为债券结算代理人，受客户的委托为其办理债券交易和结算等业务的行为。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Agency business mainly includes handling the formalities for opening or cancellation of bond custody accounts and internetworking of bond transactions for customers, dealing with bond transactions and settlement for customers in their name, and providing customers such services as market analysis, consultation and investment suggestions.	代理业务主要包括：为客户办理债券托管账户开户、销户等手续，代客户办理债券交易联网手续，以客户的名义为客户办理债券交易及结算业务，为客户提供市场分析、咨询、投资建议等服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Corporate customers such as local central banks or monetary authorities, RMB clearing banks in Hong Kong and Macao, and participating banks of RMB settlement for cross-border trade, particularly the latter. 	适用于当地中央银行或货币当局、香港及澳门地区人民币业务清算行、跨境贸易人民币结算参加行等对公客户，重点以跨境贸易人民币结算参加行为主。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. High-quality trading services.	1.优质的交易服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has strong fund strength, intensive fund operation system and experienced investment team to provide high-quality bond trading services for customers.	工商银行庞大的资金实力、集约化的资金营运体系和拥有丰富交易经验的投资团队，可为客户提供优质的债券交易服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Efficient business handling.	2.高效的业务处理。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC has a professional bond transaction and settlement agency team and an advanced business management system to provide efficient and rapid bond transaction and settlement agency services for customers.	工商银行专业的债券交易及结算代理团队和先进的业务管理系统为客户提供高效快捷的债券交易及结算代理服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Sound business messages.	3.完善的业务资讯。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC’s excellent study team can provide customers with all-round market information, differentiated investment suggestions and dynamic combined management strategies in a timely manner.	工商银行卓越的研究团队及时向客户提供全面的市场信息、差异化的投资建议和动态的组合管理策略。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
4. Rich agency experience.	4.丰富的代理经验。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ICBC is the first commercial bank engaging in such business within the territory of China, and it is familiar with business requirements and has complete business regulations and relevant documents. 	工商银行是中国境内首家开办此业务的商业银行，熟悉业务办理要求，具备完善的业务制度和相关文本。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

Cross-border RMB purchase and sale business means that ICBC’s institutions within the territory of China, at the request of overseas participating banks for RMB settlement for cross-border trade, provide RMB purchase and sale services under trade settlement within the limit stipulated by the People’s Bank of China.	跨境人民币购售业务是指工商银行中国境内机构应跨境贸易人民币结算中国境外参加银行要求，在中国人民银行规定的限额内，为中国境外参加银行提供贸易结算项下的人民币购售服务。	sample1-en-sample1-zh

X. E-banking Password Card	十、电子银行口令卡	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
E-banking password card is an e-banking security tool provided by ICBC to meet customers’ requirements on electronic channel transactions in consideration of the factors of security and costs. The product is a matrix-shaped card with certain character strings each corresponding to the sole coordinate.	电子银行口令卡是工商银行为满足客户的电子渠道交易安全要求，综合安全性与成本因素推出的一种电子银行安全工具，该产品是一张以矩阵形式印有若干字符串的卡片，每个字符串对应一个唯一的坐标。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
When a customer inputs security password when using relevant e-banking functions of ICBC, the system will display some designated coordinates, and the customer needs to input the corresponding character string on the card as password, and then the system may accept the transaction after verifying that the password characters are correct.	客户在使用工商银行电子银行相关功能时需要输入安全密码时，系统显示若干指定坐标，客户将卡片上对应的字符串作为密码输入，系统校验密码字符正确则可受理该笔交易。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal and corporate e-banking customers of ICBC.	工商银行个人电子银行客户和企业电子银行客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Secure transaction process.	1.确保交易过程安全。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
E-banking password card may effectively prevent lawbreakers from stealing user password by false website, Trojan virus and hacker attack, so as to safeguard transaction security.	电子银行口令卡可以有效地防止不法分子通过虚假网站、木马病毒、黑客攻击等手段窃取用户密码，保障交易安全。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. Secure and reliable encryption.	2.加密方式安全可靠。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
System may designate certain coordinates randomly every time, and the password used each time is sole, random and unforeseeable.	系统每次均以随机方式指定若干坐标，每次使用的密码都具有唯一性、动态变化性和不可预知性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
3. Simple, cost-effective and portable.	3.操作简单、成本低廉、便于携带。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
XI. USB Shield	十一、U盾	sample1-en-sample1-zh
i. Introduction	（一）简介	sample1-en-sample1-zh
USB shield is a high-level security tool provided by ICBC to its internet banking customers, which is used in digital signature and certification of personal and corporate internet banking.	U盾是工商银行为网上银行客户提供的高级别安全工具，用于个人网上银行及企业网上银行的电子签名和数字认证。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
USB shield is embedded in a smart card microprocessor, which may be used in encryption, decryption and digital signature of internet data by 1024-digit asymmeTric PIN key algorithm, in order to guarantee the confidentiality, truthfulness, completeness and incontestability of internet transactions.	U盾内置微型智能卡处理器，采用1024位非对称密钥算法对网上数据进行加密、解密和数字签名，确保网上交易的保密性、真实性、完整性和不可否认性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
ii. Target customers	（二）目标客户	sample1-en-sample1-zh
Personal and corporate internet banking customers of ICBC. 	工商银行个人网上银行客户及企业网上银行客户。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
iii. Characteristics and advantages	（三）特点和优势	sample1-en-sample1-zh
1. Higher trading security level.	1.交易安全级别更高。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
USB shield, as the top-level internet banking security certification tool, stores unreadable digital certificates in the form of mobile digital certificates, in order to guarantee the confidentiality and uniqueness of customer information.	U盾是最高级别的网上银行安全认证方式，通过移动数字证书的形式存放不可读取的数字证书，确保了客户信息的保密性、唯一性。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
2. More applicable functions and higher trading privilege.	2.适用功能更全面、交易权限更高。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
With a USB shield, any customer may be entitled to all the internet banking services of ICBC with a higher privilege and exempt from the restriction of security certification mode.	使用U盾，可以使用工商银行全部的网上银行业务，交易权限更高，不会受到安全认证方式的限制。	sample1-en-sample1-zh
